Nammaazhvaar aruliya Thiruvaaymozhi

Thiruvaaymozhith thaniyanngal


Naadha munigal arulich seydhadhu:
Bakthaamrutham visvajanaanumodhanam
Sarvaarththadham srisadagopa vaangmayam
Sahasrasaakopanishadh Samaagamam
Namaamyaham dhraavida vedha Saagaram.

Eesvara munigal arulich seydhadhu:
Thiruvazhudhi naadenrum thennkurukoo renrum,
Maruviniya vanporunnal enrum, - arumaraigal
Andhaadhi seythaan adiyinaiye eppozhuthum,
Sindhiyaay nenche! Thelinthu.

Chottai nambigal arulichseydhadhu:
Manaththaalum vaayaalum vankurukoor penum
Inaththaarai yallaa thirainchen, - dhanaththaalum
Ethung kuraivilen enthai sadagopan,
Paadhangal yaamudaiya parru.

Ananthaazhvaan arulichseydhddhu:
Eynthaperung keerththi iraamaanusamunithan
Vaaynthamalarp paadham vanankukinren, - aaynthaperunch
Cheeraar sadagopan senthamizh vedhantharikkum,
Peraadha vullam pera.

Battar arulichseydhavai:
Vaannthikazhum solai madhilarangar vanpugazhmel
Aanra thamizhmaraigal aayiramum, - eenra
Mudhalthaay sadagopan, moympaal valarththa
Idhaththaay iraamunusan.

Mikka irainnilaiyum meyyaam uyirnnilaiyum,
Thakka neriyum thadaiyaakith - thokkiyalum,
Oozhvinaiyum vaazhvinaiyum Odhum kurukaiyargon,
Yaazhinisai vedhath thiyal.

Thiruvaay mozhi mudhar paththu.

Uyarvara uyarnnalam udaiyavan evan? Avan
Mayarvara madhinnalam arulinan evan? Avan
Ayarvarum amarargal athipathi evan? Avan
Thuyararu sudaradi thozhuthezhen manane! (2) 1.1.1

Mananakammalamara malarmisai yezhutharum
Mananunar valavilan, poriyunar vavaiyilan
Inanunar, muzhunnalam, ethirnnikazh kazhivinum
Inanilan, enanu yir, mikunnarai yilane. 1.1.2

Ilanathu vudaiyani thenanninai variyavan
Nilanidai visumbidai uruvinan aruvinan
Pulanodu pulanalan, ozhivilan, parantha ann
Nalanudai yoruvanai nanukinam naame. 1.1.3

Naamavan ivanuvan, avalival uvaleval
Thaamavar ivaruvar, adhuvidhu vudhuvedhu
Veemavai yivaiyuvai, avainnalam, theenkavai
Aamavai, aayavai, aaynninra avare. 1.1.4

Avaravar thamathama tharivari vakaivakai
Avaravar iraiyavare Nnaa di yadaivargal
Avaravar iraiyavar kuraivilar; iraiyavar
Avaravar vidhivazhi yadaiyannin ranare. 1.1.5

Ninranar irunthanar kidanthanar thirinthanar
Ninrilar irunthilar kidanthilar thirinthilar
Enrumor iyalvinar enanninai variyavar
Enrumor iyalvodu ninrae m thidare. 1.1.6

Thidavisum perivali neernnila mivaimisai
Padarporul muzhuvathu maayavai yavaithorum
Udalmisai yuyirenak karanthenkum paranthulan
Sudarmiku suruthiyul ivaiyanda surane. 1.1.7

Surara Ri varunnilai vinmudhal muzhuvathum
Varanmutha laayavai muzhuthunda paraparan
Puramoru moonrerith thamararkku mariviyanthu
Aranayan enau la kazhiththamaith thulane. 1.1.8

Ulanenil ulana van uruvami v vuruvugal
Ulanalan enil, avan aruvamiv varuvugal
Ulanena ilanena ivaiguna mudaimaiyil
Ulani ru thakaimaiyo dozhivilan paranthe. 1.1.9

Paranthathan paravaiyulneerdhorum parandhulan
Paranthaa N damithena: nilavisum pozhivara
Karanthasi lidanthorum idanthikazh porudorum
Karanthenkum paranthulan: ivaiyunda karane. 1.1.10

Karavisum perivali neernnila mivaimisai
Varanna vil thiralvali yaliporai yaaynninra
Parana di melkuru koorchchada gopansol
Niral-nirai yaayirath thivaipaththum veede. (2) 1.1.11

Veedumin murravum--veeduseythu ummuyir
Veedudai yaannidai--veeduseymmine. (2) 1.2.1

Minnin nilaiyila--mannuyi raakkaigal
Ennu midaththu irai--unnumin neere. 1.2.2

Neernnuma thenrivai--vermuthal maayththu irai
Sermin uyirkku atha--nnernnirai yille. 1.2.3

Illathu mullathum--alla thavanuru
Ellaiyi lannnnalam--pulkupar rarre. 1.2.4

Arrathu parrenil--urrathu veeduuyir
Serrathu mannuril--arrirai parre. 1.2.5

Parrila Nneesanum--murravum ninranan
Parrilai yaay avan--murri ladanke. 1.2.6

Adankezhil sampaththu--adankakkandu eesan
Adankezhi laqthenru--adankuka vulle. 1.2.7

Ulla muraiseyal--ullavim moonraiyum
Ullik keduththu irai--yullilo dunke. 1.2.8

Odunka avannkan--odunkalu mellaam
Vidum;pinnu maakkai--vidumpozhu thenne. 1.2.9

Enperuk kannnnalaththu--onporu leerila
Vanpugazh naaranan--thinkazhal sere. (2) 1.2.10

Serththadath thennkuru--koorchchda gopansol
Seerththodai yaayiraththu--Orththaip paththe. (2) 1.2.11

Paththudai yadiyavark keliyavan; pirargaluk kariya
Viththakan malarmagal virumpumnnam arumpera ladigal
Maththuru kadaivenney kalavinilu ravidai yaappundu
Eththiram, uralino dinaindhirunn thenkiya elive! (2) 1.3.1

Elivaru miyalvinan nilaivaram pilapala pirappaay
Olivaru muzhunnalam muthalila kedila; veedaam
Thelitharum nilaimaiya thozhivilan muzhuvathum; iraiyon
Alivaru marulino dakaththanan; puraththana Nn mainthe. 1.3.2

Amaivudai yaranneri muzhuvathu muyarvara vuyarntha
Amaivudai muthalkedal odividai yarannila mathuvaam
Amaivudai yamararum yaavaiyum yaavarum thaanaam
Amaivudai naaranan maayaiyai yaripavar yaare? 1.3.3

Yaarumor nilaimaiyan enavari variya vemperumaan
Yaarumor nilaimaiyan enavari veliyavem perumaan
Perumo raayiram pirapala udaiyavem perumaan
Perumo ruruvamu mulathillai yilathillai pinakke. 1.3.4

Pinakkara aruvakaich chamayamumneriyulli yuraiththa
Kanakkaru nalaththanan; anthami laadhiyam bagavan
Vanakkudaith thavanneri vazhinninru puranneri kalaikattu
Unakkumin, pasaiyara! Avanudai yunarvukon dunarndhe. 1.3.5

Unarnthunarnn thizhinthakan Ruyarnthuru viyanthavinnnnilaimai
Unarnthunarnn thunarilum irainnilaiyunarvari thuyirgaal!
Unarnthunarnn thuraiththuraith thariyaya Nnaranennumivarai
Unarnthunarnn thuraiththuraith thirainchumin manappattathonre. 1.3.6

Onrenap palavena arivarum vadivinul ninra
Nanrezhil naaranan naanmukan aranennu mivarai
Onrannum manaththuvaith thullinnum irupasai yaruththu
Nanrena nalancheyva thavanidai nammudai naale. 1.3.7

Naalunin radunnama pazhamaiyang koduvinaiyudane
Maalum Or kuraivillai; mananaka malamarak kazhuvi
Naalunnann thiruvudai yadigaltham nalankazhal vananki
Maalumo ridaththilum vanakkodu maalvathu valame. 1.3.8

Valaththanan thiripura meriththavan, idamperath thunthith
Thalaththu ezhu thisaimukan padaiththannal lulagamum thaanum
Pulappada pinnumthan ulagaththi lakaththanan thaane
Solappukil ivaipinnum vayirrula; ivaiyavan thuyakke. 1.3.9

Thuyakkaru mathiyilnnal nyaanaththul amararaith thuyakkum
Mayakkudai maayaigal vaanilum periyana vallan
Puyarkaru niraththanan; perunnilang kadanthannal ladippodhu
Ayarppilan alarruvan thazhuvuvan vanankuvan amarnthe. 1.3.10

Amarargal thozhuthezha alaikadal kadaindhavan dhannai
Amarpozhil valankuru koorchchadagopan kur revalgal
Amarsuvai yaayirath thavarrinu Livaipaththum vallaar
Amararo duyarvirchen raruvardham piraviyany chiraiye. (2) 1.3.11

Anchiraiya madannaaraay! Aliyaththaay! Neeyumnnin
Anchiraiya sevalumaay aavaaven renakkaruli
Venchiraippul uyarththaarken vidudhoodhaaych chenrakkaal
Vannchiraiyil avanvaikkil vaippundaal enncheyyumo? (2) 1.4.1

Enncheyya thaamaraikkan perumaanaark kenndhoodhaay
Enncheyyum uraiththakkaal? Inakkuyilkaal! Neeralire?
Munncheytha muzhuvinaiyaal thiruvadikkeezhk kurreval
Munncheyya muyalaathen akalvathuvo? Vidhiyiname. 1.4.2

Vidhiyinaal pedaimanakkum mennadaiya annankaal!
Madhiyinaal kuralmaanaay ulakirandha kalvarku
'Madhiyilen valvinaiye maalaatho? Enru oruththi
Madhiyellaam ulkalanki mayankumaal' enneere! 1.4.3

Ennneermai kandiranki yithuthakaa thennaatha
Ennneela mukilvannarkensoliyaan sollukeno?
Nnanneermai yiniyavar kan thankaathen Roruvaaychchol
Nnanneela makanrilkaal! Nalkuthiro? Nalkeero? 1.4.4

Nnalkiththaan kaaththalikkum pozhilezhum; vinaiyerke
Nnalkaththaa Nnaakaatho? Naarananaik kandakkaal
Malkunneerp punarpadappai iraithervan sirukuruke!
Malkunneerk kannerkor vaasakankon darulaaye. 1.4.5

'Arulaatha neeraruli yavaraavi thuvaraamun
Arulaazhip putkadaveer avarveethi yorunnaal' enru
Arulaazhi yammaanaik kandakkaal ithusolli
Yarul aazhi varivande! Yaamumen pizhaiththome? 1.4.6

Enbizhaikop pathupolap panivaadai yeerginrathu
Enbizhaiye ninaindharuli yarulaatha thirumaalaarkku
'Enbizhaiththaal thiruvadiyin thakavinuk'ken Roruvaaychchol
Enbizhaikkum? Ilankiliye! Yaanvalarththa neeyalaiye? 1.4.7

Nneeyalaiye? Chirupoovaay! Nedumaalaark kennthoothaay
Nnoyenathu nuvalenna, nuvalaathe yirundhozhindhaay
Saayalodu manimaamai thalarndhen naani Nniyunathu
Vaayalakil innadisil vaippaarai naadaaye. 1.4.8

Naadaatha malarnaadi naaldhorum naaranandhan
Vaadaatha malaradikkeezh vaikkave vakukkinru
Veedaadi veerriruththal vinaiyarra thenseyvatho?
Oodaadu panivaadaay! Uraiththeeraay enathudale. 1.4.9

Udalaadip pirappuvee duuyirmuthalaa murrumaay
Kadalaazhi neerdhorri yathanulle kanvalarum
Adalaazhi yammaanaik kandakkaal ithusolli
Vidalaazhi madannenche! Vinaiyomon raamalave. 1.4.10

Alaviyanra Ezhulagath thavarperumaan kannanai
Valavayalchoozh vankurukoorchchadagopan vaayndhuraiththa
Alaviyanra andhaathi yaayiraththul ippaththin
Valavuraiyaal peralaakum vaanonku peruvalame. (2) 1.4.11

Valave zhulakin muthalaaya
Vaano riraiyai aruvinaiyen
'Kalavezh venney thoduvunda
Kalvaa!' enpan; pinnaiyum
'Thalavezh muruval pinnaikkaay
Vallaa Nnaayar thalaivannaay
Ilave rezhum thazhuviya
Endhaay!' enpan ninaindhunnaindhe. (2) 1.5.1

Nninaindhu naindhul karaindhuruki,
Imaiyor palarum munivarum
Punaindha kanni neersaandham
Pukaiyo dendhi vanankinaal
Nninaindha ellaap porulkatkum
Viththaay, muthalil sithaiyaame
Mananchey nyaanath thunperumai
Maasoo naatho? Maayone! 1.5.2

Maayo nnigalaay nadaikarra
Vaanor palarum munivarum
'Nneeyo nnigalaip padai' enru
Nirainnaan mukanaip padaiththavan
Seyo Nnellaa arivukkum;
Thisaika Lellaam thiruvadiyaal
Thaayon ellaa evvuyirkkum
Thaayon thaano ruruvane. 1.5.3

Thaano ruruve thaniviththaayth
Thannil moovar muthalaaya
Vaanor palarum munivarum
Marrum marrum murrumaay
Thaanor perunneer thannulle
Thorri athanul kanvalarum
Vaanor perumaan maamaayann
Vaikunn thane m perumaane. 1.5.4

Maaney nokki madavaalai
Maarvil kondaay! Maadhavaa!
Koone sithaiya vundaivil
Niraththil theriththaay! Govinndhaa!
Vaanaar sothi manivannaa!
Madhusoo dhaa!Nnee yarulaayu Nn
Thene malarum thiruppaadham
Seru maaru vinaiyene. 1.5.5

Vinaiyen vinaitheer marundhaanaay!
Vinnor thalaivaa! Kesavaa!
Manaise raayar kulamuthale!
Maa maayane! Maadhavaa!
Sinaiyey thazhaiya maraamarangal
Ezhum eythaay! Sireedharaa!
Inaiyaay! Inaiya peyarinaay!
Enru naivan adiyene. 1.5.6

Adiyen siriya nyaanaththan;
Aritha laarkku mariyaanai
Kadiser thannann thuzhaaykkanni
Punaindhaan dhannaik kannanai
Sediyaar aakkai yadiyaaraich
Cherdhal theerkkum thirumaalai
Adiyen kaanpaan alarruvan;
Ithanil mikkor ayarvunde? 1.5.7

Undaa yulakezh munname;
Umizhndhu maayai yaalpukku
Undaay venney sirumanisar
Uvalai yaakkai nilaiyeythi
Manthaan sorndha thundelum
Manisark kaakum peersirithum
Andaa vannam mankaraiya
Neyyoon marundho? Maayone! 1.5.8

Maayom theeya alavalaip
Perumaa vanchap peyveeya
Thooya kuzhavi yaayvidappaal
Amudhaa amudhu seythitta
Maayan vaanor thaniththalaivan
Malaraal maindha Nnevvuyirkkum
Thaayon thammaan ennammaan
Ammaa moorththi yaichchaarndhe. 1.5.9

Saarndha iruval vinaigalum
Sariththu maayap parraruththu
Theerndhu thanpaal manamvaikkath
Thiruththi, veedu thiruththuvaan
Aarndha nyaanach chudaraaki
Akalam keezhmel alavirandhu
Nnerndha vuruvaay aruvaakum
Ivarri Nnuyiraam nedumaale! 1.5.10

'Maale! Maayap perumaane!
Maa maayavane!' enrenru
Maale yeri maalarulaal
Mannu kurukoorch chadagopan
Paaley thamizha risaikaarar
Paththar paravum aayiraththin
Paale patta ivaipaththum
Vallaark killai parivathe. 1.5.11

Parivathi leesanaip paadi
Virivathu meva luruveer!
Pirivakai yinrinnann neerdhooy
Purivathu vumpukai poove. (2) 1.6.1

Madhuvaar thannann thuzhaayaan
Muthuve dhamuthal vanukku
Ethuve thenpani ennaa
Thathuve yaatcheyyu meede. 1.6.2

Eedu meduppumil eesan
Maadu vidaathen manane
Paadumenn naaa van paadal
Aadumenn anga mananke. 1.6.3

Anankena aadume Nnangam
Vananki vazhipadu meesann
Pinanki yamarar pitharrum
Gunankezhu kolkaiyi nnaanne. 1.6.4

Kolkaiko Laamaiyi laathaann
Elkal iraaga milaathaann
Vilkaivil Laamaivi rumpi
Ulkalann thaarkko ramudhe. 1.6.5

Amudham amarakat keendha
Nimirsuda raazhi nedumaal
Amudhilu maarra iniyan
Nnimirthirai neelkada laane. 1.6.6

Nneelkadal soozhilang gaikkon
Tholgal thalaithuni seythaan
Thaalgal thalaiyil vanangi
Naalka dalaikka zhimine. 1.6.7

Kazhiminnthon deergal kazhiththuth
Thozhuminn avanaith thozhuthaal
Vazhinninra valvinai maalviththu
Azhivinri yaakkam tharume. 1.6.8

Dharuma arumpaya Nnaaya
Thirumaka Laarthanik kelvann
Perumai yudaiya piraanaar
Irumai vinaikadi vaare. 1.6.9

Kadivaar theeya vinaigal
Nnodiyaa ruma La vaikkan
Kodiyaa adupul Luyarththa
Vadivaar maadhava nnaare. 1.6.10

Maadhavan paalchada gopan
Theethava minri yuraiththa
Ethami laayirath thippaththu
Odhaval laarpira vaare. 1.6.11

Piraviththuyarara nyaanaththulninru,
Thuravichchudarvilakkam thalaippeyvaar,
Aravanaiyaazip padaiyandhananai,
Maraviyaiyinri manaththuvaippaare. 1.7.1

Vaippaammarundhaa madiyarai, valvinaith
Thuppaampulanaindhum thunchakkodaanavan,
Eppaalyavarkkum nalaththaaluyarndhuyarndhu,
Appaalavanengka laayarkozundhe. 1.7.2

Aayar kozundhaa yavaraalpudaiyunnum,
Maayappiraanaiyen maanikkachchothiyai,
Thooyavamuthaip parukipparuki, en
Maayappiravi mayarvaruththene. 1.7.3

Mayarvaravenmanaththe manninaandhannai,
Uyarvinaiyetharu monchudarkkarraiyai,
Ayarvilamararga Laathikkozundhai, en
Isaivinaiyensolli yaanviduvene. 1.7.4

Viduvenoven vilakkaiennaaviyai,
Naduvevandhuyyak kolkinranaathanai,
Thoduvecheythila vaaychchiyarkanninul,
Vidavecheythu vizikkumpiraanaiye. 1.7.5

Piraanperunilang keendavan, pinnum
Viraaymalarththuzaay veyndhamudiyan,
Maraamarameydha maayavan, ennu
Liraanenilpinnai yaanottuveno. 1.7.6

Yaanottiyennu liruththuvamenrilan,
Thaanottivandhen dhaninencaivanciththu,
Oonottininren uyirilkalandhu, iyal
Vaanottumoini yennainegizkkave. 1.7.7

Ennainegizkkilu mennudaiynannencan
Thannai, agalvikkath thaanumgillaanini,
Pinnainedumpanaith tholmagizpeedudai,
Munnaiyamarar muzumuthalaane. 1.7.8

Amararmuzumudha laagiyavaadhiyai,
Amararkkamutheendha vaayarkozundhai,
Amaravazumpath thuzaaviyennaavi,
Amararththazuvir riniyakalumo. 1.7.9

Akalilakalu manukilanukum,
Pukalumariyan poruvallanemmaan,
Nikarilavanpugaz paadiyilaippilam,
Pakalumiravum padindhukudaindhe. 1.7.10

Kudaindhuvandunnum thuzaaymudiyaanai,
Adaindhathen kurukurchchadakopan,
Midaindhachol thodaiyaayiraththippaththu,
Udaindhunoygalai yoduvikkume. 1.7.11

Odumpulleri, sudumthanduzaay,
Needuninravai, aadumammaane. 1.8.1

Ammaanaayppinnum, emmaanpumaanaan,
Vemmaavaaykeenda, semmaakannane. 1.8.2

Kannaavaanenrum, mannorvinnorkku,
Thannaarvengkada, vinnorverpane. 1.8.3

Verpaiyonreduththu, orkaminriye,
Nirkumammaanseer, karpanvaikale. 1.8.4

Vaikalumvenney, kaikalandhundaan,
Poykalavaathu, en - meykalandhaane. 1.8.5

Kalandhennaavi, nalangkolnaathan,
Pulankolmaanaay, nilamkondaane. 1.8.6

Kondaanezvidai, undaanezvaiyam,
Thandhaamancheydhu, en - endhaanaanaane. 1.8.7

Aanaanaanaayan, meenodenamum;
Thaanaanaanennil, thaanaayasange. 1.8.8

Sangkusakkaram, angkaiyilkondaan,
Engkumthaanaaya, nangalnaathane. 1.8.9

Naadhannyaalangkol - paadhan, ennammaan,
Odhampolkilar, vedhaneerane. 1.8.10

Neerpuraivannan, seerchadagopan,
Nerdhalaayiraththu, ordhalivaiye. 1.8.11

Ivaiyumavaiyumuvaiyu mivarumavarumuvarum,
Yavaiyumyavarumthannulle yaakiyumaakkiyumkaakkum,
Avaiyul thanimuthalemmaan kannapiraanennamutham,
Suvaiyanthiruvinmanaala nnennudaichchuzalulaane. 1.9.1

Choozalpalapalavallaan thollaiyangkaalaththulagai
Kezalonraakiyidandha kesavanennudaiyammaan,
Vezamaruppaiyosiththaan vinnavarkkennalariyaan
Aazanedungkadalcherndhaa nnavanennarukalilaane. 1.9.2

Arukalilaayaperunchee ramarargalaathimuthalvan,
Karukiyaneelananmeni vannanchendhaamaraikkannan,
Porusiraippulluvandherum poomagalaarthanikkelvan,
Orukathiyinsuvaithandhit tozivilanennodudane. 1.9.3

Udanamarkaathalmagalir thirumagalmanmagalaayar
Madamagal, enrivarmoova raalumulagamummoonre,
Udanavaiyokkavizungki yaalilaichcherndhavanemmaan,
Kadalmalimaayapperumaan kannanennokkalaiyaane. 1.9.4

Okkalaivaiththumulaippaa lunnenruthandhidavaangki,
Chekkanchekavanravalpaa luyirchekavundaperumaan,
Nakkapiraanodayanu mindhiranummuthalaaka,
Okkavumthorriyaveesan maayanennenchinulaane. 1.9.5

Maayanennenchinullan marrumyavarkkumathuve,
Kaayamumseevanumthaane kaalumeriyumavane,
Cheyananiyanyavarkkum chindhaikkumkocharamallan,
Thuyan thuyakkanmayakka nnennudaiththolinaiyaane. 1.9.6

Tholinaimelum nanmaarbinmelum sudarmudimelum,
Thaalinaimelumpunaindha thannandhuzaayudaiyammaan
Kelinaiyonrumilaathaan kilarumsudarolimoorththi,
Naalanaindhonrumakalaa Nnennudainaavinulaane. 1.9.7

Naavinulninrumalarum nyaanakkalaigalukkellaam,
Aaviyumaakkaiyumthaane azippodalippavanthaane,
Pooviyalnaalthadandholan porupadaiyaazisangkendhum,
Kaavinanmenikkamalak kannanenkanninulaane. 1.9.8

Kamalakkannanen kanninullaankaanpanavankangalaale,
Amalangalaakavizikkum aimpulanumavanmoorththi,
Kamalaththayannampithannaik kannuthalaanodumthorri
Amalaththeyvaththodulaga maakkiyennerriyulaane. 1.9.9

Nerriyulninrennaiyaalum niraimalarppaathangalsoodi,
Karraiththuzaaymudikkolak kannapiraanaiththozuvaar,
Orraippiraiyanindhaanum naanmukanumindhiranum,
Marraiyamararumellaam vandhenadhuchchiyulaane. 1.9.10

Uchchiyullenirkumtheva thevarkukkannapiraarku,
Ichchaiyulchellavunarththi vankurukoorchchadakopan,
Ichchonnavaayiraththu livaiyumorpaththempiraarku,
Nichchalumvinnappamcheyya neelkazalchenniporume. 1.9.11

Porumaaneelpadai yaazisangkaththodu,
Thirumaaneelkaza lezulakumthoza,
Orumaanikkura Laakinimirndha, ak
Karumaanikkamen kannulathaakume. 1.10.1

Kannulle nirkum kaathanmaiyaalthozil,
Ennilumvaru menninivenduvam,
Mannumneeru meriyumnalvaayuvum,
Vinnumaayviriyu mempiraanaiye. 1.10.2

Empiraanaiyendhai thandhaithandhaikkum
Thampiraanai, thandhaamaraikkannanai,
Komparaavu nunneridaimaarvanai,
Empiraanaith thozaaymadanenchame. 1.10.3

Nenchamenallai nallaiunnaipperraal
Encheyyom, iniyennakuraivinam,
Maindhanai malaraalmanavaalanai,
Thunchumpothum vidaathuthodarkandaay. 1.10.4

Kandaayenenche karumangalvaaykkinru, Or
Endaanuminriye vandhiyalumaaru,
Undaanaiyulakezu mormoovadi
Kondaanai, kandu kondanaineeyume. 1.10.5

Neeyumnaanumin nernirkil, melmarror,
Noyumsaarkodaan nenchamesonnen,
Thaayumthandhaiyumaa yivvulakinil,
Vaayumeesan manivannanendhaiye. 1.10.6

Endhaiyeyenru memperumaanenrum,
Chindhaiyulvaippan cholluvanpaaviyen,
Endhaiyemperumaanenru vaanavar,
Chindhaiyul vaiththuch chollumchelvanaiye. 1.10.7

Chelvanaarana nnenracholkettalum,
Malkumkanpani naaduvanmaayame,
Allumnanpakalu midaiveedinri,
Nalkiyennai vidaannampi nampiye. 1.10.8

Nampiyaiththen kurungkudininra, ach
Chemponethika zumthirumoorththiyai,
Umparvaanava raathiyanchothiyai,
Empiraanaiyen chollimarappano. 1.10.9

Marappumnyaanamum naanon runarndhilan,
Marakkumenruchen thaamaraikkannodu,
Marapparavennulle manninaandhannai,
Marappanovini yaanenmaniyaiye. 1.10.10

Maniyaivaanavar kannanaiththannatho
Raniyai, thenkuru koorchchadakopan, chol
Panicheyaayirath thullivaipaththudan,
Thanivilar karpa relkalvivaayume. 1.10.11

Irandaam Paththu


Vaayundhiraiyugalum Kaanalmada_Naaraay,
Aayumamarulakumthunchilum Nithunchaayaal,

Ingkillaiyaalen Riraniyan Thoonpudaippa,
Angkappozuthe Yavanviyaththonriya, En
Singkappiraanperumai Yaaraayumsirmaiththe. 2.8.9

Sirmaikolvidu SuvarkkaNarakiraa,
IrmaikolthevarNaduvaa Marrepporutkum,
Vermuthalaayviththaayp ParandhuthaniNinra,
Kaarmukilpolvannanen KannanaiNaanKandene. 2.8.10

Kandalangalseyya Karumeniyammaanai,
Vandalampumsolai VazuthivalaNaadan,
Pandalaiyilsonnathami Zaayiraththippaththumvallaar,
Vindalaiyilvirrirun Thaalvaremmaavide. 2.8.11

Emmaavitduth Thiramumseppam, Nin
Semmaapaathaparputh Thalaiserththollai,
Kaimmaathunpam Kadindhapiraane,
Ammaavadiyen Venduvathithe. 2.9.1

Itheyaanunnaik Kolvathenynyaanrum, En
Maithoysothi Manivannavendhaay,
EythaaNinKazal Yaaneytha, Nyaanak
Kaithaa Kaalakkazivuseyyele. 2.9.2

Seyyelthivinaiyen Rarulseyyum, En
Kaiyaarchchakkarak Kannapiraane,
Aiyaarkandamadaikkilum NinKazal
Eyyaatheththa, Arulseyyenakke. 2.9.3

Enakkeyaatsey Yekkaalaththumenru, En
Manakkevan Thidaividinrimanni,
Thanakkeyaaka Venaikkollumithe,
Enakkekannanai YaanKolsirappe. 2.9.4

Sirappilvidu SuvarkkamNarakam,
Irappileythukaveytharka, Yaanum
Pirappil Palpiravipperumaanai,
Marapponrinri Yenrummagizvene. 2.9.5

Magizkoltheyva Mulokamalokam,
Magizkolsothi Malarndhavammaane,
Magizkolsindhai Solseykaikondu, Enrum
Magizvurrunnai Vanangkavaaraaye. 2.9.6

Vaaraayun Thiruppaathamalarkkiz,
Peraatheyaan Vandhadaiyumpadi
Thaaraathaay, Unnaiyennulvaippilenrum
Aaraathaay, Enakkenrumekkaale. 2.9.7

Ekkaalaththendhaiyaa Yennulmannil, Mar
Rekkaalaththilum Yaathonrumvenden,
Mikkaarvetha Vimalarvizungkum, En
Akkaarakkaniye Unnaiyaane. 2.9.8

Yaaneyennai Yariyagilaathe,
YaaneyenDhanathe Yenrirundhen,
YaaneNiyen NnudaimaiyumNiye,
Vaaneyeththu Memvaanavarere. 2.9.9

Erelezumven Rerkolilangkaiyai,
Nireseytha Nedunchudarchchothi,
Therelennaiyun Ponnadichcherththollai,
Verepoka Enynyaanrumvidale. 2.9.10

Vidalilsakkarath Thannalai, Meval
Vidalilvankurukoorch SadakopanSol,
Kedalilaayiraththul Livaipaththum,
Kedalilviduseyyum Kilarvaarkke. 2.9.11

Kilaroliyilamai Keduvathanmunnam,
Valarolimaayon Maruviyakoyil,
Valarilampozilsooz Maaliruncolai,
Thalarvilaraagil Saarvathusathire. 2.10.1

Sathirilamadavaar Thaazchsiyai Mathiyaathu,
Athirkuralsangkath ThazakarThamkoyil,
Mathithavazkudumi Maaliruncolai,
Pathiyathuveththi Yezuvathupayane. 2.10.2

Payanallaseythu PayanillaiNenche,
Puyalmazaivannar Purindhuraikoyil,
Mayalmikupozilsooz Maaliruncholai,
Ayanmalaiyadaivathathukarumame. 2.10.3

Karumavanpaasam Kaziththuzanruyyave,
Perumalaiyeduththaan Piduraikoyil,
Varumazaithavazum Maaliruncholai,
Thirumalaiyathuve Yadaivathuthirame. 2.10.4

Thiramudaivalaththaal Thivinaiperukkaathu,
Aramuyalaazip PadaiyavanKoyil,
Maruvilvansunaisooz Maaliruncholai,
Puramalaisaarap Povathukiriye. 2.10.5

KiriyenaNinaimin Kizmaiseyyaathe,
Uriyamarvenne Yundavan Koyil,
Mariyodupinaiser Maaliruncholai,
Neripadavathuve NinaivathuNalame. 2.10.6

NalamenaNinaimin Narakazundhaathe,
Nilamunamidandhaan Niduraikoyil,
Malamarumathiser Maaliruncholai,
Valamuraiyeythi Maruvuthalvalame. 2.10.7

Valamseythuvaikal Valangkaziyaathe,
ValamseyyumAaya Maayavan Koyil,
Valamseyyumvaanor Maaliruncholai,
ValamseythuNaalum Maruvuthalvazakke. 2.10.8

VazakkenaNinaimin Valvinaimoozkaathu,
Azakkodiyattaa NnamarPerungkoyil,
Mazakkalirrinancer Maaliruncholai,
Thozukkaruthuvathe Thunivathusoothe. 2.10.9

Soothenrugalavum Soothumseyyaathe,
Vethamunviriththaan Virumpiyakoyil,
Maathurumayilser Maaliruncholai,
Pothavizmalaiye Pukuvathuporule. 2.10.10

Porulenrivvulagam Padaiththavanpugazmel,
Marulilvankurukoor Vansadakopan,
Therulkollachchonna Voraayiraththulippaththu,
AruludaiyavanThaa Lanaivikkummudiththe. 2.10.11


Moondraam Patthu

Mudicchothi Yaayunathu Mugacchothi Malanthathuvo,
Adicchothi NeeNinra Thaamaraiyaay Alarnthathuvo,
Padicchothi Yaadaiyodum Palkalanaay, Ninpaimpon
Kadicchothi Kalanthathuvo? Thirumaale! Katturaiye. (2) 3.1.1.

Katturaikkil ThaamaraiNin Kanpaatham Kaiyovvaa,
Katturaittha Nan Ponnul Thirumeni Oli Ovvaathu,
Otturaitthiv Vulagunnaip Pugazvellaam Perumpaalum,
Patturaiyaayp Purkenre Kaattumaal Parancothee! 3.1.2.

Parancothi! Neeparamaay Ninnigazhnthu Pin, Marror
Parancothi Yinmaiyil Padiyovi Nigazkinra,
Parancothi Ninnulle Padarulakam Padaittha,Em
Parancothi Govinthaa! Panpuraikka Maattene. 3.1.3.

Maattaathe Yaakilumim MalarThalaimaa Nyaalam,Nin
Maattaaya Malarpuraiyum Thiruvuruvum Manamvaikka
Maattaatha Palasamaya Mathikodutthaay, Malartthuzaay
MaatteNee Manamvaitthaay Maanyaalam Varunthaathe? 3.1.4.

Varunthaatha Arunthavattha Malarkathirin Sudarudampaay,
Varunthaatha Nyaanamaay Varampinri Muzhuthiyanraay,
Varungaalam Nigazkaalam Kazikaala Maay,Ulakai
Orungaaka Alippaayseer Engulakka Othuvane? 3.1.5.

Othuvaar Otthellaam Evvulagath Thevvevaiyum,
Saathuvaay Ninpugazin Thagaiyallaal Pirithillai,
Pothuvaaz Punanthuzaay Mudiyinaay, Poovinmel
Maathuvaaz Maarpinaay! Ensolliyaan Vaaztthuvane? 3.1.6.

Vaaztthuvaar Palaraaga Ninnulle Naanmuganai,
MooztthaNee Rulakellaam Padaiyenru Muthalpadaitthaay
Keztthasee Raranmuthalaak Kilardheyva Maaykkilarnthu,
Sooztthamarar Thuthitthaalun Tholpugazmaa Soonaathe? 3.1.7.

Maasoonaac Sudarudampaay Malaraathu Kuviyaathu,
Maasoonaa Nyaanamaay Muzuthumaay Muzuthiyanraay,
Maasoonaa VaanKolath Thamararkon Vazipattaal,
Maasoonaa Unpaatha Malarsothi Mazungaathe? 3.1.8.

Mazungaatha VainNuthiya SakkaraNal Valatthaiyaay,
Thozungaathal Kaliralippaan Pulloornthu Thonrinaiye,
Mazungaatha Nyaaname Padaiyaaga, Malarulakil
Thozumpaayaark Kalitthaalun Sudarchchothi Maraiyaathe? 3.1.9.

Maraiyaaya Naalvedhath ThulNinra Malarsudare,
Muraiyaaliv Vulakellaam Padaitthidanthun Dumiznthalanthaay,
Piraiyeru Sadaiyaanum Naanmuganum Inthiranum
Iraiyaathal Arinthettha Veerrirutthal Ithuviyappe? 3.1.10.

Viyappaaya Viyappillaa Meynynyaana Vedhiyanai,
Sayappugazaar Palarvaazum Thadankurukoor Sadagopan,
Thuyakkinrith Thozuthuraittha Aayiratthu Lippatthum,
Uyakkondu Pirapparukkum OlimunNeer Nyaalatthe. (2) 3.1.11

MunNeer Nyaalam Padaitthavem Mukilvannane,
AnNaalNee Thantha Aakkaiyin Vaziyuzalven,
VenNaalNoy Veeya Vinaigalaiver Arappaaynthu,
EnNaalyaan Unnai Inivanthu Kooduvane? (2) 3.2.1.

Vanmaa Vaiyam Alantha Em Vaamanaa,Nin
Panmaa Maayap Palpiraviyil Padikinrayaan,
Thonmaa Valvinaith Thodargalai Muthalarinthu,
Ninmaathaal Sernthu Nirpatheny Nyaanrukolo? 3.2.2.

Kollaa Maakkol Kolaiseythu Paarathappor,
Ellaac Senaiyum IruNilath Thavitthaventhaay,
Pollaa Aakkaiyin Punarvinai Arukkalaraa,
Sollaayyaa Nnunnaic Saarvathor Soozcchiye. 3.2.3.

Soozcchi Nyaanac Sudaroli Yaaki,Enrum
Ezcchikke Dinri Enganum Nirainthaventhaay,
Thaazcchimar Rengum ThavirnthuNin Thaalinakkeez
Vaazcchi,Yaan Serum Vagaiyarulaay Vanthe. 3.2.4.

Vanthaaypo Levanthum Enmanath ThinaiNee,
Sinthaamal Seyyaay Ithuve Yithuvaakil,
Konthaarkaa Yaavin Kozumalarth ThiruNiraththa
Enthaay,Yaa Nnunnai Enguvann Thanukirpane? 3.2.5.

Kirpan Killen Enrilan MunaNaalaal,
Arpasaa Rangal Avaisuvaith Thakanrozinthen,
Parpal Laayiram Uyirseytha Paramaa,Nin
NarponSo Thitthaal Nanukuva Thenynyaanre? 3.2.6.

Enynyaanru Naamirunn Thirunthirangi Nence!
Meynynyaana Minri Vinaiyiyal Pirappazunthi,
Enynyaanrum Engum Ozivara NirainthuNinra,
Meynynyaanac Sothik Kannanai Mevuthume? 3.2.7.

Mevu Thunpa Vinaigalai Vidutthumilen,
Ovutha Linri UnKazal Vanangirrilen,
Paavuthol Seerkkannaa! En Parancudare,
Koovukinren Kaanpaan Engoythak Koovuvane? 3.2.8.

Koovikkoovik Koduvinaith Thoorrul Ninru
Paaviyen Palakaalam Vazithigaith Thalamarkinren,
Meviyan RaaNirai Kaatthava Nnulakamellaam,
Thaaviya Ammaanai Enginith Thalaippeyvane? 3.2.9.

Thalaippey Kaalam NamanDhamar Paasamvittaal,
Alaippoo Nunnumav Vallalel Laamakala,
Kalaippal Nyaanatthen Kannanaik Kandukondu,
Nilaipperren Nnencam Perrathu Needuyire. 3.2.10.

Uyirga Lellaa Ulakamu Mudaiyavanai,
Kuyilkol Solaith ThenKurukoorc Sadagopan,
Seyirilsol Isaimaalai Aayiratthu Lippatthum,
Uyirinme Laakkai Oonidai Ozivikkume. (2) 3.2.11

Ozivil Kaalamellaam Udanaay Manni,
Vazuvilaa Adimai Seyya VendumNaam,
Theziku RalAru Vitthiru Vengadatthu,
Ezilkol Sothi Enthaithanthai Thanthaikke (2) 3.3.1

Enthai Thanthai Thanthai Thanthaikkum
Munthai, Vaanavar Vaanavar Konodum,
Sinthupoo Makizum Thiruveng Kadatthu,
Antha Milpugazk Kaarezil Annale. 3.3.2

Annal Maayan Anikolsenn Thaamaraik
Kannan, Sengani Vaaykkaru Maanikkam,
Thenni Raiccunai Neertthiru Vengadatthu,
Ennil Tholpugaz Vaanava Reesane. 3.3.3

Isan Vaanavark Kenpanen Raal,Athu
Thesa Mothiru Vengadath Thaanukku?,
Neesa NnenNirai Vonrumi Len,EnKan
Paasam Vaittha Parancudarc Sothikke. 3.3.4

Sothi Yaakiyel Laavula Kumthozum,
Aathi Moortthiyen Raalala Vaagumo?,
Vethi Yarmuzu Vedhath Thamuthatthai,
Theethil SeerTthiru Vengadath Thaanaiye. 3.3.5

Venga Dangalmeym Melvinai Murravum,
Thaangal Thangatku Nallana Veseyvaar,
Venga Datthurai Vaarkku Namavenna
Laanga Damai,A Thusumann Thaarkatke. 3.3.6

Sumanthu Maamalar Neersudar Dheepamkondu,
Amarnthu Vaanavar Vaanavar Konodum,
Namanre Zumthiru Vengadam Nangatku,
SamanKol Veedu Tharumthadang Kunrame. 3.3.7

Kunram Enthik Kulirmazai Kaatthavan,
Anru Nyaalam Alantha Piraan,Paran
Senru SerThiru Vengada Maamalai,
Onru Methoza Namvinai Oyume. (2) 3.3.8

Oyu Mooppup Pirappirap Puppini,
Veeyu Maarusey VaanThiru Vengadath
Thaayan, Naanmala Raamadith Thaamarai,
Vaayul Lummanath Thullumvaip Paargatke. 3.3.9

Vaittha Naalvarai Ellai Kurukiccenru,
Eytthi Laippathan Munnam Adaimino,
Paittha Paambanai YaanThiru Vengadam,
Moyttha Solaimoy Poonthadam Thaazvare. 3.3.10

Thaalpa Rappiman Vathaaviya Isanai,
Neelpo Zilkuru Koorccada Gopansol,
Kezil Aayirath Thippatthum Vallavar,
Vaazvar Vaazveythi Nyaalam Pugazave. (2) 3.3.11

PugazhuNal Oruvan EnGo!
Poruvilseerp Boomi YenGo,
Thigazhumthan Paravai EnGo!
TheeyenGo! Vaayu EnGo,
NigazumAa Kaasa MenGo!
Neelsudar Irandum EnGo,
Igazviliv Vanaitthum EnGo
Kannanaik Koovumaare! (2) 3.4.1

Koovumaa Rariya Maatten
Kunrangal Anaitthum EnGo,
Mevuseer Maari EnGo!
Vilanguthaa Ragaigal EnGo,
Naaviyal Kalaigal EnGo!
NyaanaNal Laavi EnGo,
Paavuseerk Kannan Emmaan
Pangayak Kanna Nnaiye! 3.4.2

Pangaiyak Kannan EnGo!
Pavalassev Vaayan EnGo,
Angathir Adiyan EnGo!
Ancana Vannan EnGo,
Sengathir Mudiyan EnGo!
Thirumaru Maarvan EnGo,
Sangusak Karatthan EnGo!
Saathimaa Nikkath Thaiye! 3.4.3

Saathimaa Nikkam EnGo!
Savikolpon Muttham EnGo,
SaathiNal Vayiram EnGo,
Thavivilseer Vilakkam EnGo,
Aathiyany Sothi EnGo!
Aathiyam Purudan EnGo,
Aathumil Kaalath Thenthai
Acchuthan Amala Nnaiye! 3.4.4

Acchuthan Amalan EnGo,
Adiyavar Vinaikedukkum,
Naccumaa Maruntham EnGo!
Nalangadal Amutham EnGo,
Acchuvaik Katti EnGo!
Arusuvai Adisil EnGo,
Neyccuvaith Theral EnGo!
KaniyenGo! Paalen Geno! 3.4.5

PaalenGo! NaanGu Vedhap
PayanenGo, Samaya Neethi
NoolenGo! Nudangu Kelvi
IsaiyenGo! Ivarrul Nalla
MelenGo, Vinaiyin Mikka
PayanenGo, Kannan EnGo!
MaalenGo! Maayan EnGo
Vaanavar Aathi Yaiye! 3.4.6

Vaanavar Aathi EnGo!
Vaanavar Theyvam EnGo,
Vaanavar Bogam EnGo!
Vaanavar Murrum EnGo,
Oonamil Selvam EnGo!
Oonamil Suvarkkam EnGo,
Oonamil Mokkam EnGo!
Olimani Vanna Nnaiye! 3.4.7

Olimani Vannan EnGo!
Oruvanen Rettha Ninra
Nalirmathic Sadaiyan EnGo!
Naanmugak Kadavul EnGo,
Alimagiznn Thulakamellaam
Padaitthavai Ettha Ninra,
Kalimalarth Thulava Nnemmaan
Kannanai Maaya Nnaiye! 3.4.8

Kannanai Maayan Dhannaik
Kadalkadainn Thamuthang Konda,
Annalai Acchu Thannai
Ananthanai Ananthan Dhanmel,
NanniNan Kuraikin Raanai
Nyaalamun Dumizntha Maalai,
Ennumaa Rariya Maatten,
Yaavaiyum Yavarum Thaane. 3.4.9

Yaavaiyum Yavarum Thaanaay
Avaravar Samayann Thorum,
Thoyvilan Pulanainn Thukkum
Solappadaan Unarvin Moortthi,
Aaviser Uyirin Ullaal
Athumor Parri Laatha,
Paavanai Athanaik Koodil
Avanaiyum Kooda Laame. 3.4.10

Koodivan Daraiyum ThanDhaarkkondalpol Vannan Dhannai
Maadalar Pozilku Rukoor Vansada Gopan Sonna,
Paadalor Aayi Ratthul Ivaiyumor Patthum Vallaar,
Veedila Boga Meythi Virumbuvar Amarar Moytthe (2) 3.4.11

Moymmaam Poompozhil Poygai
Mudhalaic Siraippattu Ninra,
Kaimmaa Vukkarul Seytha
Kaarmugil Polvannan Kannan,
Emmaa Nnaiccollip Paadi
Ezhunthum Paranthumthul Laathaar,
Thammaal Karumamen Solleer
Thankadal Vattatthul Leere! (2) 3.5.1

Thankadal Vattatthul Laaraith
Thamakkirai Yaaththadinn Thunnum,
Thinkazar Kaalasu Rarkkuth
Theengizaik Kumthiru Maalai,
Pangal Thalaikkollap Paadip
Paranthum Kunitthuza Laathaar,
Mankol Ulakil Pirappaar
Valvinai Motha Malainthe. 3.5.2

Malaiyai Yedutthukkal Maari
Kaatthup PasuNirai Thannai,
Tholaivu Thavirttha Piraanaic
Solliccol LiNirep Pothum,
Thalaiyino Daathanam Thattath
Thadukutta Maayppara Vaathaar,
Alaikol Naragath Thazunthik
Kidanthuzaik Kinra Vambare. 3.5.3

Vampaviz Gothai Poruttaa
Maalvidai Yezhum Adarttha,
Sempava Latthiral Vaayan
Sireedharan Tholpugaz Paadi,
Kumbidu Nattamit Taadik
Kokukat Tunduzha Laathaar,
Thampirap Paalpaya Nnenne
Saadhu Sananga Lidaiye? 3.5.4

Saadhu Sanatthai Naliyum
Kancanaic Saathippa Tharku,
Aathiyany Sothi Yuruvai
Anguvaith Thingup Pirantha,
Vedha Muthalvanaip Paadi
Veethigal Thorumthul Laathaar,
Othi Yunarnthavar Munnaa
Ensavip Paarma Nnisare? 3.5.5

Manisarum Marrum Murrumaay
Maayap Piravi Pirantha,
Thaniyan Pirappili Thannaith
Thadangadal Serntha Piraanai,
Kaniyaik Karumbinin Saarraik
Kattiyaith Thenai Amudhai,
Munivinri Etthik Kunippaar
Muzhuthunar Neermaiyi Nnaare. 3.5.6

Neermai Noorruvar Veeya
Aivark Karulseythu Ninru,
Paarmalku Senai Avittha
Parancuda RaiNinainn Thaadi.
Neermalgu Kannina Raagi
Nencam KuzhainthuNai Yaadhe,
Urmalgi Modu Paruppaar
Utthamarkat Kensey Vaare? 3.5.7

Vaarpunal Anthan Naruvi
Vadathiru Vengadath Thenthai,
Perpala Sollip Pitharrip
Pittharen Repirar Koora,
Urpala Pukkum Pukaathum
Ulokar SirikkaNin Raadi,
Aarvam Perukik Kunippaar
Amarar Thozappadu Vaare. 3.5.8

Amarar Thozappadu Vaanai
Anaitthula Kukkum Piraanai,
Amarar Manatthinul Yogu
Punarnthavan Dhannodon Raaga,
Amarath Thuniyaval Laargal
OzhiyaAl Laathava Rellaam,
Amara Ninainthezhunn Thaadi
Alarruva Thekaru Mame. 3.5.9

Karumamum Karuma Palanum
Aakiya Kaaranan Dhannai,
Thirumani Vannanaic Sengan
Maalinaith Theva Piraanai,
Orumai Manatthinul Vaitthu
Ullang Kuzainthezhunn Thaadi,
Perumaiyum Naanum Thavirnthu
Pitharrumin Pethamai Theernthe. 3.5.10

Theerntha Adiyavar Thammaiththirutthip Panikolla Valla,
Aarntha Pukazhac Suthanai Amarar Piraanaiyem Maanai,
Vaayntha Valavayal Soozhthan Valanguru Koorccadagopan,
Nernthavo Raayirath Thippath Tharuvinai Neeru Seyyume. (2) 3.5.11

Seyya Thaamaraik Kanna Nnaayula
Kezu Munda AvanKandeer,
Vaiyam Vaanam Manisar Dheyvam
Marrum Marrum Matrum Murrumaay,
Seyya Soozsudar Nyaana Maayvelip
Patti Vaipadaith Thaanpinnum,
Moykol Sothiyo Daayi Nnaanoru
Moova Raagiya Moortthiye. (2) 3.6.1

Moova Raagiya Moortthi Yaimudhal
Moovark Kumuthal Vanrannai,
Saava Mullana Neekku Vaanaith
Thadanga Dalgidann ThaanDhannaith,
Dheva Dhevanaith Thenni Langai
Eriye Zaccerra Villiyai,
Paava Naasanaip Panga Yatthadang
Kanna Nnaippara Vumino. 3.6.2

Paravi Vaanava Rettha Ninra
Parama Nnaipparany Sothiyai,
Kuravai Kottha Kuzaka Nnaimani
Vanna Nnaikkudak Kootthanai,
Arava Meri Yalaika Dalama
Rumthu Yilkonda Annalai,
Iravum Nanpaga Lumvi Daathenrum
Etthu Thalmanam Vaimmino. 3.6.3

Vaimmin Nummanath Thenru Yaanuraik
Kinra Maayavan Seermaiyai
Emma Nnorga Luraippa Then? Athu
Nirka Naaldhorum, Vaanavar
Thammai Yaalum Avanum Naanmuga
Nnumsa Daimudi Annalum,
Semmai Yaalavan Paatha Pangayam
Sinthith Thetthi Thirivare. 3.6.4

Thiriyum Karro Dakalvi Sumbu
Thinintha Mankidann Thakadal,
Eriyum Theeyo Dirusu Dardheyvam,
Marrum Marrum Murrumaay,
Kariya Meniyan Seyya Thaamaraik
Kannan Kannanvin Norirai,
Suriyum Palkarung Kunci Yengal
Sudarmu Diyannal Thorrame. 3.6.5

Thorrak Kedavai Yilla Vanudai
Yaana Vanoru Moortthiyaay,
Seerrath Thodarul Perra Vanadik
Keezppu KaNinra Senganmaal,
Naarrath Thorrac Suvaiyo LiOo Ral
Aagi Ninra,Em Vaanavar
Errai Yeyanri Marro Ruvarai
Yaani Lenezu Maikkume. 3.6.6

Ezumaik Kumena Thaavik Kinnamu
Thaththi NnaiE Nna Thaaruyir,
Kezumi Yagathirc Sothi Yaimani
Vanna Nnaikkudak Kootthanai,
Vizumi Yavama Rarmu Nivarvi
Zungum Kannal Kaniyinai,
Thozumin Thooyama Nnattha Raayirai
YumNil Laathuya Rangale. 3.6.7

Thuyara Metharu Thunba Inba
Vinaika LaayA Vai Allanaay,
Uyara Ninrathor Sothi Yaayula
Kezu Mundumiznn ThaanDhannai,
Ayara Vaangu NamanDha Markkaru
Nanci Nnaiyaccu ThanDhannai,
Thayara Tharkuma KanDhan Nnaiyanri
Marri Lennthanca Maagave. 3.6.8

Thanca Maagiya Thanthai Thaayodu
Thaanu Maayavai Allanaay,
Enca Lilama Rarku Lamudhal
Moovar Thammullu Maathiyai,
Anci Neerula Katthul Leergal!
Avani Vanenru Koozenmin,
Nenci NnaalNinaip Paanya Vanavan
Aagum Neelkadal Vannane. 3.6.9

Kadalvan NanKannan Vinna Varkaru
Maanik Kamena Thaaruyir
Padava Ravina Naikki Dantha
Parancu Darpandu Noorruvar,
Adava Rumpadai Manga Aivarkat
Kaaki Vencamatthu, Anruther
Kadavi Yaperu MaanKa Nnaikazal
Kaanba Thenrukol Kangale? 3.6.10

Kangal Kaandar Kariya Nnaaykkaruth
Thukku Nanrume Liyanaay,
Mankol Nyaalatthu Yirkkel Laamarul
Seyyum Vaanava Reesanai,
Pankol Solai Vazuthi Naadan

Naangaam Paththu

Orunnaa Yagamaay Oda,Vulaguda Nnaandavar,
Karunnaay Kavarntha Kaalar Sidhaigiya Paanaiyar,
Perunnaadu Kaana Immaiyilepichchai Thaamkolvar,
ThirunnaarananThaal Kaalam Perachchindhith Thuymmino. 4.1.1

Uymmin Thiraikonarnn Thenrulagaandavar, Immaiye
Thammin Suvaimada Vaaraippirar Kollath Thaamvittu
Vemmi Nnoliveyil Kaanagampoykkumai Thinpargal,
Semmin Mudiththiru Maalaiviraindhadi Sermino. 4.1.2

Adiser Mudiyina Raagiyarasargal Thaamthozha,
Idiser Murasangal Murraththiyamba Irunthavar,
Podiser Thugalaayp Povargalaadhalin Nokkena
Kadiser Thuzhaaymudik Kannan Kazhalgal Ninaimino. 4.1.3

Ninaippaan Pugilkadal Ekkalin Nunmana Lirpalar,
Enaiththo Rugangalum Ivvula Gaandu Kazhinthavar,
Manaippaal Marungara Maaydhalallaalmarruk Kandilam,
Panaiththaal Madhakali Rattavan Paadham Panimino. 4.1.4

Panimin Thiruvarul EnnumAnceedhap Paimpoomballi,
Animen Kuzhalaar Inbakkalavi Amudhundaar,
Thunimunbu Naalappal Lezhaiyar Thaamizhip Pachchelvar,
Maniminnu Meninnam Maayavan Persolli Vaazhmino. 4.1.5

Vaazhndhaargal Vaazhndhadhu Maamazhai Mokkulin Maayndhumaayndhu,
Aazhndhaaren Rallaal Anru Mudhalin Rarudhiyaa,
Vaazhndhaargal Vaazhndhe Nirparen Badhillai Nirkuril,
Aazhndhaar Kadalpalli Annal Adiyavar Aamino. 4.1.6

Aamin Suvaiyavai Aarodadisilun Daarndhapin,
Thoomen Mozhimada Vaarirakkappinnum Thurruvaar,
'Eemin Emakkoru Thur'renridaruva Raadhalin,
Komin Thuzhaaymudi Aadhiyanchodhi Gunangale. 4.1.7

Gunangol Niraipugazh Mannarkodaikkadan Poondirundhu,
Inangi Yulaguda Nnaakkilum Aangava Nnaiyillaar,
Manangonda Pogaththu Manniyu Meelvargal Meelvillai,
Panangol Aravanai YaanThiru Naamam Padimino. 4.1.8

Padimannu Palkalan ParrodaruththuAim Bulanvenru,
Chedimannu Kaayamserraargalu Maangava Nnaiyillaar,
Kudimannu Minsuvargga Meydhiyumeelvargal Meelvillai,
Kodimannu Pulludai Annal Kazhalgal Kurugumino. 4.1.9

Kuruga Migavunar Vaththodu Nokkiyel Laamvitta,
Iruga Lirappennum Nyaanikkum Appaya Nnillaiyel,
Siruga Ninaivadhor Paasamundaampinnum Veedillai,
Marupagalil Eesanaip Parri Vidaavidil Veedaqdhe. 4.1.10

Aqdhe Uyyap Pugumaarenru Kannan Kazhalgalmel,
Koypoom Pozhilsoozh Kurugoorchchadagopan Kurreval,
Seykolath Thaayiram Seerththodaippaadal Ivaipaththum,
Aqgaamar Karpavar Aazhthuyar Poyuyyar Paalare. (2) 4.1.11

Baalanaa Yezhula Gundu Parivinri,
Aalilai Yannava Sanycheyyum Annalaar,
Thaalinai Melani Thannann Thuzhaayenre
Maalumaal, Valvinai Yenmada Valliye. (2) 4.2.1

Valliser Nunnidai Yaaychchiyar Thammodum,
Kollaimai Seydhu Kuravai Pinaindhavar,
Nalladi Melani Naaru Thuzhaayenre
Sollumaal, Soozhvinai Yaattiyen Paavaiye. 4.2.2

Paaviyal Vedhannan Maalai Palakondu,
Dhevargal Maamuni Varirainy Channinra
Sevadi Melani Sembor Ruzhaayenre
Koovumaal, Kolvinai Yaattiyen Godhaiye. 4.2.3

Kodhila Vanpugazh Kondu Samayigal,
Pedhangal Sollip Pidharrum Piraanparan,
Paadhangal Melani Paimpor Ruzhaayenre
Odhumaal, Oozhvinai YenThadann Tholiye. 4.2.4

Tholiser Pinnai Porutteru ThezhthazheeI K
Koliyaar Kovala Nnaarkudak Kooththanaar,
Thaalinai Melani Thannandhu Zhaayenre
Naalunnaal, Naiginra DhaalE NnDhan Maadhare. 4.2.5

Maadharmaa Manmadann Dhaiporut Tenamaay,
Aadhiyang Kaalath Thagalidam Keendavar,
Paadhangal Melani Paimpor Ruzhaayenre
Odhummaal, Eydhinal EnnDhan Madandhaiye. 4.2.6

Madandhaiyai Vankama Laththiru Maadhinai,
Thadangoldhaar Maarbinil Vaiththavar Thaalinmel,
Vadangolpoonn Thannann Thuzhaaymalark Keyival
Madangumaal, Vaanudha Leer!En Madakkombe. 4.2.7

Kombupol Seedhai Poruttilang Gainnagar
Amberi Yuyththavar Thaalinai Melani,
Vambavizh Thannandhu Zhaaymalark Keyival
Nambumaal, Naanidhar Kenseygen Nangaimeer! 4.2.8

Nangaimeer! NeerumO R Penperru Nalgineer,
Enynyane Sollugen Yaanperra Ezhaiyai,
Sangennum Sakkara Mennum Thuzhaayennum,
Inynyane Sollum Iraappagal Enseygen? 4.2.9

Enseygen Ennudaip Pedhaiyen Komalam,
Ensollum Envasa Mumallal Nangaimeer,
Minseypoon Maarbinan Kannan Kazhalthuzhaay,
Ponseypoon Menmulaik Kenru Meliyume. 4.2.10

Meliyunnoy Theerkkumnnang Kannan Kazhalgalmel,
Malipugazh Vankuru Goorchchada Gobansol,
Olipugazh Aayirath Thippaththum Vallavar,
Malipugazh Vaanavark Kaavarnnar Kovaiye.(2) 4.2.11

Kovai Vaayaal Porutterrin
Eruththam Iruththaay, Madhililangaik
Kovai Veeyach Chilaikuniththaay!
Kulannal Yaanai Marupposiththaay,
Poovai Veeyaa NeerThoovip
Podhaal Vanange Nnelum,Nnin
Poovai Veeyaam Menikkup
Poosum Saandhen Nnenchame. (2) 4.3.1

Punaiyum Kanni Enadhudaiya,

EnKai Kooppuch Cheygaiye,

'Kaala Sakka Raththodu Vensang Gamkai Yendhinaay,

Ola Mittu Naanazhaiththaal Onrum Vaaraa Yaagilum,

Kuraika Zhalgal Neettiman Konda Kola Vaamanaa,

Enna Dhaavi Melaiyaay Ergol Ezhu Lagamum,

Unna Dhenna Dhaaviyum Enna Dhunna Dhaaviyum
Inna Vanna Menninraay Enru Raikka Vallene? 4.3.8

'Nedumaal Adiyaar'en Rodum,
Naaru Thuzhaaymalar Kaanil
'Naaranan Kanniyee 'Dhennum,
Theriyum Theraadhu Maayon
Thiraththana Leyith Thiruve. 4.4.7

Thiruvudai Mannaraik Kaanil
'Thirumaalaik Kandene' Ennum,
Uruvudai Vannangal Kaanil
'Ulagalann Thaan'enru Thullum,
Karuvudaith Thevilga Lellaam
'Kadalvannan Koyile' Ennum
Veruvilum Veezhvilum Ovaal
Kannan Kazhalgal Virumbume. 4.4.8

Virumbip Pagaivaraik Kaanil
'Viyalidam Undaane!' Ennum,
Karumperu Megangal Kaanil
'Kannan'en Rerap Parakkum,
Perumpula Aannirai Kaanil
'Piraanulan' Enrupin Sellum,
Arumperal Penninai Maayon
Alarri AyarPpikkin Raane! 4.4.9

Ayarkkumsur Rumparri Nokkum
Agalave Neel Nokkuk Kollum,
Viyarkkum Mazhaikkan Thulumba
Vevvuyirk Kollummey Sorum,
Peyarththum'kan Naa!'Enru Pesum,
'Perumaane! Vaa!'Enru Koovum,
Mayalperung Kaadhalen Pedhaik
Kenseygen Valvinai Yene! 4.4.10

Valvinai Theerkkum Kannanai
Vankuru Goorchchada Gopan,
Solvinai Yaalsonna Paadal
Aayirath Thullivai Paththum,
Nalvinai Yenrukar Paargal
Nalanidai Vaigundham Nanni,
Tholvinai Theeravel Laarum
Thozhudhezha Veerrirup Paare. (2) 4.4.11

Veerrirunn Dhezhulagum Thanikkol Sella, Veevilseer,
Aarralmik Kaalum Ammaanaivemmaa PilandhaanDhannai,
Porri Yenre Kaigalaarath Thozhudhu Solmaalaigal,
Erra Norrer Kiniyennakurai Yezhumaiyume? (2) 4.5.1

Maiya Kannaal Malarmeluraivaa Luraimaarbinan,
Seyya Kolath Thadangannan Vinnor PerumaanDhannai
Moyya Sollaa Lisaimaalaigaleththi Yullap Perren,
Veyya Noygal Muzhudhum ViyanNyaalaththu Veeyave. 4.5.2

Veevi Linba MigaEllai Nigazhndhannam Achchudhan,
Veevil Seeran Malarkkannan Vinnor PerumaanDhannai,
Veevil Kaalam Isaimaalaigal Eththi Mevapperren,
Veevi Linbamiga Ellai Nigazhndhanan Meviye. 4.5.3

Mevi Ninru Thozhuvaar Vinaipoga Mevumpiraan,
Thooviyam Pullu Daiyaan Adalaazhiyam MaanDhannai,
Naaviya Laalisai Maalaiga Leththinnan Napperren,
Aaviyen Nnaaviyai Yaanariyenseydha Vaarraiye. 4.5.4

Aarra Nalla Vagaikaattum Ammaanai, Amarardham
Errai Yellaap Porulum Viriththaanai EmmaanDhannai,
Maarra Maalai Punaindheththi Naalum Magizhveydhinen,
Kaarrin Munnam Kadugi Vinainnoygal Kariyave. 4.5.5

Kariya Menimisai Veliya Neerusiri Dheyidum,
Periya Kolath Thadangannan Vinnor PerumaanDhannai,
Uriya Sollaa Lisaimaalaigal Eththiyullap Perrerku,
Ariya Dhundo Enakkinru Thottumini Yenrume? 4.5.6

Enrum Onraagi Yoththaarummikkaargalum, Thanranak
Kinri Ninraanai Yellaavulagum Udaiyaan Dhannai,
Kunra Monraal Mazhaikaaththapiraanaichchon Maalaigal,
Nanru Soottum Vidhiyeydhinam Enna Kurainnamakke? 4.5.7

Namakkum Poovinmisai Nangaikkum Inbanai, Nyaalaththaar
Thamakkum Vaanath Thavarkkum Perumaanai, Thandaamarai
Sumakkum Paadhap Perumaanaich Chonmaalaigal, Sollumaa
Ramaikka Valler Kiniyaavar Nigaragal Vaanaththe? 4.5.8

Vaanaththum Vaanaththul Lumbarum
Mannullum ManninKeezhth
Thaanaththum, Endisai Yumthavi
Raathunnin RaanDhannai,
Koonarsang Gaththadak Kaiyavanaik
Kudamaadiyai Vaanak
Konaik, Kavisolla Valler
Kinimaa Rundo? 4.5.9

Undum Umizhnndhum Kadandhum
Idandhum Kidandhumnninrum,
Konda Kolath Thoduveer
Rirundhum Manangoodiyum,
Kanda Vaarraal Thanadhe
Yulagena NinraanDhannai,
VanThamizh Noorka Norren
Adiyaark Kinbamaariye. 4.5.10

Maari Maaraatha Thannammalai
Vengadath Thannalai,
Vaari Vaaraatha Paimpoom
Pozhilsoozh Kurugoornnagar,
Kaari Maaran Sadagopan
Sollaayirath Thippaththaal,
Veri Maaraatha Poome
Liruppaal Vinaitheerkkume. (2) 4.5.11

Theerppaarai Yaamini Yenynyanam
Naaduthum Annaimeer,
Orppaaliv Vonnuthal Urrannan
Noyidhu Therinom,
Porppaagu Thaanseydhan Raivarai
Velviththa, Maayapporth
Therppaaga Nnaarkkival Sindhai
Thuzhaayththisaik Kinradhe. 4.6.1

Thisaikkinra Theyival Noyidhu
Mikka Perundheyvam,
Isaippinri Neeranang Gaadum
Ilandheyvam Anrithu,
Thisaippinri Yesangu Sakkara
Menrival Ketka,Neer
Isaikkirri Raagilnnan Reyil
Perumithu Kaanmine. 4.6.2

Idhukaanmin Annaimeer! Ikkattu
Vichchisor Kondu,Neer
Edhuvaanum Seydhangor Kallum
Iraichchiyum Thoovelmin,
Madhuvaar Thuzhaaymudi Maayap
PiraanKazhal Vaazhththinaal,
Adhuve Yivalurra Noykkum
Arumarunn Thaagume. 4.6.3

Marunthaagum Enrangor Maaya
Valavaisor Kondu,Neer
Karunchorum Marraich Chenychorum
Kalanizhaith Thenpayan?
Orungaaga Veyula Gezhum
Vizhungi Umizhnnthitta,
Perunnthevan Persolla Kirkil
Ivalaip Peruthire. 4.6.4

Ivalaip Perumpari Sivvanang Gaaduthal Anrantho,
Kuvalaith Thadankannum Kovaichchevvaayum Payanthanal,
Kavalak Kadaakkali RattapiraanThiru Naamaththaal,
Thavalap Podikkondu Neerittidumin Thaniyume. 4.6.5

Thaniyum Pozhudhillai Neerananggaaduthir Annaimeer,
Piniyum Ozhiginra Thillai Perugu Mithuvallaal,
Maniyin Aninnira Maayan Thamaradi Neerukondu,
Aniya Muyalinmar Rillaikandeeriv Vanangukke. 4.6.6

Ananguk Karumarunn Thenrangor Aadumkal Lumbaraay
Thunangai Yerinthunnunn Tholkulaikkappadum Annaimeer,
Unangal Kedakkazhu Dhaiyuthataattamkan Denpayan?
Vanangeergal Maayap PiraanThamar Vedhamval Laaraiye. 4.6.7

Vedhamval Laargalaik KonduvinnorPeru MaanThirup
Paadham Paninthu,Ival Noyidhu Theerththukkol Laadhupoy
Edham Parainthalla Seydhugalloodu Kalaayththooy,
Geetha Muzhavittu Neer Anang Gaaduthal Keezhmaiye. 4.6.8

Keezhmaiyinaa Langor Keezhmagannitta MuzhavinKeezh,
Naazhmai Palasolli Neeranangaadumpoy Kaangilen,
Ezhmaip Pirappukkum Semaminn Noykkumee Themarunthu,
Uzhmaiyil Kannapi RaanKazhal Vaazhththumin Unniththe. 4.6.9

Unniththu Marroru Dheyvamthozhaalava Nnaiyallaal,
Nummichchai Sollinnum Tholkulaikkappadum Annaimeer,
Mannap Padummarai Vaananai Vanthuva Raapathi
Mannanai, Eththumin Eththudhalumthozhu Dhaadume. 4.6.10

Thozhudhaadi Thoomani Vannanukkaatseythu Noytheerntha
Vazhuvaatha Tholpugazh Vangurukoorchchada Gopan, Sol
Vazhuvaatha Aayirath Thullivai Paththu Verigalum,
Thozhudhaadip Paadaval LaarThukka Seelam Ilargale. 4.6.11

'Seelam Illaach Chiriya Nnelum Seyvinai Yoperidhaal,
Nyaalam Undaay Nyaanamoorththi 'Naaraaya Naa!' Enrenru,
Kaalann Dhorum Yaanirundhu Kaidhalai Poosalittaal
Kola Meni Kaana Vaaraay Kooviyum Kollaaye. (2) 4.7.1

'Kolla Maalaa Inba
Vellam Kodhila Thandhidum,En
Valla Leyo! Vaiyang Konda
Vaamanaa Vo!'Enrenru,
Nalli Raavum Nanpagalum
Naanirunn Dholamittaal,
Kalla Maayaa! Unnai
YenKan Kaanavann Theeyaaye. 4.7.2

'Eevi Laadha Theevinaigal Eththanai Seydha Nnannkol?
Thaavi Vaiyam Konda Endhaay! Thaamodharaa!'Enrenru
Koovik Koovi Nenychurugik Kanpani Sora Ninraal,
Paavi Neeyen Ronru Sollaay Paaviyen Kaanavandhe. 4.7.3

'Kaana Vandhena Kanmugappe Thaamaraik Kanpirazha,
Aani Sembon Meniyendhaay! Ninrarulaay' Enrenru,
Naana Millaach Chirudhakaiyen Naaning Kalarruvadhen,
Peni Vaanor Kaanamaattaap Peedudai Yappanaiye? 4.7.4

Appa Nne!Ada Laazhiyaane,
Aazhkada Laikkadaindha
Dhuppa Nne,Un Tholgal
Naanngum Kandidakkoodung Kolenru,
Eppo Zhudhum Kanna
Neergon Daavi Thuvarndhuvarndhu,
Ippo Zhudhe Vandhi
Daayen Rezhaiyen Nokkuvane. 4.7.5

Nokki Nokki Unnaik
Kaanbaan Yaanena Dhaaviyulle,
Naakku Neelvan Nyaana
Millai Naadoru Mennudaiya,
Aakkai Yullu Maavi
Yullum Allapu Raththinullum,
Neekka Minri Yengum
Ninraay! Ninnai Yarindharindhe. 4.7.6

Arindha Rindhu Therith
Theri Yaanena Dhaaviyulle,
Niraindha Nyaana Moorththi
Yaayai Ninnmala Maagavaiththu,
Pirandhum Seththum Ninridarum
Bedhaimai Theerndho Zhindhen
Narundhu Zhaayin Kanni
Yammaa! Naanunnaik Kandukonde! 4.7.7

Kandu Konden Kaiga Laara
NinThirup Paadhangalmel,
Endi Saiyu Mulla
Pookkon Deththi Yugandhugandhu,
Thonda Rongal Paadi
Yaadach Choozhkadal Nyaalaththulle,
Vandu Zhaayin Kanni
Vendhe! Vandhida Gillaaye. 4.7.8

Idagi Lenon Ratta
Gillen Aimbulan Vellagillen,
Kadava Nnaagik Kaalann
Thorum Poopparith Theththagillen,
Madavan Nenycham Kaadhal
Koora Valvinai YenA Yarppaay,
Thadavu Ginre Nnenguk
Kaanban Sakkarath Thannalaiye? 4.7.9

Sakka Raththan Naleyenru
Thaazhndhu Kanneer Thadhumba,
Pakkam Nokki Ninra
Landhen Paaviyen Kaanginrilen,
Mikka Nyaana Moorththi
Yaaya Vedha Vilakkinai,En
Thakka Nyaanak Kanga
Laale Kandu Thazhuvuvane. 4.7.10

Thazhuvi Ninra Kaadhalthannaal Thaamaraik KannanDhannai,
Kuzhuvu Maadath ThenKuru Goormaa Ransada Gopan,Sol
Vazhuvi Laatha Vondhamizhgal Aayiraththu Lippaththum,
Thazhuvap Paadi Yaada Vallaar Vaigundha Meruvare. (2) 4.7.11

Eraalum Iraiyonum Dhisaimuganum Thirumagalum,
Kooraalum Thaniyudamban Kulangulamaa Asurargalai,
Neeraagum Padiyaaga Nirumiththup Padaithotta,
Maaraalan Kavaraadha Manimaamai Kuraivilame. (2) 4.8.1

Manimaamai Kuraivillaa Malarmaadhar Uraimaarvan,
Animaanath Thadavaraiththol Adalaazhith Thadakkaiyan,
Panimaanam Pizhaiyaame Yadiyenaip Panikonda,
Manimaayan Kavaraadha Madannenychaal Kuraivilame. 4.8.2

Madannenychaal Kuraivillaa Magalthaaysey Thorupeychchi,
Vidannanycha Mulaisuvaiththa Migunyaanach Chirukuzhavi,
Padannaagath Thanaikkidandha Paruvaraiththol Paramburudan,
Nedumaayan Kavaraadha Niraiyinaal Kuraivilame. 4.8.3

Niraiyinaar Kuraivillaa
Nedumbanaiththol Madappinnai,
Poraiyinaal Mulaiyanaivaan
PoruvidaiEzh Adarththugandha,
Karaiyinaar Thuvarudukkai
Kadaiyaavin Kazhikolkai,
Saraiyinaar Kavaraadha
Thalirnniraththaal Kuraivilame. 4.8.4

Thalirnniraththaal Kuraivillaath
Thanichchiraiyil Vilappurra,
Kilimozhiyaal Kaaranamaak
Kilararakkan Nagareriththa,
Kalimalarth Thuzhaayangal
Kamazhmudiyan Kadalnyaalaththu,
Alimikkaan Kavaraadha
Arivinaal Kuraivilame. 4.8.5

Arivinaal Kuraivillaa Agalnyaalath Thavarariya,
Neriyella Meduththuraiththa Nirainyaanath Thorumoorththi,
Kuriyamaan Uruvaagik Kodungolaal Nilangonda,

Kilaroliyaal Kuraivillaa

Thagalmaarbam Kizhindhugandha,
Valaroliya Kanalaazhi
Valampuriyan Maninneela,

Varivalaiyaal Kuraivilame. 4.8.7

Amarar Kon Panindheththum,
Viripugazhaan Kavaraadha
Megalaiyaal Kuraivilame. 4.8.8

Megalaiyaal Kuraivillaa

Viralvaanan Puyamthuniththu,
Naagamisaith Thuyilvaanpol
Ulagellaam Nanngodunga,

Vudambinaal Kuraivilame. 4.8.9

Asurar Kuzhaam Thuniththugantha,

Thaniyorukoo Ramarnthuraiyum,

Uyirinaal Kuraivilame. 4.8.10

Uyirinaal Kuraivillaa
Ulagezhthan Ullodukki,
Thayirvenne Yundaanaith,
Thadangurugoorch Chadagopan,
Seyirilsol Lisaimaalai
Yaayiraththu Lippaththaal
Vayiramser Pirapparuththu
Vaigundham Nannuvare. (2) 4.8.11

Nannaadhaar Muruvalippa
Nallurraar Karainthenga,
Ennaaraath Thuyarvilaikkum
Ivaiyenna Ulagiyarkai?,
Kannaalaa! Kadalkadaindhaay!
Unagazharke Varumparisu,
Thannaavaa Dhadiyenaip
Panikandaay Saamaare. (2) 4.9.1

Saamaarum Kedumaarum

Aravanaiyaay! Ammaane,
Koomaare Viraikandaay
Adiyenaik Kurikkonde. 4.9.2

Kadalvannaa! Adiyenaip
Pandepol Karudhaadhun
Adikkekooyp Panikolle. 4.9.3

Kollenru Kilarndhezhundha
Perunychelvam Neruppaaga,
Kollenru Thamammoodum

Vallale! Manivannaa!
Unagazharke Varumparisu,
Vallalsey Dhadiyenai
Unadharulaal Vaangaaye. 4.9.4

Vaangunneer Malarulagil
Nirpanavumee Thirivanavum,

Pinimooppaal Thagarppunnum,
Eengidhanmel VenNaragam
Ivaiyenna Ulagiyarkai?
Vaangenainnee Manivannaa!
Adiyenai Marukkele. 4.9.5

Veriththulava Mudiyaane!
Vinaiyenai Yunakkadimai
Arakkondaay, Iniyennaa
Ramudhe!Kooy Arulaaye. 4.9.6

Aaye!Iv Vulagaththu Nirpanavum Thirivanavum
Neeyemar Roruporulum Inrinnee Ninramaiyaal,

Kaattinnee Karanthumizhum NilanneerThee Visumbukaal,
Eetteennee Vaiththamaiththa Imaiyorvaazh Thanimuttaik,
Kottaiyinil Kazhiththenaiyun Kozhunchothi Yuyaraththu,

Koottudhinnin Kuraikazhalgal Imaiyorum
Thozhaavagai Seydhu,
AattuthiNee Yaravanaiyaay!
Adiyenum Aqdharivan,
Vetkaiyellaam Viduththenaiyun
Thiruvadiye Sumandhuzhala,
Koottariya Thiruvadikkal
KoottinaiNaan Kandene. 4.9.9

Kanduket Turrumonthunduzhalum Aingaruvi
Kandavinbam, Therivariya Alavillaach Chirrinbam,
Ondodiyaal Thirumagalum Neeyume Nilaannirpak,
Kandasadhir Kandozhindhen Adaindhenun Thiruvadiye. 4.9.10

Thiruvadiyai Naarananaikkesavanaip Paranychudarai,
Thiruvadiser Vadhukarudhich Chezhungurugoorch Chadagopan,
Thiruvadime Luraiththathamizh Aayiraththu Lippaththum,
Thiruvadiye Adaivikkum Thiruvadisernn Thonrumine. (2) 4.9.11

Onrunn Dhevu Mulagum
Uyirum Marrum Yaadhumillaa
Anru, Naanmugan Dhannodu
Dheva Rulago DuyirPadaiththaan,

Needu Thirukkuru Gooradhanul,
Ninra Aadhippi RaanNirka
Marraith Dheyvam Naadudhire. (2) 4.10.1

Naadi Neerva Nangum
Dheyvamum Ummaiyu Munpadaiththaan,
Veedil Seerppuga Zhaadhippi

Selminngal Pallula Geer!Paranthe. 4.10.2

Parantha Dheyvamum Pallula
Gumpadaith Thanruda Nnevizhungik,

Danthathu Kandum Theliyagilleer,
Siranga LaalA Mararva
Nangum Thirukkuru Gooradhanul,
Parannthira Manrip Pallulageer!
Dheyvam Marrillai Pesumine! 4.10.3

Pesa Ninra Sivanuk
Kumbira ManDhanak Kumpirarkkum
Naaya Ganava Nne,Ka
Baalannan Mokkaththuk Kandukolmin,
Dhesa Maamadhil Soozhnthazha
Kaaya Thirukkuru Gooradhanul,
Eesan Paalor Avamba
Raithalen Nnaavathi Lingiyarkke? 4.10.4

Ilingath Thitta Puraanath
Theerum Samanarum Saakkiyarum
Valinthu Vaadhusey Veergalum
Marrunnunn Dheyvamu Maaginninraan
Malinthu SenNel Kavari
Veesum Thirukkuru Gooradhanul,
Polinthu Ninrapi RaanKandee
Ronrum Poyyillai Porrumine. (2) 4.10.5

Porri Marror Dheyvam
Penap Puraththittu Ummaiyinne
Therri Vaiththathel Leerum
Veedu Perraalula Gillaiyenre,
Serril SenNel Kamalam
Ongu Thirukkuru Gooradhanul,
Aarra Vallavan Maayam
Kandeeradhu Arintharinn Thodumine. 4.10.6

Odi Yodip Palpirappum Piranthumar Rordheyvam,
Paadi Yaadip Paninthupalpadikaal Vazhiye Rikkandeer,
Koodi Vaanava Reththaninra Thirukkuru Gooradhanul,
Aadu Putkodi Yaadhi Moorththik Kadimai Puguvathuve. 4.10.7

Pukku Adimaiyinaal Thannaik Kanda
Maarkkandeyan Avanai
Nakkapiraanum Anru Uyakkondadhu
Naaraayanan Arule
Kokku Alar Thadam Thaazhai Velith
Thirukkurugoor Adhanul
Mikka Aadhippiraan Nirka Marraith
Theyvam Vilambudhire

Vilambum Aaru Samaya
MumA Vai Yaagiyum Marrumthanpaal,
Alanthu Kaandar Kariya
Nnaagiya Aadhippi Raanamarum,
Valangol Thanbanai Soozhnthazha
Kaaya Thirukkuru Gooradhanai,
Ulangol Nyaanaththu Vaimmin
Ummai Uyyakkondu Pogurile. 4.10.8

Uruva Thaava Theththevum
Evvulaga Gangalum Marrumthanpaal,
Maruvil Moorththiyo Doththith
Thanaiyum Ninravan Namnnirkave,
Seruvil SenNel Karumbo
Dongu Thirukkuru Gooradhanul
Kuriya Maanuru Vaagiya
Neelkudak Kooththanuk Kaatseyvadhe. 4.10.9

Aatseydha Thaazhippi Raanaich
Chernthavan Vankuru Goornnagaraan
Naatka Mazhmagizh Maalai
Maarbinan Maaran Sadagoban,
Vetkai Yaalsonna Paadal
Aayirath Thulippath Thumvallaar,
Meetchi Yinri Vaigundha
Maannagar Marrathu Kaiyadhuve. (2) 4.10.10

Aindhaam Paththu

'Kaiyaar Sakkaraththenkarumaanikka Me!'Enrenru,
Poyye Kaimmaisollippuramepura Meyaadi,
Meyye Perrozhindhen, Vidhivaaykkinru Kaappaaraar,
Aiyo Kannapiraan! Araiyo Inipponaale. (2) 5.1.1

'Ponaay Maamarudhin Naduveyenpol Laamaniye,
Thene! Innamudhe!'Enrenresila Koorruchcholla,
Thaane Lemperumaanavanennaa Giyozhindhaan,
Vaane Maannilamemarrumurrumen Nnullanave. 5.1.2

Ullana Marrulavaappuramesila Maayancholli,
Vallal Manivannane! Enrenreyunai Yumvanchikkum,
Kallama Nnamthavirndheyunaikkandukon Duyndhozhindhen,
Vellath Thanaikkidandhaayiniyunnaivit Tenkolvane? 5.1.3

Ennkolva Nnunnaivitten
Nnumvaasagang Galsolliyum,
Vanngalva Nnenmanaththai
Valiththukkanna Neer Karandhu,
Ninnkan Nnerungavaiththe
Enndhaaviyai Neekkagillen,
Ennkan Malinamaruth
Thennaikkoovi Yarulaaykannane! 5.1.4

Kannapi Raanaivinnor
Karumaanikkath Thaiyamudhai,
Nanniyum Nannagillen
Naduveyo Rudambilittu,
Thinna Mazhundhakkattip
Palaseyvinai Vannkayirraal,
Punnai Maraiyavarinn
Thenaipporavaith Thaaypurame. 5.1.5

Puramarak Kattikkondiru
Valvinai Yaargumaikkum,
Muraimurai Yaakkaipugalozhiyak
Kandu Kondozhindhen,
Niramudai Naalthadandhol
Seyyavaayseyya Thaamaraikkan,
Aramuya Laazhiyangaik
Karumeniyam MaanDhannaiye. 5.1.6

Ammaa Nnaazhippiraanavanevvidath Thaan?Yaanaar?,
Emmaa Paaviyarkkumvidhivaaykkinru Vaaykkumkandeer,
'Kaimmaa Thunpozhiththaay!'Enrukaithalai Poosalitte,
Meymmaa Laayozhindhennempiraanumen Melaane. 5.1.7

Melaath Thevargalum Nilaththevarum Meviththozhum,
Maalaar Vandhinannaal Adiyenmanaththe Manninaar,
Seley Kanniyarum Perunchelvamum Nanmakkalum,
Melaath Thaaythandhaiyum Avareyini Yaavaare. 5.1.8

Aavaa RaarThunaiyenralainneerkkada Lulazhundhum
Naavaay Pol,Piravik Kadalulnninru Naanndhulanga,
Thevaar Kolaththodum Thiruchchakkaram Sanginodum,
Aavaa Venrarul Seydhadiyenodu Maanaane. 5.1.9

Aanaan Aaludaiyaannenraqdhekon Dugandhuvandhu,
Thaane Yinnarulseythennaimurravum Thaanaanaan,
Meenaa Yaamaiyumaay Narasingamu Maaykkuralaay,
Kaanaa Renaamumaayk Karkiyaaminnam Kaarvannane. 5.1.10

Kaarvannan Kannapiraan Kamalaththadang KannanDhannai,

Maasaru Sothiyen Seyya Vaaymanik Kunraththai

Esaru Mooravar Kavvai Thozhee! Enseyyume? (2) 5.3.1

Enseyyu Mooravar Kavvai Thozhee! Ininnammai,

Iraikkum Karungadal Vannan KannapiraanDhannai,

'Neerenne?' Ennaathe Neeliravum Thunchuvaraal,

Pinnninra Kaadhalnnoy Nencham Perithadumaal,
