Ilaiyaa Thunathaal Orungap Pitiththu
Potha Isainneeye. 5.8.8

Isaivith Thennai Yunndhaal Inaikeezh
Iruththum Ammaane,
Asaivil Amarar Thalaivar Thalaivaa
Aadhi Perumoorththi,
Thisaivil Veesum Sezhumaa Manigal
Serum Thirukkutandhai,
Asaivil Ulagam Paravak Kitandhaay!
Kaana Vaaraaye. 5.8.9

Vaaraa Varuvaay Varumen Maayaa! Maayaa Moorththiyaay,
Aaraa Amuthaay Adiyen Aavi Agame Thiththippaay,
Theeraa Vinaigal Theera Ennai Aantaay! Thirukkutandhai
Ooraay!Unakkaatpattum Adiyen Innam Uzhalveno? 5.8.10

Uzhalai Yenpin Peychchi Mulaiyoodu
Avalai Yuyiruntaan,
Kazhalkal Avaiye Saranaak Konta
Kurukoorch Chatagopan,
Kuzhalil Maliyach Sonna Oraayiraththul Ippaththum
Mazhalai Theera Vallaar Kaamar Maaney Nokkiyarkke. 5.8.11

Maaney Nokkunnalleer! Vaigalumvinai Yenmeliya,
Vaanaar Vankamugum Mathumalligai Yungamazhum,
Thenaar Solaigalsoozh Thiruvalla Vaazhuraiyum
Konaa Rai,Adiyen Adikootuva Thenrukolo? 5.9.1

Enrukol Thozhimeergaalemmainneernnalinn Thenseytheero?
Ponnthigazh Punnaimagizh Puthumaathavi Meethanavi,
Thenral Manangamazhum Thiruvalla Vaazhnnagarul
Ninrapi Raan,Adinnee Radiyongontu Sootuvathe? 5.9.2

Sootum Malarkkuzhaleer! Thuyaraattiye Nnaimeliya,
Paadunnal Vethavoli Paravaiththirai Polmuzhanga,
Maaduyarnn Thomappugai Kamazhumthan Thiruvallavaazh
Needurai Kinrapiraan Kazhalkantungol Nichchalume? 5.9.3

Nichchalum Thozhimeergaal! Emmainneernnalinn Thenseytheero?
Pachchilai Neelkamugum Palavumthengum Vaazhaikalum,
Machchani Maatangalmee Thanavumthan Thiruvallavaazh
Nachchara Vinanaimel Nampiraanathu Nannalame. 5.9.4

Nannalath Thozimeergaal! Nallavandhanar Velvippugai,
Mainnnnalang Kontuyarvin Maraikkumthan Thiruvallavaazh,
Kannalang Kattithannaik Kaniyaiyin Nnamuthandhannai,
Ennalang Kolsutarai Enrukolkankal Kaanpathuve? 5.9.5

Kaanpatheny Nyaanrukolo Vinaiyennkani Vaaymataveer,
Paankural Vantinotu Pasundhenralu Maagiyengum,
Sensinai Yongumarach Sezhungaanal Thiruvallavaazh,
Maankural Kolappiraan Malarththaamaraip Paathangale? 5.9.6

Paathangal Melanipooth Thozhakkootungol Paavainnalleer,
Othanne Tundhataththul UyarThaamarai Sengazhunneer,
Maathargal Vaanmugamum Kannumendhum Thiruvallavaazh,
Naathaniny Nyaalamunta NampiraanDhannai Naatorume? 5.9.7

Naadorum Veedinriye Thozhakkootungol Nannuthaleer,
Aaduru Theengarumpum Vilaisennnnelu Maagiyengum,
Maaduru Poondhatancher Vayalsoozhthan Thiruvallavaazh,
Needurai Kinrapiraan Nilandhaaviya Neelkazhale? 5.9.8

Kazhalvalai Poorippayaam Kantukaithozhak Kootungolo,
Kuzhalenna Yaazhumennak Kulirsolaiyul Thenarundhi,
Mazhalai Varivantugal Isaipaadum Thiruvallavaazh,
Suzhalin Malisakkarap Perumaanathu Thollarule? 5.9.9

Thollarul Nalvinaiyaal Sollakkootungol Thozhimeergaal,
Thollarul Mannumvinnum Thozhanninra Thirunnagaram,
Nallaru Laayiravar Nalanendhum Thiruvallavaazh,
Nallarul Namperumaan Naaraayanan Naamangale? 5.9.10

Naamanga Laayira Mutaiyannamperu Maanadimel,
Semangol Thennkurugoorchchatagopan Therindhuraiththa,
Naamanga Laayiraththul Ivaipaththum Thiruvallavaazh,
Semangol Thennagarmel Seppuvaarsirann ThaarPirandhe. 5.9.11

Pirandha Vaarum Valarndha Vaarum
Periya Baaratham Kaiseythu, Aivarkkuth
Thirangal Saatti Yittuch Seythu Pona Maayangalum,
Nirandha Nnootupuk Kenathaaviyai Ninrunninru
Urukki Yunkinra,Ich
Chirandha Vaansuta Re!Unnai Yenrukol Servathuve! 5.10.1

Vathuvai Vaarththaiyul Eru Paayndhathum
Maaya Maavinai Vaaypi Landhathum
Mathuvaivaar Kuzhalaar Kuravai Pinaindha Kuzhagum,
Athuvithu Uthuvenna Laavana Valla
Ennaiyun Seygai Naivikkum,
Muthuvaiya Muthalvaa!Unnai Yenru Thalaip Peyvane? 5.10.2

Peyyum Poonguzhal Peymulai Yunta
Pillaith Therramum, Perndhor Saadirach
Seyya Paathamon Raalseytha Ninsiruch Sevagamum,
Neyyun Vaarththaiyul, Annai Kolkolla
Neeyun Thaamaraik Kankal Neermalga,
Paiyave Nilaiyum Vandhen Nnenchai Yurukkungale. 5.10.3

Kalla Vetaththaik Kontupoyp Purampukka
Vaarum, Kalandhasurarai
Ullam Pethamsey Thittuyi Runta Upaayangalum,
Vella Neerchchatai Yaanum Ninnitai Veralaamai
Vilanga Ninrathum,
Ullamul Kutaindhen Uyirai Yurukki Yunnume. 5.10.4

Unna Vaanavar Konuk Kaayar
Oruppa Tuththa Adisi Luntathum,
Vannamaal Varaiyai Yeduththu Mazhaikaaththathum,
Mannai Munpataith Thuntu Mizhndhuka Tandhi Tandhu
Manandha Maayangal,
Ennunn Thorumen Nnenyseri Vaay
Mezhu Kokkunninre. 5.10.5

Ninra Vaaru Mirundha Vaarum
Kitandha Vaarum Ninaippariyana
Onralaa Vuruvaay Aruvaayannin Maayangal,
Ninru Ninru Ninaikkin Renunnai
Engnga Nnamnninai Kirpan, Paaviyerku
Onrunnan Kuraiyaay Ulaga Munta Onsutare! 5.10.6

Onsutaro Tirulumaay Ninra Vaarum
Unmaiyo Tinmaiyaay Vandhu,En
Kanko Laavagai Neegarann Thennaich Cheykinrana,
Enkol Sindhaiyul Naikinrenen Kariya
Maanikka Me!En Kankatkuth
Thinkolla Vorunnaal Arulaayun Thiruvuruve. 5.10.7

Thiruvuruvu Kitandha Vaarum Koppoozhch
Sendhaa Maraimel, Thisaimugan
Karuvulveer Rirundhu Pataiththitta Karumangalum,
Poruvi Lundhani Naayagamavai Ketkunn
Thorumen Nnencham Ninru Nekku,
Aruvi Sorum Kannee Renseygen Adiyene! 5.10.8

Adiyai Moonrai Yirandha Vaarum Angenninraam
Katalum Mannum Vinnum
Mudiya, Eeradiyaal Mudiththuk Konta Mukkiyamum,
Notiyu Maaravai Ketkunn Thorumen
Nencham NinDhanak Keka Raindhugum,
Kotiyaval Vinaiyen Unnai Yenrukol Kootuvathe? 5.10.9

Kooti Neerai Kataindha Vaarum
Amutham Thevar Unna, Asurarai
Veedum Vannanga Leseythu Pona Viththagamum,
Ootu Pukkena Dhaaviyai Yurukki
Yuntitu Kinra, NinDhannai
Naadum Vannam Sollaay Nachchunnaa Ganaiyaane! 5.10.10

Naaganaimisai Nampiraan Sarane
Saran Nnamak Kenru, Naadorum
Ega Sindhaiya Nnaaykkuru Koorchchata Gopan Maaran,
Aaga Noorra Ann Thaathi Yaayiraththul
Ivaiyumor Paththum Vallaar,
Maaga Vaikundhaththu Magizhveythuvar Vaigalume. 5.10.11


Aaraam Paththu

Vaigalpoong Kazhivaay Vandhu Meyum Kuruginangaal,
Seykol Senne Luyarthiruvanvan Tooruraiyum,
Kaikol Sakkarath Thennkani Vaayperu Maanaikkandu,
Kaigal Kooppich Solleer Vinaiyaattiyen Kaadhanmaiye. 6.1.1

Kaadhal Menpedai Yodudan Meyum Karunnaaraay,
Vedha Velvi Yolimuzhangum Than Tiruvanvandoor,
Naadhan Nyaalamel Laamunda Namperu Maanaikkandu,
Paadham Kaithozhudhu Paniyee Radiyen Thirame. 6.1.2

Thiranga Laakiyeng Kumseygalootuzhal Pullinangaal,
Sirandha Selvam Malgu Thiruvanvan Tooruraiyum,
Karangu Sakkarak Kaikkani Vaaypperu Maanaikkandu,
Irangi Neerthozhudhu Paniyeeradiye Nnidare. 6.1.3

Idaril Pogam Moozhgi Yinaindhaatum Madavannangaal,
Vidalil Vedha Volimuzhangumthan Thiruvanvandoor,
Kadalil Menip Piraannkan Nanainnetu Maalaikkandu,
`Udalam Naindhoruth Thiyuru Gum' En Runarththumine. 6.1.4

Unarththa Loota Lunarndhudan Meyum Madavannangaal,
Thinarththa Vandalkal Melsangu Serum Thiruvanvandoor,
Punarththa Poondhan Tuzhaaymudi Namperu Maanaikkandu,
Punarththa Kaiyinaraa Yadiyenukkum Porrumine. 6.1.5

Porriyaan Irann Thenpunnai Melurai Poonguyilgaal,
Serril Vaalai Thullum Thiruvanvan Tooruraiyum,
Aarra Laazhiyang Kaiyama Rarperu Maanaikkandu,
Maarrang Kondaru Leermaiyal Theerva Thoruvanname. 6.1.6

Oruvan Namsenru Pukkenakku
Onrurai Yonkiliye,
Seruvon Poompozhil Soozhsekkar
Velai Thiruvanvandoor,
Karuvannam Seyyavaay Seyyakan
Seyyakai Seyyakaal,
Seruvon Sakkaram Sangu
Adaiyaalam Thirundhak Kande. 6.1.7

Thirundhak Kandenak Konrurai
Yaayon Sirupoovaay.
Serundhi Nyaazhal Makizhpunnai
Soozhthan Tiruvanvandoor,
Perundhan Thaamaraik Kanperu
Neenmudi Naalthadandhol,
Karundhin Maamugil Polthiru
Meni Yadigalaiye. 6.1.8

Adigal Kaithozhu Thalarmel
Asaiyum Annangaal,
Vidivai Sangolik Kumthiru
Vanvan Tooruraiyum,
Kadiya Maayanthan Nnaikkannanai
Nedu Maalaikkandu,
Kodiya Valvinai Yenthiram
Koorumin Verukonde. 6.1.9

Veru Kondummai Yaanirann
Thenveri Vandinangaal,
Theru Neerppam Paivada
Paalaith Thiruvanvandoor,
Maaril Porarak Kanmathil
Neerezhach Serrugandha,
Erusevaga Nnaarkkennai
Yumulal Enminnkale. 6.1.10

Minnkol Serpuri Noolkura
Laayagal Nyaalamkonda,
Vannkal Vanadi Melkuru
Koorchchada Gopansonna,
Pankol Aayirath Thullivai
Paththum Thiruvanvandoorkku,
Innkol Paadal Vallaar
Madhanarmin Nnidaiyavarkke. 6.1.11

Minnidai Madavaargal Ninnarul Sootuvaar
Munpunnaa Nnadhanchuvan,
Mannudai Ilangai Yarankaayndha Maayavane,
Unnudaiya Sundaayam Naanarivan Nninniyathu
Kondu Seyvathen,
Ennudaiya Pandhum Suzhalum Thandhu Pogu Nampi! 6.2.1

Pogunnam Pee!Unthaamarai Puraikan Ninaiyum
Sevvaay Muruvalum,
Aagulangal Seyya Azhitharke Norro Meyaam?,
Thogaimaa Mayilaargal Ninnarul Sootuvaar
Seviyosai Vaiththezha,
Aagal Pogavittup Kuzhaloothu Poyirunthe. 6.2.2

Poyi Rundhumnnin Pulluvam Ariyaadha
Varkkurai Nampi, Ninseyya
Vaayirung Kaniyung Kangalum Vipareetha Minnaal,
Veyi Rundhadann Tholinaa Riththiru
Varulperu Vaaryavar Kol
Maayirung Kadalaik Kadaindha Perumaanaale? 6.2.3

Aali Nneelilai Yezhulaga Mundanru Neekidann
Thaay,Un Maayangal
Melai Vaanavaru Mariyaa Riniyem Parame?
Veli Nnerthadang Kanninaar Vilaiyaatu
Soozhalaich Choozhave Ninru
Kaali Meykkaval Laay!Emmainnee Kazharele. 6.2.4

Kazharel Nampee!Un Kaithavam Mannum Vinnum
Nannkariyum, Thinsakkara
Neezharu Tholpadai Yaay!Unak Konrunarth Thuvan Naan,
Mazharu Thenmozhi Yaargal Ninnarul
Sootuvaar Manam Vaadi Nirka,Em
Kuzharu Poovaiyodum Kiliyodum Kuzhakele. 6.2.5

Kuzhaki Yengal Kuzhamanan Kondu
Koyinmai Seythu Kanmamon Rillai,
Pazhaki Yaamirup Pompara Meyith Thiruvarulkal?,
Azhagi Yaariv Vulagumoon Rukkum
Thevithamai Thaguvaar Palarular,
Kazhaga Merel Nampee!Unakkum Ilaithe Kanmame. 6.2.6

Kanmaman Rengal Kaiyil Paavai Parippathu
Kadalnyaa Munditta,
Ninmalaa! Nediyaay! Unakkelum Pizhaipizhaiye,
Vanmame Solli Yemmainnee Vilaiyaatuthi
Athuketkil Ennaimaar,
Thanma Paavamen Nnaaroru Naanru Thadipinakke. 6.2.7

Pinakki Yaavaiyum Yaavarum Pizhaiyaamal
Pethiththum Pethi Yaadhathu,Or
Kanakkil Keerththi Vellak Kathirnyaana Moorththiyinaay,
Inakki Yemmaiyenn Thozhimaar `Vilaiyaadap
Pothumin' Ena Pondhomai,
Unakki Neevalaith Thaalensol Laaruga Vaadhavare? 6.2.8

Ugavaiyaal Nencham Ullurugi
Unthaamaraith Thadangan Vizhikalin,
Agavalaip Patuppaan Azhiththaayun Thiruvadiyaal,
Thagavu Seythilai Engal Sirrilum Yaamatu
Sirusorung Kandu,Nnin
Mugavoli Thigazha Muruval Seythu Ninrilaiye. 6.2.9

Ninrilangu Mudiyinaay! Irupath Thor Kaal
Arasu Kalai Katta,
Venri Neenmazhuvaa! Viyannyaalam Munpadaiththaay,
Inriv Vaayar Kulaththai Veeduyyath
Thonriya Karumaa Nikkachchudar,
Nindhannaal Nalive Patuvo Menrum Aaychchi Yome. 6.2.10

Aaychchi Yaagiya Annaiyaal Anru Venney
Vaarththaiyul, Seerra Mundazhu
Kooththa Appan Dhannaik Kurukoorch Chadagopan,
Eththiya Thamizhmaalai Yaayiraththul Ivaiyu
Morpath Thisaiyodum,
Naaththannaal Navila Vuraippaark Killai Nalgurave. 6.2.11

Nalkuravum Selvum Narakum Suvarkkamumaay,
Velpagaiyum Natpum Vidamum Amuthamumaay,
Palvagaiyum Parandhaperu Maanennai Yaalvaanai,
Selvammalgu Kudiththiru Vinnagark Kandene. 6.3.1

Kandavinpam Thunpam Kalakkangalum Therra Mumaay,
Thandamum Thanmaiyum Thazhalum Nizhalumaay,
Kanduko Tarkariya Perumaanennai Yaalvaanoor,
Thendiraip Punalsoozh Thiruvinnagar Nannagare. 6.3.2

Nagaramum Naatugalum Nyaanamum Mootamumaay,
Nigarilsoozh Sudaraayiru Laaynnila Nnaayvisumpaay,
Sigaramaa Tangalsoozh Thiruvinnagarch Cherndhapiraan,
Pugargol Keerththiyallaalillai Yaavarkkum Punniyame. 6.3.3

Punniyam Paavam
Punarchchipiri Venrivaiyaay
Ennamaay Marappaay Unmaiyaay
Inmayaayallanaay,
Thinnamaa Tangalsoozh
Thiruvinnagarch Cherndhapiraan,
Kannanin Nnarulekandu
Konminngal Kaithavame. 6.3.4

Kaithavam Semmai
Karumai Velumaiyumaay,
Meypoy Yilamai
Mudhumaipudhumai Pazhamaiyumaay,
Seyyathin Mathilsoozh
Thiruvinnagarch Cherndhapiraan,
Peythagaavu Kandeer
Perundhevudai Moovulage. 6.3.5

Moovulagang Galumaay
Allanaayugap Paaymunivaay,
Poovilvaazh Magalaayth
Thavvaiyaayppu Zhaaypazhiyaay,
Thevarme Viththezhum
Thiruvinnagarch Cherndhapiraan,
Paaviyen Manaththe
Yuraikinra Paranchudare. 6.3.6

Paranchudar Udampaay
Azhukkupathiththa Vudampaay,
Karandhumthon Riyumnninrum
Kaithavangal Seyyum,Vinnor
Sirangalaal Vanangum
Thiruvinnagarch Cherndhapiraan,
Varangolpaadha Mallaalillai
Yaavarkkum Vansarane. 6.3.7

Vansaran Surarkkaay
Asurarkkuveng Koorramumaay,
Thansaran Nizharkee
Zhulagamvaiththum Vaiyaathum,
Thensaran Thisaikkuth
Thiruvinnagarch Cherndhapiraan,
Ensaranen Kannan
Ennaiyaaludai Ennappane. 6.3.8

Ennappan Enakkaayikulaay
Ennaip Perravalaay,
Ponnappan Maniyappan
Muththappanen Appanumaay,
Minnappon Mathilsoozhthiru
Vinnagarch Cherndhavappan,
Thannoppaa Rillappan
Thandhanannthana Thaalnnizhale. 6.3.9

Nizhalveyil Sirumaiperumai
Kurumai Nedumaiyumaay,
Suzhalvanannir Panamarru
Maayavai Allanumaay,
Mazhalaivaazh Vanduvaazh
Thiruvinnagar Mannupiraan,
Kazhalgalanri Marror
Kalaikanilam Kaanminngale. 6.3.10

`Kaanminnga Lulageer!' Enru
Kanmugap Pennimirndha,
Thaalinaiyan Dhannaik Kurugoorch
Sadagopan Sonna,
Aanaiyaa Yiraththuththiru
Vinnagarppath Thumvallaar,
Konaiyinri Vinnork
Konrumaavar Kuravargale. 6.3.11

Nallavalathhaal Nammai Serndhon Mun Nannaarai
Vellum Viruththa Viboothiyenenru
Ellaiaraththaan Irundhu Vaazhththum Thamizhmaaran
Sol Vallaar Vaanavarkku Vaayththakuravar. .Seeyar.

Kuravai Yaaychchiya Rodu Koththathum
Kunramon Rendhiyathum
Uravunneerp Poygai Naagam Kaayndhathum
Utpada Marrumpala,
Aravil Pallip Piraanthan Maaya
Vinaikalai Yeyalarri,
Iravum Nanpaga Lumtha Virgilam
Enna Kuraivenakke? 6.4.1

Keyath Theenguzha Loothirrum Niraimeyththa
Thum,Kendai Yonkan
Vaasap Poonguzhal Pinnai Tholgal
Manandhathum Marrumpala,
Maayak Kolap Piraandhan Seygai
Ninaindhu Manamkuzhaindhu,
Neyath Thodu Kazhindha Pothenaku
Evvula Gamnnigare? 6.4.2

Nigaril Mallaraich Serra Thumnnirai
Meyththathum Neenedungaich,
Chigara Maakali Rattathum Ivai
Polvanavum Piravum,
Pugar Kol Sothip Piraandhan Seygai
Ninaindhu Pulampi,Enrum
Nugar Vaigal Vaigapper Ren Enakku
Eni Nni Novathuve? 6.4.3

Nova Aaychchi Yuralo Taarkka
Irangirrum Vanchappennaich,
Chaavap Paalun Tathumoo R Chagadam
Irachchaa Tiyathum,
Thevak Kola Piraandhan Seygai
Ninaindhu Manamkuzhaindhu,
Mevak Kaalangal Koodi Nnene Nnakku
Eni Nni Venduvathe? 6.4.4

Vendi Theva Rirakka Vandhu
Pirandhathum Veengirulvaay,
Poondu Anrannai Pulampap Poyangor
Aaykkulam Pukkathum,
Kaanda Linri Valarndhu Kanchanaith
Thunchavany Chamseythathum,
Eendu Naana Lar Rapper Rene Nnakku
Enna Igalulathe? 6.4.5

Igalkol Pullai Pilandha Thumi Mil
Erugal Serrathuvum,
Uyargol Solaik Kurundho Siththathum
Utpada Marrumpala,
Agalkol Vaiyam Alandha Maayanen
Appandhan Maayangale,
Pagaliraap Paravap Perren Enakkenna
Manappa Rippe? 6.4.6

Manappari Pota Zhukku Maanida
Saathiyil Thaanpirandhu,
Thanakku Venduruk Kondu Thaan Thana
Seerraththinai Mudikkum,
Punaththu Zhaaymudi Maalai Maarbanen
Appandhan Maayangale,
Ninaikkum Nenchudai Yene Nnakkini
Yaarnnigar Neenilaththe? 6.4.7

Neenilath Thotuvaan Viyappa Niraiperum
Porgal Seythu,
Vaana Nnaayiram Tholthu Niththathum
Utpada Marrumpala,
Maani Yaaynnilam Konda Maayanen
Appandhan Maayangale,
Kaanum Nenchudai Yenenak Kiniyena
Kalakka Munde? 6.4.8

Kalakka Vezhkada Lezhmalai Yulage
Zhumkazhi Yakkadaay,
Ulakkath Ther Kotu Senra Maayamum
Utpada Marrumpala,
Valakkai Yaazhi Yidakkai Sangam
Ivaiyudai Maalvannanai,
Malakkunnaa Vudaiyergu Maarula Thovim
Mannin Misaiye? 6.4.9

Manmisaip Perumpaaram Neengavorpaaradha
Maape Rumpor,
Panni, Maayangal Seythu, Senaiyaip
Paazhpada Noorrittuppoy,
Vinmi Saiththana Thaama Mepuga
Meviya Sothithannthaal,
Nanni Naanvanang Gapper Rene Nnak
Kaarpirar Naayagare? 6.4.10

Naaya Ganmuzhu Vezhula Gukkumaay
Muzhuve Zhulagum,Than
Vaaya Gampuga Vaiththumizhnn Thavaiyaay
Avaiyal Lanumaam,
Kesavan Adiyinai Misaikkuru Koorchchada
Gopan Sonna
Thooya Vaayirath Thippaththaal
Paththaraavar Thuvalinriye. 6.4.11

Thuvalil Maamani Maada Mongu
Tholaivil Limanga Lamthozhum
Ivalai, Neerini Yannai Meer!Umak
Kaasai Yillai Vitumino,
Thavala Vonsangu Sakka Ramenrum
Thaama Raiththadang Kanenrum,
Kuvalai Yonmalark Kangal Neermalga
Ninru Ninru Kumurume. 6.5.1

Kumuru Mosai Vizhavo Liththolai
Villi Mangalam Kondupukku,
Amutha Menmozhi Yaalai Neerumak
Kaasai Yinri Agarrineer,
Thimirkgon Taaloththu Nirkum Marrival
Theva Thevapi Raanenre,
Nimiyum Vaayotu Kangal Neermalga
Nekko Sindhu Karaiyume. 6.5.2

Karaikol Paimpozhil Thanpa Naiththolai
Villi Mangalam Kondupukku,
Uraiko Linmozhi Yaalai Neerumak
Kaasai Yinri Agarrineer,
Thiraikol Pelavaththu Serndha Thumthisai
Nyaalam Thaavi Yalandhathum,
Niraigal Meyththathu Mepi Tharri
Nedungan Neermalga Nirkume. 6.5.3

Nirkum Naanmarai Vaanar Vaazhtholai
Villi Mangalang Kandapin,
Arga Monrum Arivu Raalmalinn
Thaalkan Teerival Annaimeer,
Karkum Kalviyel Laamka Rungadal
Vannan Kannapi Raanenre,
Orga Monrumi Lalugandhukandhu
Ulmagizhndhu Kuzhaiyume. 6.5.4

Kuzhaiyum Vaalmugath Thezhai Yaiththolai
Villi Mangalam Kondupukku,
Izhaikol Sothichchenn Thaama Raikkan
Piraani Rundhamai Kaattineer,
Mazhaipey Thaalokkum Kanna Neerinodu
Anru Thottummai Yaandhu,Ival
Nuzhaiyum Sindhaiyal Annai Meer!Thozhum
Aththi Saiyurru Nokkiye. 6.5.5

Nokkum Pakkamel Laamka Rumpotu
Senne Longusenn Thaamarai,
Vaaykkum Thanporu Nalva Tagarai
Vandho Laivilli Mangalam,
Nokku Mela Th Thisaiyal Laalmaru
Nokki Lalvaigal Naaldhorum,
Vaaykkol Vaasaga Mumma Nivannan
Naama Meyival Annaimeer! 6.5.6

Annai Meer!Ani Maama Yilsiru
Maani Valnnammaik Kaivalindhu,
Enna Vaarththaiyum Ketku Raaltholai
Villi Mangalam Enrallaal,
Munnam Norra Vithiko Lomugil
Vannan Maayango Lo,Avan
Chinna Mumthiru Naama Mumival
Vaaya Nnakalthi Rundhave. 6.5.7

Thirundhu Vedhamum Velvi Yumthiru
Maama Kalirum Thaam,Malinn,
Thirundhu Vaazhporu Nalva Takarai
Vandho Laivilli Mangalam,
Karundha Tanganni Kaitho Zhuthaa Nn
Naaltho Tangiyinn Naaldhorum,
Irundhi Rundhu 'Ara Vindha Losana!'
Enren Rennaindhi Rangume. 6.5.8

Irangi Naaldhorum Vaayve Reei Yival
Kanna Neergal Alamara,
Maranga Lumirang Guva Gai`Mani
Vanna Vo!'Enru Koovumaal,
Thurangam Vaaypilann Thaanu Raitholai
Villi Mangala Menru,Than
Karangal Kooppith Thozhumav Voorththiru
Naamang Karradhar Pinnaiye. 6.5.9

Pinnai Kolnnila Maama Galkol?
Thiruma Galkol? Pirandhittaal,
Enna Maayango Lo?I Valnnedu
Maalen Renninru Koovumaal,
Munni Vandhavan Ninri Rundhurai
Yumtho Laivilli Mangalam
Senni Yaalvanang Guma V Voorththiru
Naamam Ketpathu Sindhaiye. 6.5.10

Sindhai Yaalumsol Laalum Seygaiyinaalum
Theva Piraanaiye,
Thandhai Thaayen Radaindha Vankuru
Koora Varsada Gopansol,
Mundhai Yaayirath Thulli Vaitholai
Villi Mangalath Thaichchonna,
Sendhamizhpaththum Vallaaradimai
Sey Vaarthiru Maalukke. 6.5.11

Maalukku Vaiyam Alandha Manaalarku,
Neelak Karunnira Mega Niyaayarku,
Kolachchenn Thaamaraik Kannarku,En Kongalar
Elak Kuzhali Yizhandhathu Sange. 6.6.1

Sanguvil Vaalthandu Sakkarak Kaiyarku,
Sengani Vaaychcheyya Thaamarai Kannarku,
Kongalar Thannann Thuzhaaymudi Yaanukku,En
Mangai Yizhandhathu Maamai Nirame. 6.6.2

Nirangari Yaanukku Needula Gunda,
Thiramkilar Vaaychchiru Kalla Nnavarku,
Karangiya Sakkarak Kaiyava Nnukku,En
Pirangirung Koondhal Izhandhathu Peete. 6.6.3

Peedudai Naanmuga Nnaippadaith Thaanukku,
Maatudai Vaiyam Alandha Manaalarku,
Naatudai Mannarkkuth Thoothusel Nampikku,En
Paatudai Algul Izhandhathu Panpe. 6.6.4

Panpudai Vedham Payandha Paranukku,
Manpurai Vaiyam Idandha Varaagarku,
Thenpunal Palliyenn Thevap Piraanukku,En
Kanpunai Kothai Izhandhathu Karpe. 6.6.5

Karpagak Kaavana Narpala Tholarku,
Porchudark Kunranna Poondhan Mudiyarku,
Narpala Thaamarai Naanmalark Kaiyarku,En
Virpuru Vakkodi Thorrathu Meyye. 6.6.6

Meyyamar Palkalan Nannkaninn Thaanukku,
Paiyara Vinanaip Palliyi Nnaanukku,
Kaiyotu Kaalseyya Kanna Piraanukku,En
Thaiyal Izhandhathu Thannudaich Chaaye. 6.6.7

Saayak Kurundham Osiththa Thamiyarku,
Maayach Chagadam Uthaiththa Manaalarku,
Peyaip Pinampadap Paalun Piraanukku,En
Vaasak Kuzhali Izhandhathu Maanpe. 6.6.8

Maanpamai Kolaththem Maayak Kuralarku,
Chensudark Kunranna Senchudar Moorththikku,
Kaanperunn Thorraththeng Gaakuththa Nampikku,En
Poonpunai Menmulai Thorrathu Porpe. 6.6.9

Porpamai Neenmudip Poondhan Tuzhaayarku,
Marporu Tholudai Maayap Piraanukku,
Nirpana Palluru Vaaynnirku Maayarku,En
Karpudai Yaatti Yizhandhathu Katte. 6.6.10

Kattezhil Solainnal Vengada Vaananai,
Kattezhil Thenkuru Koorchchada Gopansol,
Kattezhil Aayirath Thippaththum Vallavar,
Kattezhil Vaanavar Pogamun Paare. 6.6.11

Unnuny Choru Parugunneer
Thinnumver Rilaiyumellaam
Kannan, Emperumaan Nnenren
Rekankal Neermalgi,
Manninul Avanseer Valammik
Kavanoor Vinavi,
Thinna Mennila Maanpugu
Moorthiruk Koloore. 6.7.1

Oorum Naatum Ulagum
Thannaippol, Avanudaiya
Perum Thaargalu Mepitharrak
Karpu Vaanidari,
Serunnal Valancher Pazhanath
Thiruko Loorkke,
Porung Kolurai Yeerkodi
Yennkodi Poovaigale! 6.7.2

Poovai Paingiligal Pandhu
Thoothaipoom Puttilkal,
Yaavaiyum Thirumaal Thirunnaamang
Kalekoovi Yezhum,En
Paavai Poyinith Thanpazhanath
Thirukko Loorkke,
Kovaivaay Thudippa Mazhaikkanno
Tensey Yungolo? 6.7.3

Kollai Yenparko Lokunam
Mikkanal Enparkolo,
Silalai Vaayppen Tukalayar
Seriyul Laarumelle,
Selvam Malgi Yavankidandha
Thirukko Loorkke,
Mellidai Nudanga Ilamaan
Sella Mevinale. 6.7.4

Mevi Naindhu Naindhuvilai
Yaadaluraa Lensiruth
Thevipoy, Iniththan
Thirumaal Thirukko Looril,
Pooviyal Pozhilum Thadamum
Avanko Yilungandu,
Aaviyul Kulira Engngane
Yugakkungol Inre? 6.7.5

Inrenak Kuthavaa Thaganra
Ilamaan Inippoy,
Thenthisaith Thiladha Manaiya
Thirukko Loorkke
Senru,Than Thirumaal Thirukkannum
Sevvaayum Kandu,
Ninru Ninru Naiyum
Nedungankal Panimalgave. 6.7.6

Malgunneer Kannodu Maiyalurra Manaththanalaay,
Allunnan Pagalum Nedumaalenrazhaith Thinippoy,
Selvam Malgi Avankidandha Thirukko Loorkke,
Olgi Yolgi Nadandhengngane Pugungo Losinthe? 6.7.7

Osindha Nunnidai Melkaiyai
Vaiththu Nondhunnondhu,
Kasindha Nenchina Laaykkanna
Neerththulumpach Chellungol,
Osindha Vonmala Raalkozhunnan
Thirukko Loorkke,
Kasindha Nenchina Laayemmai
Neeththae M Kaarigaiye? 6.7.8

Kaariyam Nallana Kalavai Kaanilen
Kannanukkenru,
Eeriyaa Yiruppaali Thellaam
Kidakka Inippoy,
Seri Palpazhi Thooyiraippath
Thirukko Loorkke,
Nerizhai Nadandhaa Lemmai
Yonrum Ninaiththilale. 6.7.9

Ninaikkilen Theyvangaal Nedungan
Ilamaan Inippoy,
Anaiththu Lagumu Taiya
Aravindha Losananai,
Thinaiththanai Yumvidaa Lavanser
Thirukko Loorkke,
Manaikku Vaanpazhiyum Ninaiyaal
Sella Vaiththanale. 6.7.10

Vaiththa Maannithi Yaammathu
Soothanai Yeyalarri,
Koththa Larpozhil Soozhkuru
Koorchchada Gopansonna,
Paththu Nooru Lippath
Thavanser Thirukkoloorkke,
Siththam Vaiththu Raippaar
Thigazhpon Nnulagaalvaare. 6.7.11

Ponnula Gaaleero? Puvanimuzhu Thaaleero?,
Nannalap Pullinangaal! Vinaiyaattiyennaanirandhen,
Munnula Kangalellaam Padaiththamugilvannankannan,
Ennalang Kondapiraan Dhanakken Nilaimaiyuraiththe? 6.8.1

Maiyamar Vaalnnedungan Mangaimaarmunpen Kaiyirundhu,
Neyyama Rinnadisil Nichchalpaalodu Meveero,
Kaiyamar Sakkaraththen Kanivaaypperu Maanaikkandu
Meyyamar Kaadhalsollik Kilikaal!Virainn Thotivandhe? 6.8.2

Otivann Thenkuzhalmel Olimaamala Rootheero,
Koodiya Vandinangaal! Kurunnaatudai Aivargatkaay
Aadiya Maannedundherp Padainneerezha Serrapiraan,
Soodiya Thandulava Mundathoomathu Vaaykalkonde? 6.8.3

Thoomathu Vaaykalkondu
Vandhenmullaikal Melthumpikaal,
Poomathu Vunnachchellil
Vinaiyenaip Poyseythaganra,
Maamathu Vaarthanduzhaay
Mudivaanavar Konaikkandu,
Yaamithu Vothakkavaa
Rennavendumkan Teernnungatke. 6.8.4

Nungatki Yaanuraikken
Vamminyaanvalarth Thakilikaal,
Vengatpul Loorndhuvandhu
Vinaiyenainneny Chamkavarndha,
Sengat Karumugilaich
Cheyyavaaychchezhung Karpagaththai,
Enguchchen Raagilumkandu
Idhuvothakka Vaarenmine. 6.8.5

Enminnu Noolmaarva
Nnenkarumperu Maannenkannan,
Thanmannu Neelkazhalmel
Thanduzhaaynnamak Kanrinnalgaan,
Kanminnka Lenrummaiyaan
Karpiyaavaiththa Maarramsolli,
Senminnkal Theevinaiyen
Valarththasiru Poovaikale! 6.8.6

Poovaikal Polnniraththan
Pundareekangal Polumkannan,
Yaavaiyum Yaavarumaay
Ninramaayanen Aazhipiraan,
Maavaival Vaaypilandha
Mathusootharken Maarramsolli,
Paavaikal! Theerkkirrire
Vinaiyaattiyen Paasarave. 6.8.7

Paasara Veythiyinne
Vinaiyenenai Yoozhinnaiven?,
Aasaru Thoovivellaik
Kuruge!Arul Seyyorunnaal,
Maasaru Neelachchudar
Mudivaanavar Konaikkandu,
Esarum Nummaiyallaal
Marunnokkilal Perththumarre. 6.8.8

Perththumar Rorgalaikan
Vinaiyaattiyen Naanonrilen,
Neerththirai Melulavi
Yiraitherumpu Thaavinangaal,
Kaarththiral Maamugilpol
Kannanvinnavar Konaikkandu,
Vaarththaikal Kondaruli
Yuraiyeervaigal Vandhirundhe. 6.8.9

Vandhirunn Thummudaiya
Manichchevalum Neerumellaam,
Andhara Monruminri
Yalarmelasai Yumannangaal,
Enthiru Maarvarkennai
Yinnaavaarival Kaanminenru,
Mandhirath Thonrunarththi
Yuraiyeervaigal Marumaarrangale. 6.8.10

Maarranga Laayndhukondu
Mathusoothapi Raanadimel,
Naarrangol Poompozhilsoozh
Kurukoorchchada Gopansonna,
Thorranga Laayiraththul
Ivaiyumoru Paththumvallaar,
Oorrinkan Nunmanalpol
Urugaannirpar Neeraaye. 6.8.11

Neeraay Nilanaay Theeyaayk Kaalaay Neduvaanaay,
Seeraar Sudarka Lirandaaych Chivanaay Ayanaay,
Kooraar Aazhi Vensang Kendhik Kodiyenpaal
Vaaraay, Orunnaal Mannum Vinnum Makizhave. 6.9.1

Mannum Vinnum Makizhak Kuralaay Valangaatti,
Mannum Vinnum Konda Maaya Ammaane,
Nanni Yunainnaan Kandu Kandhu Kooththaada,
Nanni Yorunnaal Nyaalath Thoote Nadavaaye. 6.9.2

Nyaalath Thoote Nadandhum Ninrum Kidandhirundhum,
Saalap Palannaal Ugandho Ruyirgal Kaappaane,
Kolath Thirumaa Magalo Tunnaik Kootaathe,
Saalap Palannaal Adiyen Innam Thalarveno? 6.9.3

Thalarndhum Murindhum Sagada Vasurar Udalveraa,
Pilandhu Veeyath Thirukkaa Laanda Perumaane,
Kilarndhu Piraman Sivaninn Thiranvin Navarsoozha,
Vilanga Vorunnaal Kaana Vaaraay Vinmeethe. 6.9.4

Vinmeedhiruppaay! Malaimel Nirpaay! Kadalserppaay,
Manmeedhuzhalvaay! Ivarrulengum Maraindhuraivaay,
Enmeedhiyanra Puravandaththaay! Enadhaavi,
Unmeedhaadi Urukkaattaathe Yolippaayo? 6.9.5

Paayor Adivaith Thadhankeezhp Paravai Nilamellaam
Thaay,Or Adiyaay Ellaa Vulagum Thadavandha
Maayon, Unnaik Kaanpaan Varundhi Yenainnaalum,
Theeyodudanser Mezhugaay Ulagil Thiriveno? 6.9.6

Ulagil Thiriyum Karuma Gathiyaay Ulagamaay,
Ulaguk Keyo Ruyiru Maanaay Puravandaththu,
Alagil Polindha Thisaipath Thaaya Aruveyo,
Alagil Polindha Arivi Lenuk Karulaaye. 6.9.7

Arivi Lenuk Karulaay Arivaa Ruyiraanaay,
Verikol Sothi Moorththi! Adiyen Nedumaale,
Kirisey Thennaip Purathit Tinnam Keduppaayo,
Pirithon Rariyaa Adiye Nnaavi Thigaikkave? 6.9.8

Aavi Thigaikka Aivar Kumaikkum Sirrinpam,
Paavi Yenaip Palannee Kaattip Patuppaayo,
Thaavi Vaiyam Konda Thadandhaa Maraikatke,
Koovik Kollum Kaala Minnam Kurugaatho? 6.9.9

Kurugaa Neelaa Iruthi Kootaa Enaiyoozhi,
Sirugaa Perugaa Alavi Linpam Serndhaalum,
Marugaa Linri Maayo Nnunakke Yaalaagum,
Sirukaa Laththai Yurumo Andho Theriyile? 6.9.10

Therithal Ninaithal Ennal Aagaath Thirumaalukku,
Uriya Thondar Thondar Thondan Sadagopan,
Theriyach Chonna Oraa Yiraththu Lippaththum
Uriya Thonda Raakkum Ulagam Undaarke. 6.9.11

Ulagam Unda Peruvaayaa!
Ulappil Keerththi Yammaane,
Nilavum Sudarsoo Zholimoorththi!
Nediyaay! Adiye Nnaaruyire,
Thiladham Ulaguk Kaaynninra
Thiruveng Kadaththem Perumaane,
Kulathol Ladiyen Unpaadham
Kootu Maaru Kooraaye. 6.10.1

Kooraay Neeraay Nilanaakik
Kotuval Lasurar Kulamellaam
Seeraa Eriyum Thirunnemi
Valavaa! Theyvak Komaane,
Seraar Sunaiththaa Maraisendhee
Malarum Thiruveng Kadaththaane,
Aaraa Anpil Adiyenun
Adiser Vannam Arulaaye. 6.10.2

Vanna Marulkol Animega
Vannaa! Maaya Ammaane,
Ennam Pugundhu Thiththikkum
Amuthe! Imaiyor Athipathiye,
Thennal Aruvi Maniponmuth
Thalaikkum Thiruveng Kadaththaane,
Anna Le!Un Adisera
Adiyer Kaavaa Vennaaye! 6.10.3

Aavaa Vennaa Thulagaththai
Alaikkum Asurar Vaanaalmel,
Theevaay Vaali Mazhaipozhindha
Silaiyaa! Thirumaa Magalkelvaa,
Thevaa Surargal Munikkanangal
Virumpum Thiruveng Kadaththaane,
Poovaar Kazhalkal Aruvinaiyen
Porundhu Maaru Punaraaye. 6.10.4

Punaraa Ninra Maramezhan
Reytha Voruvil Valavaavo,
Punarey Ninra Maramirandin
Natuve Pona Muthalvaavo,
Thinaraar Megam Enakkaliru
Serum Thiruveng Kadaththaane,
Thinaraar Saarngath Thunpaadham
Serva Thadiye Nnennaale? 6.10.5

`Ennaa Lennaam Mannalandha
Inaiththaa Maraikal Kaanpadharke'nnru,
Ennaa Lumnnin Rimaiyorgal
Eththi Yirainchi Yinaminamaay,
Meynnaa Manaththaal Vazhipaatu
Seyyum Thiruveng Kadaththaane,
Meynnaa Nneythi Yennaalun
Adikkan Adiyen Mevuvathe? 6.10.6

Adiyen Mevi Yamarginra
Amuthe! Imaiyor Athipathiye,
Kodiyaa Atupul Ludaiyaane!
Kolak Kanivaayp Perumaane,
Sediyaar Vinaikal Theermarundhe!
Thiruveng Kadaththem Perumaane,
Nodiyaar Pozhudhum Unpaadham
Kaana Nolaa Thaarrene. 6.10.7

Nolaa Thaarren Nunpaadham
Kaana Venru Nunnunarvil,
Neelaar Kandath Thammaanum
Nirainnaan Muganu Mindhiranum,
Seley Kannaar Palarsoozha
Virumpum Thiruveng Kadaththaane,
Maalaay Mayakki Yadiyenpaal
Vandhaay Pola Vaaraaye. 6.10.8

Vandhaay Pole Vaaraadhaay!
Vaaraa Thaaypol Varuvaane,
Sendhaa Maraikkan Senganivaay
Naaltho Lamuthe! Enathuyire,
Sindhaa Manikal Pagarallaip
Pagalsey Thiruveng Kadaththaane,
Andho! Adiyen Unpaadham
Agala Killen Iraiyume. 6.10.9

`Agala Killen Iraiyum'en
Ralarmel Mangai Yuraimaarpaa,
Nigaril Pugazhaay! Ulagamoon
Rudaiyaay! Ennai Aalvaane,
Nigaril Amarar Munikkanangal
Virumpum Thiruveng Kadaththaane,
Pugalon Rillaa Adiyenun
Adikkee Zhamarndhu Pugundhene. 6.10.10

`Adikkee Zhamarndhu Pugundhadiyeer!
Vaazhmin' Enren Rarulkotukkum
Padikke Zhillaap Perumaanaip
Pazhanak Kurukoorch Chadagopan,
Mudippaan Sonna Aayiraththuth
Thiruveng Kadaththuk Kivaipaththum,
Pidiththaar Pidiththaar Veerrirundhu
Periya Vaanul Nilaavuvare. 6.10.11


Ezaam Paththu

Unni Laaviya Aiva Raalkumai
Theerri Yennaiyun Paadha Pangayam,
Nannilaa Vagaiye Nalivaa Nninna Mennu Kinraay,
Enni Laapperu Maayane! Imaiyorgal
Eththu Mulaga Moonrudai,
Anna Le!Amu The!Appa Nne!Ennai Yaalvaane! (2) 7.1.1

Ennai Yaalum Vango Vorainn Thivaipey
Thiraappagal Mothu Viththittu,
Unnai Naananu Kaavagai Cheydhu Pothi Kantaay,
Kanna Le!Amu The!Kaar Mukilvanna
Nne!Katal Nyaalam Kaakkinra,
Minnu Nemiyi Nnaay!Vinai Yenudai Vethiyane! 7.1.2

Vethiyaa Nirkum Aivaraal Vinaiyenai
Mothu Viththu,Un Thiruvadich
Chaathi Yaavagai Neethaduth Thenperu Thiyandho,
Aathi Yaagi Yagali Tampataith Thuntu Mizandhu
Katandhitann Thitta,
Chothi Neenmudi Yaay!Thonta Nnenmadhu Choothanane! 7.1.3

Choothu Naanari Yaavagai Chuzarriyor
Aivaraik Kaatti,Un Adip
Pothu Naananu Kaavagai Cheydhu Pothi Kantaay,
Yaadhum Yaavaru Minrinnin Nnagampaal
Otukkiyo Raali Nneelilai,
Meethu CherKuzavi! Vinaiyen Vinaitheer Marundhe! 7.1.4

Theermarunn Thinri Yaindhu Noyadum
Chekki Littuth Thirikkum Aivarai,
Nerma Rungudaith Thaavataiththu Nekizippaan
Okkinraay,
Aarma Rundhini Yaakuvar? Atalaazi
Yendhi Yachurar VanGulam,
Verma Rungaruth Thaay!Vinnu LaarPeru Maaneyo! 7.1.5

Vinnu LaarPeru Maarka Timaichey
Vaarai Yumcherum Aimpu Lanivai,
Mannu Lennaip Perraa Lenchey
Yaamarru Neeyumvittaal?
Pannu Laay!Kavi Thannu Laay!
Paththiyinul Laay!Para Meechane, Vandhen
Kannulaay! Nenchulaay! Chollulaay!
Onru Chollaaye. 7.1.6

Onru Cholli Oruththinil Nirkilaadha
Oraivar VanKayavarai,
Enru Yaanvel Kirpanun Thiruvaru Lillaiyel?,
Anru Thevar Achurar Vaanga
Alaikata Laravam Alaavi,Or
Kunram Vaiththa Endhaay!Kodiyen Parukin Nnamuthe! 7.1.7

Inna Muthenath Thonri Yoraivar
Yaavaraiyum Mayakka, Neevaiththa
Munna Maayamel Laalmuzu Verarindhu, Ennaiyun
Chinna Mumthiru Moorththiyum Chindhith Theththik
Kaithoza Veyaru Lenakku,
Ennam Maa!En Kannaa! Imaiyordham Kulamuthale! 7.1.8

Kulamutha Litumthee Vinaikkodu VanGuziyinil
Veezkkum Aivarai
Valamuthal Ketukkum Varame Thandharul Kantaay,
Nilamutha Liniev Vulakukkum Nirpana
Chelvana Ena,Porul
Palamuthal Pataiththaay!En Kannaa!En Paranchudare! 7.1.9

`Enparany Chudare!' Enrunnai Alarriyun
Inaiththaa Maraikatku,
Anpuruki Nirkum Adhunnirkach Chumadu Thandhaay,
Vanparanga LetuththuAivar Thichaithichai
Valiththerru Kinranar:
Munparavai Kataindhamuthang Konta Moorththiyo! 7.1.10

Konta Moorththiyor Moovaraayk Kunangal
Pataiththalith Thukketuk Kum,Ap
Punta Reekapkop Poozppunar Palli Yappanukke,
Thontar Thontar Thontar Thontan Chatakopan
Chollaa Yiraththu Lippaththum,
Kantu Paataval Laarvinai Pomkangu Lumpagale. (2) 7.1.11

Kangulum Pagalum Kan Thuyi Lariyaal
Kannanneer Kaikalaal Iraikkum,
Changuchak Karanga Lenrukai Kooppum
`Thaamaraik Kan' Enru Thalarum,
`Engngane Tharikke Nnunnaivittu' Ennum
Irunnilam Kaithuzaa Virukkum,
Chengayal Paaynneerth Thiruvarang Kaththaay!
Ivalthirath Thencheykin Raaye?' (2) 7.2.1

'Encheykin Raayen Thaamaraik Kannaa!
Ennumkan Neermalka Irukkum,
`Encheyke Nnerinneerth Thiruvarang Kaththaay?'
Ennumvev Vuyirththuyirth Thurukum:
`MunCheydha Vinaiye! Mukappataay' Ennum
`Mukilvannaa! Thakuvatho?' Ennum,
Muncheydhiv Vulagam Untumizann Thalandhaay!
Engolo Mudikinra Thivatke? 7.2.2

Vatkilal Iraiyum `Manivannaa!' Ennum
Vaaname Nokkummai Yaakkum,
`Utkudai Yachurar Uyirellaa Munta
Oruvane!' Ennumul Lurukum,
`Katkilee! Unnaik Kaanumaa Rarulaay
Kaakuththaa! Kannane!' Ennum,
Thitkodi Mathilchooz Thiruvarangaththaay!
Ivalthirath ThenCheydhit Taaye? 7.2.3

Ittagaal Itta Kaiyalaay Irukkum
Ezundhulaay Mayangumkai Kooppum,
`Kattame Kaadhal!' Enrumoorch Chikkum
`Katalvannaa! Kadiyaikaan' Ennum,
`Vattavaay Nemi Valangaiyaa!' Ennum
`Vandhitaay' Enrenre Mayangum,
Chittane! Chezunneerth Thiruvarang Kaththaay!
Ivalthirath Thenchindhith Thaaye? 7.2.4

Chindhikkum Thisaikkum Therumkai Kooppum
`Thiruvarang Kaththullaay!' Ennum
Vandhikkum, Aange Mazaikkanneer Malka
`Vandhitaay' Enrenre Mayangum,
Andhippo Thavunan Udalitann Thaane!
Alaikatal Kataindhavaa Ramuthe,
Chandhiththun Charanam Chaarvathe Valiththa
Thaiyalai Maiyalchey Thaane! 7.2.5

`Maiyalchey Thennai Manamkavarnn Thaane!'
Ennum`Maa Maayane!' Ennum,
`Cheyyavaay Maniye!' Ennum`Than Punalchooz
Thiruvarang Kaththullaay!' Ennum,
`Veyyavaal Thantu Changuchak Karamvil
Endhumvin Normuthal!' Ennum,
Paikolpaam Panaiyaay! Ivalthirath Tharulaay
Paaviyen Cheyyarpaa Ladhuve. 7.2.6

`Paaladhun Pangal Inpangal Pataiththaay!
Parrilaar Parrannin Raane,
Kaalachak Karaththaay! Katalitang Konta
Katalvannaa! Kannane!' Ennum,
`Chelkolthan Punalchooz Thiruvarang Kaththaay!'
Ennum`En Theerththane!' Ennum,
Kolamaa Mazaikkan Panimalka Irukkum
Ennudaik Komalak Kozundhe. 7.2.7

`Kozundhuvaa Nnavargatku' Ennum Kunrendhik
Konnirai Kaaththavan! Ennum,
Azundhozum Aavi Analavev Vuyirkkum
`Anchana Vannane!' Ennum,
Ezundhumel Nokki Yimaippilal Irukkum
`Engngane Nokkuken?' Ennum,
Chezundhatam Punalchooz Thiruvarang Kaththaay!
EnCheyken EnDhiru Magatke? 7.2.8

`EnDhiru Magalcher Maarvane!' Ennum
`Ennudai Yaaviye!' Ennum,
`NinDhiru Eyirraal Itandhunnee Konta
Nilamagal Kelvane!' Ennum,
`Anruru Vezum Thazuvinnee Konta
Aaymagal Anpane!' Ennum,
ThenDhiru Varangam Koyilkon Taane!
Thelikilen Mudivival Thanakke. (2) 7.2.9

`Mudivival Thanakkon Rarikilen' Ennum

Maayaa! Vaamana Nne!Madhu Choothaa! Neeyarulaay,

Engngane Chollinum Inpam Payakkume. (2) 7.9.11

Inpam Payakka Ezilmalar
