Anpur Ramarndhurai Kinraa
Nipozil Choozthiru Vaaranvilai,
Anpur Ramarndhu Valamcheydhu
Kaithozum Naalkalum Aakungolo! (2) 7.10.1

Aakungol Aiyamon Rinri
Agalitam Murravum, Eeradiye
Aakum Parichu Nimirndha
Thirukkural Appan Amarndhuraiyum,
Maagam Thikazkodi Maatangal
Neetum Mathilthiru Vaaranvilai,
Maagandha NeerKontu Thoovi
Valancheydhu Kaithozung Kootungolo! 7.10.2

Kootungol Vaikalum Kovindha
Nnaimadhu Choothanaik Kolariyai,
Aadum Paravai Michaikkantu
Kaithozu Thanri Yavanuraiyum,
Paadum Perumpukaz Naanmarai
Velviyainn Thaarangam Panninarvaaz,
Neetu Pozilthiru Vaaran
Vilaithoza Vaaykkungol Nichchalume! 7.10.3

Vaaykkungol Nichchalum Eppozu
Thummanaththu Eengu Ninaikkappera
Vaaykkum Karumpum Perunchenn
Nelumvayal Choozthiru Vaaranvilai,
Vaaykkum Perumpukaz Moovula
Keechan Vatamadhu Raippirandha,
Vaaykkum Maninnirak Kannapi
Raanran Malaradip Pothukale. 7.10.4

Malaradip Pothukal Ennenchath
Theppozu Thumiruth Thivananga,
Palaradi Yaarmun Paruliya
Paampanai Yappan Amarndhuraiyum,
Malaril Maninnetu Maatangal
Neetu Mathilthiru Vaaranvilai,
Ulagam Malipukaz Paatannam
Melvinai Onrumnnil Laaketume. 7.10.5

Onrumnnil Laaketum Murravum
Theevinai Yullith Thozumindhonteer,
Anrang Kamarven Ruruppini
Nangai Yaninnetunn Tholpunarndhaan,
Enrumep Pothumen Nnencham
Thuthippavul Leyiruk Kinrapiraan,
Ninra Anithiru Vaaran
Vilaiyennum Neenaga Ramadhuve. 7.10.6

Neenaga Ramadhu Vemalarch
Cholaikal Choozthiru Vaaranvilai,
Neenaga Raththurai Kinrapi
RaanNedu Maalkannan VinnavarKon
Vaana Purampukku Mukkatpi
Raanaith Tholaiyavem Porgalcheydhu,
Vaananai Yaayirann Tholthunith
Thaancharan Anrimar Ronrilame. 7.10.7

`Anrimar Ronrilam NinSara
NE!'En Ragalirum Poykaiyinvaay,
Ninruthan Neelkaza Leththiya
Aanaiyin Nenchitar Theerththapiraan,
Chenrang Kinithurai Kinra
Chezumpozil Choozthiru Vaaranvilai,
Onri Valancheyya Onrumo?
Theevinai Yullaththin Chaarvallave. 7.10.8

Theevinai Yullaththin Chaarvalla
Vaagith Theliveechum Peralurraal,
Naavinul Lumullath Thullum
Amaindha Thozilinul Lumnnavinru,
Yaavarum Vandhu Vanangum
Pozilthiru Vaaran Vilaiyadhanai,
Mevi Valancheydhu Kaithozak
Kootungol Ennumen Chindhanaiye. 7.10.9

Chindhaimar Ronrin Thiraththadhal
Laaththanmai Thevapi Raanariyum,
Chindhaiyi Nnaalcheyva Thaanari
Yaadhana Maayangal Onrumillai,
Chindhaiyi Nnaalcholli Nnaalcheykai
Yaalnnilath Thevar Kuzuvanangum,
Chindhai Magizthiru Vaaran
Vilaiyurai Theerththanuk Karrapinne. 7.10.10

Theerththanuk Karrapin Marror
Charanillai Yenrenni, Theerththanukke
Theerththa Manaththana Nnaagich
Chezunguru Koorchchata Kopanchonna,
Theerththanga Laayirath Thullivai
Paththumval Laargalai, Thevarvaikal
Theerththanga Leyenru Poochiththu
Nalgi Yuraippaardham Theviyarkke. (2) 7.10.11


Ettaam Paththu

Thevimaa Raavaar Thirumagal Poomi
Yevamar Ramararaat Cheyvaar,
Meviya Vulagam Moonravai Yaatchi
Venduven Turuvamnnin Nnuruvam,
Paaviyen Dhannai Yaduginra Kamalak
Kannadhor Pavalavaay Maniye,
Aaviye! Amudhe! Alaigadal Kadaindha
Appane! Kaanumaa Rarulaay. 8.1.1

`Kaanumaa Rarulaay' Enrenre Kalangik
Kannanneer Alamara Vinaiyen
Penumaa Rellaam Peninnin Peyare
Pidharrumaa Rarulenak Kandho,
Kaanumaa Rarulaay Kaaguththaa! Kannaa!
Thondanen Karpagak Kaniye,
Penuvaar Amudhe! Periyathan Punalchooz
Perunnilam Eduththape Raalaa! 8.1.2

Eduththape Raalan Nandhako Pandhan
Innuyirch Chiruvane, Achothaik
Kaduththape Rinbak Kulavilang Kalire!
Adiyanen Periyavam Maane,
Kaduththapor Avunan Utaliru Pilavaak
Kaiyugi Raandaveng Kadale,
Aduththadhor Uruvaay Inrunnee Vaaraay
Engnganam Theruvar Umare? 8.1.3

Umarukann Thukandha Vuruvamnnin Nnuruvam
Aagiyun Dhanakkanba Raanaar
Avar,Ukann Thamarndha Cheykaiyun Maayai
Arivonrum Changippan Vinaiyen,
Amarathu Panni Agalidam Putaichooz
Adupadai Aviththaam Maane,
Amarardham Amudhe! Achurargal Nanyche!
Ennutai Aaruyi Reyo! 8.1.4

Aaruyi Reyo! Agalidam Muzuthum
Padaiththidann Thundumiznn Thalandha,
Peruyi Reyo! Periyanneer Padaiththang
Kuraindhathu Kadaindhadaith Thutaiththa,
Cheeriya Reyo!Manicharkkuth Thevar
Polaththe Varkkumthe Vaavo,
Oruyi Reyo! Ulagangat Kellaam
Unnainnaan Enguvann Thuruko? 8.1.5

Enguvann Thuruko Ennaiyaal Vaane!
Ezula Kangalum Neeye,
Angavark Kamaiththa Theyvamum Neeye
Avarravai Karumamum Neeye,
Pongiya Purampaal Porulula Velum
Avaiyumo Neeyinne Yaanaal
Mangiya Aruvaam Nerppamum Neeye
Vaanbulam Irandhathum Neeye. 8.1.6

Irandhathum Neeye Ethirndhathum Neeye
Nigazvadho Neeyinne Yaanaal,
Chirandhannin Thanmai Yathuvithu Vuthuven
Rarivonrum Changippan Vinaiyen,
Karandhapaal Neyye! Neyyin Chuvaiye!
Kadalinul Amuthame, Amuthil
Pirandhavin Chuvaiye! Chuvaiyathu Payane!
Pinnaithol Manandhape Raayaa! 8.1.7

Manandhape Raayaa! Maayaththaal Muzuthum
Valvinai Yenaiyeer Kinra,
Kunangalai Yudaiyaay! Achurarvan Kaiyar
Koorrame! Kotiyapul Luyarththaay,
Panangalaa Yiramum Utaiyapainn Naagap
Palliyaay! Paarkadal Cherppaa,
Vanangumaa Raariyen! Manamumvaa Chagamum
Cheykaiyum Yaanumnnee Thaane. 8.1.8

Yaanumnnee Thaane Yaavadho Meyye
Arunnara Kavaiyum Neeyaanaal,
Vaanuya Rinbam Eythilen Marrai
Naragame Yeythilen? Enilum,
Yaanumnnee Thaanaayth Thelithorum Nanrum
Anychuvan Naragamnnaa Nnadaidhal,
Vaanuya Rinbam Manniveer Rirundhaay!
Arulunnin Thaalkalai Yenakke. 8.1.9

Thaalkalai Yenakke Thalaiththalai Chirappath
Thandhape Ruthavikkaim Maaraa,
Tholkalai Yaarath Thazuvithen Nnuyirai
Aravilai Cheythanan Chothee,
Tholkalaa Yiraththaay! Mudigalaa Yiraththaay!
Thunaimalark Kankalaa Yiraththaay,
Thaalkalaa Yiraththaay! Pergalaa Yiraththaay!
Thamiyanen Periya Appane! 8.1.10

Periya Appanaip Piraman Appanai
Uruththiran Appanai, Munivark
Kuriya Appanai Amarar Appanai
Ulagukkor Thaniyappan Dhannai,
Periyavan Kurukoor Vanchada Kopan
Penina Aayirath Thullum,
Uriyachol Maalai Ivaiyumpath Thivarraal
Uyyalaam Thondeer!Nnang Katke. (2) 8.1.11

Nangal Varivalai Yaayang Kaalo!
Nammutai Ethalar Munbu Naani,
Nungat Kiyaanonru Raikkum Maarram
Nokkugin Renengum Kaana Maatten,
Changam Charindhana Chaayi Zandhen
Thadamulai Ponnira Maayththa Larndhen,
Vengan Paravaiyin Paaga Nnengon
Vengada Vaananai Vendich Chenre. (2) 8.2.1

Vendichchen Ronru Perugir Paaril
Ennutaith Thoziyar Nungat Kelum,
Eendithu Raikkum Padiyai Yandho!
Kaankinri Lenida Raatti Yennaan,
Kaandhagu Thaamaraik Kannan Kalvan
Vinnavar Konnangal Konaik Kandaal,
Eendiya Changum Niraivum Kolvaan
Eththanai Kaalam Ilaikkin Rene! 8.2.2

Kaalam Ilaikkilal Laalvi Nnaiyen
Naanilaik Kinrilan Kandu Konmin,
Nyaalam Ariyap Pazichu Mandhen
Nannutha Leer!Ini Naanith Thaanen,
Neela Malarnneduny Chothi Choozndha
Neenda Mugilvannan Kannan Konda,
Kola Valaiyodu Maamai Kolvaan
Eththanai Kaalamkoo Tachchenre? 8.2.3

Kootachchen Renini Enko Dukken?
Kolvalai Nenychath Thotakka Mellaam,
Paadar Roziya Izandhu Vaigal
Palvalai Yaarmun Paricha Zindhen,
Maadak Kotimathil Thenku Landhai
Vankuta Paalnninra Maayak Kooththan,
Aadal Paravai Uyarththa Velpor
Aazi Valavinai Yaathariththe. 8.2.4

Aazi Valavinai Aatharippum Aangavan
Nammil Varavum Ellaam,
Thoziyar Kaal!Nnam Mutaiya Methaan?
Cholluva Thoving Kariyathuthaan,
Oozitho Roozi Oruva Nnaaga
Nangunar Vaarkkum Unara Laagaa,
Chooza Lutaiya Chutarko Laathith
Thollaiyany Chothi Ninaikkung Kaale. 8.2.5

Thollaiyany Chothi Ninaikkung Kaalen
Chollala Vanrimai Yortha Makkum,
Ellaiyi Laathana Koozppuch Cheyyum
Aththiram Nirkavem Maamai Kondaan,
Alli Malarththan Tuzaayum Thaaraan
Aarkkidu Kovinip Poochal Cholleer,
Valli Valavayal Choozku Tandhai
Maamalark Kanvalar Kinra Maale. 8.2.6

`Maalari Kechavan Naara Nanychee
Maathavan Kovindhan Vaikundhan' Enrenru,
Ola Midavennaip Panni Vittit
Tonru Muruvum Chuvadum Kaattaan,
Ela Malarkuzal Annai Meergaal!
Ennutaith Thoziyar Kaal!En Cheyken?
Kaalam Palachenrum Kaanpa Thaanai
Ungalo Tenga Lidaiyil Laiye. 8.2.7

Idaiyil Laiyaan Valarththa Kiligaal!
Poovaigal Kaal!Kuyil Kaal!Ma Yilkaal,
Utaiyannam Maamaiyum Changum Nenychum
Onrum Oziyavot Taathu Kondaan,
Adaiyum Vaikundha Mumpaar Kadalum
Anychana Verpum Avainna Niya,
Kadaiyarap Paachangal Vitta Pinnai
Anri Yavanavai Kaanko Taane. 8.2.8

Kaankodup Paanalla Nnaarkkum Thannaik
Kaicheyap Paaladhor Maayann Thannaal,
Maankural Kola Vadivu Kaatti
Mannum Vinnum Niraiya Malarndha,
Chenchutarth Tholkal Palatha Zaiththa
Theva Piraarken Niraivinodu,
Naankoduth Thenini Yengodukken
Ennutai Nannuthal Nangai Meergaal. 8.2.9

Ennutai Nannuthal Nangai Meergaal!
Yaaninach Cheyvathen? Enneny Chennai,
`Nninnidai Yenallen' Enru Neengi
Nemiyum Changum Irukaik Kondu,
Panneduny Choozchutar Nyaayir Rodu
Paanmathi Endhior Kola Neela,
Nannedung Kunram Varuva Thoppaan
Naanma Larppaa Thamadainn Thathuve. 8.2.10

Paatham Adaivathan Paachath Thaale
Marravan Paachangal Murra Vittu,
Kothil Pukazkkan Nandhan Nnadimel
Vankuru Koorchchada Kopan Chonna,
Theethilandhaadhiyo Raayi Raththul
Ivaiyumor Paththichai Yodum Vallaar,
Aathumor Theethila Raagi Yingum
Angumel Laamamai Vaargal Thaame. (2) 8.2.11

Angu Mingum Vaanavar Thaanavar Yaavarum,
Engum Inaiyaiyen Runnai Ariyagilaa Thalarri,
Angam Cherum Poomagal Manmagal Aaymagal,
Changu Chakkarak Kaiyava Nnenbar Charaname. (2) 8.3.1

Charana Maagiya Naanmarai Noolkalum Chaaraathe,
Maranam Thorram Vaanbini Mooppen Rivaimaayththom,
Karanap Palpadai Parrara Vodum Kanalaazi,
Aranath Thinpadai Yendhiya Eechar Kaalaaye. 8.3.2

Aalum Aalaar Aaziyum Changum Chumappaardhaam,
Vaalum Villung Kondupin Chelvaar Maarrillai,
Thaalum Tholum Kaigalai Yaarath Thozakkaanen,
Naalum Naalum Naaduvan Adiyen Nyaalaththe. 8.3.3

Nyaalam Ponagam Parriyor Murraa Vuruvaagi,
Aalam Perilai Yannava Chanycheyyum Ammaane,
Kaalam Pervadhor Kaariru Luziyoth Thulathaal,Un
Kolang Kaarezil Kaanalur Raazum Kotiyerke. 8.3.4

Kotiyaar Maadak Kolu Ragaththum Pulingudiyum,
Madiyaa Thinne Neethuyil Mevi Magizndhathuthaan,
Adiyaar Allal Thavirththa Achaivo? Anrel,Ip
Padidhaan Neendu Thaaviya Achaivo? Paniyaaye. 8.3.5

Paniyaa Amarar Panivum Panpum Thaameyaam,
Aniyaar Aaziyum Changamu Mendhum Avarkaanmin,
Thaniyaa Venno Yulagil Thavirppaan, Thirunneela
Maniyaar Meniyo Tenmanam Chooza Varuvaare. 8.3.6

Varuvaar Chelvaar Vanpari Saarath Thirundha,En
Thiruvaaz Maarvar Kendhiram Chollaar Cheyvathen,
Uruvaar Chakkaram Changu Chumandhing Kummodu,
Orupaa Tuzalvaa Nnoradi Yaanu Mulanenre. 8.3.7

Enre Yennaiyun Eraar Kolath Thirundhadikkeez,
Ninre Yaatcheyya Neekon Tarula Ninaippathuthaan,
Kunrez Paarez Choozkadal Nyaalam Muzuvezum,
Ninre Thaaviya Neelkazal Aazith Thirumaale! 8.3.8

Thirumaal Naanmukan Chenychadai Yaanen Rivargal,Em
Perumaan Thanmaiyai Yaarari Kirpaar Pechiyen,
Orumaa Muthalvaa! Oozip Piraanen Nnaiyaalutai,
Karumaa Meniyan Enbanen Kaathal Kalakkave. 8.3.9

Kalakka Millaa Nalthava Munivar Karaigandor,
Thulakka Millaa Vaanava Rellaam Thozuvaargal,
Malakka Meytha Maagadal Thannaik Kadaindhaanai,
Ulakka Naampukaz Kirpathen Cheyva Thuraiyeere. 8.3.10

Uraiyaa Vennoy Thavira Arulnneen Mudiyaanai,
Varaiyaar Maadam Mannu Kurukoorch Chadakopan,
Uraiyey Cholthotai Oraa Yiraththu Lippaththum,
Niraiye Vallaar Needula Kaththup Piravaare. (2) 8.3.11

Vaarkadaa Aruvi Yaanaimaa Malaiyin
Maruppinaik Kuvadiruth Thurutti,
Oorkolthin Paagan Uyirchekuth Tharangin
Mallaraik Konruchooz Paranmel,
Porkadaa Varachar Purakkida Maada
Meemachaik Kanychanaith Thagarththa,
Cheerkolchir Raayan Thiruchchengun Rooril
Thiruchchirraa Rengalchel Chaarve. (2) 8.4.1

Engalchel Chaarvu Yaamutai Amutham
Imaiyavar Appanen Appan,
Pongumoo Vulagum Padaiththalith Thazikkum
Porundhumoo Vuruvanem Aruvan,
Chengayal Ukalum Thempanai Putaichooz
Thiruchchengun Roorththiruch Chirraaru
Angamar Kinra, Aathiyaan Allaal
Yaavarmar Renamar Thunaiye? 8.4.2

Ennamar Perumaan Imaiyavar Perumaan
Irunnilam Idandhavem Perumaan,
Munnaival Vinaigal Muzuthutan Maala
Ennaiyaal Kinraem Perumaan,
Thendhichaik Kanikol Thiruchchengun Rooril
Thiruchchirraa Rangarai Meepaal
Ninravem Perumaan, Adiyallaal Charanam
Ninaippilum Pirithillai Enakke. 8.4.3

Pirithillai Yenakkup Periyamoo Vulagum
Niraiyappe Ruruvamaay Nimirndha,
Kuriyamaan Emmaan Kuraigadal Kadaindha
Kolamaa Nikkamen Emmaan,
Cherikulai Vaazai Kamukutheng Kanichooz
Thiruchchengun Roorththiruch Chirraaru
Ariya,Meym Maiye Ninravem Perumaan
Adiyinai Yalladhor Arane. 8.4.4

Alladhor Aranum Avanilve Rillai
Athuporu Laagilum, Avanai
Allathen Aavi Amarndhanai Killaa
Thaathalaal Avanurai Kinra,
Nallannaan Maraiyor Velviyul Maduththa
Narumpukai Vichumpoli Maraikkum,
Nallanneel Maadath Thiruchchengun Rooril
Thiruchchirraa Renakkunnal Larane. 8.4.5

Enakkunnal Laranai Enathaa Ruyirai
Imaiyavar Thandhaidhaay Thannai,
Thanakkundhan Thanmai Arivari Yaanaith
Thadangadal Palliyam Maanai,
Manakkolcheer Moovaa Yiravarvan Chivanum
Ayanum Thaanumop Paarvaaz,
Kanakkolthin Maadath Thiruchchengun Rooril
Thiruchchirraa Rathanulkan Tene. 8.4.6

Thiruchchengun Rooril Thiruchchirraa Rathanul
Kandavath Thiruvadi Yenrum,
Thiruchcheyya Kamalak Kannoomchev Vaayum
Chevvadi Yumcheyya Kaiyum,
Thiruchcheyya Kamala Vundhiyum Cheyya
Kamalamaar Pumcheyya Vutaiyum,
Thiruchcheyya Mudiyum Aaramum Padaiyum
Thigazaven Chindhaiyu Laane. 8.4.7

Thigazaven Chindhai Yullirunn Thaanaich
Chezunnilath Thevarnnaan Maraiyor,
Thichaigaikooppi Yeththum Thiruchchengun Rooril
Thiruchchirraa Rangarai Yaanai,
Pukarkolvaa Nnavargal Pukalidann Thannai
Achurarvan Kaiyarveng Koorrai,
Pukazumaa Rariyen Porundhumoo Vulagum
Padaippodu Keduppukkaap Pavane! 8.4.8

Padaippodu Keduppuk Kaappavan Pirama
Paramparan Chivaperumaan Avane,
Idaippukko Ruruvum Ozivillai Yavane
Pukazvillai Yaavaiyum Thaane,
Kotaipperum Pukazaar Inaiyardhan Nnaanaar
Kooriya Vichchaiyo Tozukkam,
Nadaippali Yiyarkaith Thiruchchengun Rooril
Thiruchchirraa Ramarndha Naathane. 8.4.9

Amarndha Naathanai Yavarava Raagi
Avarkkarul Arulumam Maanai
Amarndhathan Pazanath Thiruchchengun Rooril
Thiruchchirraar Rangarai Yaanai,
Amarndhacheer Moovaa Yiravarve Thiyargal
Thampathi Yavanithe Varvaazvu,
Amarndhamaa Yonai Mukkanam Maanai
Naanmuka Nnaiyamarnn Thene. 8.4.10

Thenainnan Paalaik Kannalai Yamuthaith
Thirundhula Kundavam Maanai,
Vaanannaan Mukanai Malarndhan Koppooz
Malarmichaip Padaiththamaa Yonai,
Konaivan Kurukoorch Vanchada Kopan
Chonnavaa Yiraththulip Paththum,
Vaaninmee Therri Yarulcheythu Mudikkum
Piravimaa Maayakkooth Thinaiye. (2) 8.4.11

Maayak Kooththaa! Vaamanaa!
Vinaiyen Kannaa! Kankaigaal
Thooya Cheyya Malargalaach
Chothich Chevvaay Mugizathaa,
Chaayal Chaamath Thirumeni
Thanpaa Chadaiyaa, Thaamarainneel
Vaachath Thadampol Varuvaane!
Orunnaal Kaana Vaaraaye. (2) 8.5.1

`Kaana Vaaraay' Enrenru
Kannum Vaayum Thuvarndhu,Adiyen
Naani Nannaat Talamandhaal
Irangi Yorunnaal Neeyandho,
Kaana Vaaraay Karunnaayi
Ruthikkum Karumaa Maanikka,
Naanal Malaipol Chutarchchothi
Mudicher Chenni Yammaane! 8.5.2

`Mudicher Chenni Yammaa!Nnin
Moypoonn Thaamath Thanduzaay,
Kadicher Kannip Perumaane!'
Enren Rengi Yazuthakkaal,
Padicher Magarak Kuzaigalum
Pavala Vaayum Naaltholum,
Thudise Ridaiyum Amaindhadhor
Thoonneer Mugilpol Thonraaye. 8.5.3

Thoonneer Mugilpol Thonrumnnin
Chutarkol Vadivum Kanivaayum,
Thenneerk Kamalak Kankalum
Vandhen Chindhai Niraindhavaa,
Maanneer Vellee Malaidhanmel
Vankaar Neela Mugilpola,
Thoonneerk Kadalul Thuyilvaane!
Endhaay! Cholla Maattene. 8.5.4

Cholla Maatten Adiyenun
Thulangu Chothith Thiruppaatham,
Ellai Yilchee Rilanyaayi
Rirandu Polen Nnullavaa!,
Allal Ennum Irulcherdhar
Kupaayam Enne?, Aazichooz
Mallal Nyaala Muzuthunda
Maanneerk Kondal Vannane! 8.5.5

`Kondal Vannaa! Kutakkooththaa!
Vinaiyen Kannaa! Kannaa,En
Anda Vaanaa!' Enrennai
Aalak Kooppit Tazaiththakkaal,
Vindan Melthaan Manmelthaan
Virinneerk Kadalthaan Marruththaan,
Thonda Nnenul Kazallaana
Orunnaal Vandhu Thonraaye. 8.5.6

Vandhu Thonraa Yanrelun
Vaiyam Thaaya Malaradikkeez,
Mundhi Vandhu Yaannirpa
Mukappe Koovip Panikollaay,
Chendhan Kamalak Kankaigaal
Chivandha Vaayor Karunnaayiru,
Andha Millaak Kathirparappi
Alarndha Thokkum Ammaane! 8.5.7

Okkum Ammaa Nnuruvamen
Rullam Kuzaindhu Naanaalum,
Thokka Mekap Palkuzaangal
Kaanunn Thorum Tholaivannaan,
Thakka Aivar Thamakkaayanru
Eeraim Pathinmar Thaalchaaya,
Pukka Naltherth Thanippaagaa!
Vaaraay Ithuvo Poruththame? 8.5.8

`Ithuvo Poruththam Minnaazip
Padaiyaay! Erum Irunychichiraippul,
Athuve Kotiyaa Vuyarthththaane!'
Enren Rengi Yazuthakkaal,
Ethuve Yaagak Karuthungol
Immaa Nyaalam Poraitheerppaan,
Mathuvaar Cholai Yuththara
Mathuraip Pirandha Maayane? 8.5.9

Pirandha Maayaa! Paaratham
Porutha Maayaa! Neeyinne,
Chirandha Kaalthee Neervaanman
Piravu Maaya Perumaane,
Karandha Paalul Neyyepol
Ivarru Lengum Kandukol,
Irandhu Ninra Perumaayaa!
Unnai Enge Kaankene? 8.5.10

`Enge Kaanken Eendhuzaay
Ammaan Dhannai Yaan?'Enrenru
Ange Thaazndha Chorkalaal
Andhan Kurukoorch Chadakopan,
Chengez Chonna Vaayiraththul
Ivaiyum Paththum Vallaargal,
Inge Kaana Ippirappe
Magizvar Elliyum Kaalaiye. (2) 8.5.11

Elliyum Kaalaiyum Thannai Ninaindheza,
Nalla Arulkal Namakkethann Tharulcheyvaan,
Alliyann Thannann Thuzaaymudi Yappanoor,
Chelvargal Vaazum Thirukkadith Thaaname. (2) 8.6.1

Thirukkadith Thaanamum Ennutaich Chindhaiyum,
Orukkaduth Thulle Uraiyum Piraangandeer,
Cherukkaduth Thanru Thigaiththa Arakkarai,
Urukketa Vaali Pozindha Oruvane. 8.6.2

Oruva Riruvaror Moova Renanninru,
Uruvu Karandhul Lundhorum Thiththippaan,
Thiruvamar Maarvan Thirukkadith Thaanaththai,
Maruvi Yuraikinra Maayap Piraane. 8.6.3

Maayap Piraanena Valvinai Maayndhara,
Neyaththi Nnaalnnenycham Naadu Kudikondaan,
Thechath Thamarar Thirukkadith Thaanaththai,
Vaachap Pozilmannu Koyilkon Taane. 8.6.4

Koyilkon Taandhan Thirukkadith Thaanaththai,
Koyilkon Taanatha Nnetumen Nnenychagam,
Koyilkol Theyvamel Laamthoza, Vaikundham
Koyilkon Tagutak Kooththavam Maane. 8.6.5

Kooththavam Maangoti Yenidar Murravum,
Maayththavam Maanmathu Choothavam Maanurai,
Pooththa Pozilthan Thirukkadith Thaanaththai,
Eththannil Laagurik Kondamin Idare. 8.6.6

Kondamin Idarketa Vullaththuk Kovindhan,
Manvin Muzuthum Alandhavon Taamarai,
Mannavar Thaamthoza Vaanavar Thaamvandhu,
Nannu Thirukkadith Thaana Nagare. 8.6.7

Thaana Nagargal Thalaichirann Thengengum,
Vaaninn Nilamkadal Murrumem Maayarke,
Aana Vidaththumen Nenychum Thirukkadith
Thaana Nagarum, Thanathaayap Pathiye. 8.6.8

Thaayap Pathigalthalaichirann Thengengum,
Maayaththi Nnaalmanni Veerrirunn Thaanurai,
Theyath Thamarar Thirukkadith Thaanaththul,
Aayark Kathipathi Arputhan Thaane. 8.6.9

Arputhan Naaraa Yananari Vaamanan,
Nirpathu Mevi Yiruppathen Nnenychagam,
Narpukaz Vethiyar Naanmarai Ninrathir,
Karpagach Cholaith Thirukkadith Thaaname. 8.6.10

Cholai Thirukkadith Thaanath Thuraithiru
Maalai, Mathilkuru Koorchchadakopanychol,
Paalo Tamuthanna Aayirath Thippaththum,
Melaivai Kundhath Thiruththum Viyandhe. (2) 8.6.11

Iruththum Viyandhennaith Thanbon Nnadikkeezenru,
Aruththith Thenaiththor Palannaal Azaiththerku,
Poruththa Mutaivaa Manandhaan Pukundhu,Endhan
Karuththai Yuraveer Rirundhaan Kandukonde. (2) 8.7.1

Irundhaan Kandukon Tenathezai Nenychaalum,
Thirundhaatha Voraiva Raiththeynn Tharamanni,
Perundhaal Kalirruk Karulcheytha Perumaan,
Tharundhaan Arulthaan Iniyaan Ariyene. 8.7.2

Arulthaa Nniniyaan Ariyen Avanennul,
Irulthaan Araveer Rirundhaan Ithuvallaal,
Porulthaa Nnenilmoo Vulagum Porulalla,
Marulthaanee Tho?Maaya Mayakku Mayakke. 8.7.3

Maaya Mayakkumayak Kaanennai Vanychiththu,
Aayan Amarark Kariye Renathammaan,
Thooya Chutarchchothi Thanathennul Vaiththaan,
Theyam Thigazumthan Thiruvarul Cheythe. 8.7.4

Thigazundhan Thiruvarul Cheythula Kaththaar,
Pukazum Pukazthaa Nnathukaattith Thandhu,Ennul
Thigazum Manikkunra Monre Yoththunninraan,
Pukazum Pukazmar Renakkumor Porule? 8.7.5

Porulmar Renakkumor Porulthannil Cheerkkath
Tharumel,Pin Yaarkkavan Thannaik Kodukkum?,
Karumaa Nikkak Kunraththuth Thaamaraipol,
Thirumaarbu Kaalkankai Chevvaay Undhiyaane. 8.7.6

Chevvaayundhi Venpal Chutarkkuzai, Thannodu
Evvaaych Chutarum Thammilmun Valaaykkolla,
Chevvaay Muruvalo Tenathullath Thirundha,
Avvaa Yanriyaan Ariyenmar Rarule. 8.7.7

Ariyenmar Rarulennai Yaalum Piraanaar,
Verithe Yarulcheyvar Cheyvaargat Kukandhu,
Chiriye Nnutaichchindhai Yulmoo Vulagum,Tham
Neriyaa Vayirrirkondu Ninrozinn Thaare. 8.7.8

Vayirrirkondu Ninrozinn Thaarum Yavarum,
Vayirrirkondu Ninroru Moovula Kum,Tham
Vayirrirkondu Ninravan Namnninra Maalai,
Vayirrirkondu Mannavaith Thenmathi Yaale. 8.7.9

Vaiththen Mathiyaa Lenathullath Thagaththe,
Eyththe Yozivenal Lenenrum Eppothum,
Moyththey Thiraimothu Thanpaar Kadalulaal,
Paiththey Chutarppaam Panainnam Paranaiye. 8.7.10

Chutarppaam Panainnam Paranaith Thirumaalai,
Adichcher Vagaivan Kurukoorch Chadakopan,
Mudippaan Chonnavaa Yiraththippath Thumchanmam
Vida,Theynn Tharannokkum Thangankal Chivandhe. (2) 8.7.11

Kankal Chivandhu Periyavaay
Vaayum Chivandhu Kanindhu,Ulle
Venpal Ilagu Chutarilagu
Vilagu Magara Kundalaththan,
Kondal Vannan Chutarmudiyan
Naangu Tholan Kunichaarngan,
Onchang Kathaivaa Laaziyaan
Oruvan Adiye Nnullaane. (2) 8.8.1

Adiye Nnullaan Utalullaan
Andath Thagaththaan Puraththullaan,
Padiye Yithuven Ruraikkalaam,
Padiyan Allan Paramparan,
Kadicher Naarrath Thullaalai
Inbath Thunbak Kazinnermai,
Otiyaa Inbap Perumaiyon
Unarvi Lumpa Roruvane. 8.8.2

Unarvi Lumpa Roruvanai
Avana Tharulaa Luralporuttu,En
Unarvi Nnulle Yiruththinen
Athuvum Avana Thinnarule,
Unarvum Uyirum Utampum
Marrulappi Lanavum Pazudheyaam,
Unarvaip Peravoornn Thiraveri
Yaanum Thaanaa Yozindhaane. 8.8.3

Yaanum Thaanaa Yozindhaanai
Yaathum Yavarkkum Munnonai,
Thaanum Chivanum Piramanum
Aagip Panaiththa Thanimuthalai,
Thenum Paalum Kannalum
Amuthum Aagith Thiththiththu,En
Ooni Luyiri Lunarvinil
Ninra Vonrai Yunarndhene. 8.8.4

Ninra Onrai Yunarndhenukku
Athanul Nermai Athuvithuvenru,
Onrum Oruvark Kunaralaagaadhu
Unarndhum Melum Kaanparithu
Chenru Chenru Paramparamaay
Yaathu Minrith Theyndharru,
Nanru Theethen Rarivaridhaay
Nanraay Nyaanam Kadandhathe. 8.8.5

Nanraay Nyaanam Kadandhupoy
Nallinn Thiriya Mellaameerththu,
Onraayk Kidandha Arumperumpaaz
Ulappi Lathanai Yunarndhunarndhu,
Chenraang Kinba Thunbangal
Cherruk Kalaindhu Pachaiyarraal,
Anre Yappo Theveedu
Athuve Veedu Veetaame. 8.8.6

Athuve Veedu Veedu
Perrinbann Thaanum Athudheri,
Ethuve Thaanum Parrinri
Yaathu Miliga Laagirkil,
Athuve Veedu Veedu
Perrinbann Thaanum Athudheraathu,
`Ethuve Veedu Edhu Inbam?'En
Reyththaa Reyththaa Reyththaare. 8.8.7

Eyththaa Reyththaa Reyththaaren
Rillaath Thaarum Puraththaarum
Moyththu,Aang Kalari Muyangaththaam
Pokum Pothu,Un Maththarpol
Piththe Yeri Yannuraagam
Poziyum Pothem Pemmaanodu
Oththe Chenru,Ang Kulamkootak
Kootir Raagil Nalluraippe. 8.8.8

Kootir Raagil Nalluraippuk
Kootaa Maiyaik Kootinaal,
Aadal Paravai Yuyarkotiyem
Aaya Nnaava Thathuvathuve,
Veetaip Panni Yorupariche
Ethirvum Nigazvum Kazivumaay,
Otith Thiriyum Yokigalum
Ularu Millai Yallare. 8.8.9

Ularu Millai Yallaraay
Ularaa Yillai Yaagiye,
Ularem Moruvar Avarvandhen
Ullath Thulle Yuraikinraar
Valarum Piraiyum Theypiraiyum
Pol Achaivum Aakkamum,
Valarum Chutarum Irulumpol
Therulum Marulum Maayththome. 8.8.10

Therulum Marulum Maayththuththan
Thirundhu Chempor Kazaladikkeez
Aruli Yiruththum Ammaanaam
Ayanaam Chivanaam,Thirumaalaal
Arulap Patta Chadakopan
Oraa Yiraththu Lippaththaal,
Aruli Yadikkee Ziruththumnnam
Annal Karumaa Nikkame. (2) 8.8.11

Karumaa Nikka Malaimelmanith
Thadandhaamaraik Kaadukalpol,
Thirumaarvu Vaaykankai Yundhigaalutai
Yaadaigal Cheyyapiraan
Thirumaa Lemmaan Chezunneervayal
Kuttannaattuth Thiruppuliyoor,
Arumaayan Peranrip Pechchilal
Annaimeeridhar Kencheykenaa. (2) 8.9.1

Annaimee Ridharken Cheyken?
Animeruvin Meethulavum,
Thunnu Choozchutar Nyaayirum
Anriyumpal Chutargalumpol,
Minnu Neenmudi Yaarampalkalan
Thaanutai Yemperumaan,
Punnai Yampozil Choozthirup
Puliyoor Pukazumivale. 8.9.2

Pukazu Mivalnnin Riraappagal
Porunneerkkadal Theeppattu,Engum
Thigazu Meriyodu Chelvathoppach
Chezungathi Raazimuthal
Pukazum Porupadai Yendhippor
Pukkachuraraip Ponruviththaan
Thigazu Maninnedu Maadamnneedu
Thiruppooli Yurvalame. 8.9.3

Oorva Lamkilar Cholaiyum
Karumpumperuny Chennelumchoozndhu
Erva Lamkilar Thanpanaik
Kuttannaattuth Thiruppooliyur,
Cheerva Lamkilar Moovula
Kundumiz Thevapiraan,
Perva Lamkilarnn Thanrip
Pechchilalinrip Punaiyizaiye. 8.9.4

Punaiyizaigal Anivum Aadaiyutaiyum Puthukka Nippum,
Ninaiyum Neermaiya Thanrivatkithu Ninru Ninaikkappukkaal,
Chunuyi Nnulthadann Thaamarai Malarumthan Thiruppuliyur,
Munaivan Moovula Kaaliappan Thiruvarul Moozkinale. 8.9.5

Thiruvarul Moozki Vaigalum Chezunneernnirak Kannapiraan,
Thiruvarul Kalumchernn Thamaikkadai Yaalam Thirundhavula,
Thiruvarul Arulaal Avanychenru Cherthan Thiruppooliyur,
Thiruvarul Kamukon Pazaththathu Melliyal Chevvidhaze. 8.9.6

Mellilaich Chelvan Kotipulka Veengilann Thaalkamugin,
Mallilai Madalvaazai Yeengani Choozndhu Manamkamazndhu,
Pullilaith Thengi Nnoodukaal Ulavumthan Thiruppooliyur,
Mallalam Chelvak Kannandhaal Adaindhaalim Madavarale. 8.9.7

Madavaral Annaimeerkat Kenychollich
Cholluken? Mallaichchelva
Vadamozi Maraivaanar Velviyul
Neyyazal Vaanbukaipoy
Thidavichum Pilamarar Naattai
Maraikkumthan Thiruppooliyur,
Padavara Vanaiyaan Dhannaamam
Allaal Paravaa Livale. 8.9.8

Paravaa Livalnnin Riraappagal
Paninneernnirak Kannapiraan,
Viravaa Richaimarai Vethiyaroli
Velaiyin Ninrolippa,
Karavaar Thadandhorum Thaamaraik
Kayandheevigai Ninralarum,
Puravaar Kazanigal Choozthirup
Puliyoorppuka Zanrimarre. 8.9.9

Anrimar Rorupaaya Menniva
Landhandu Zaaykamazthal,
Kunra Maamani Maadamaaligaik
Kolakku Zaangalmalki,
Thendhi Chaiththila Thampuraik
Kuttannaattuth Thiruppooliyur,
Ninra Maayappi Raandhiru
Varulaamival Nerppattathe. 8.9.10

Nerppatta Niraimoo Vulagukkum
Naayagan Dhannadimai,
Nerppatta Thondarthondar
Thondarthondan Chadako Pan,Chol
Nerppatta Thamizmaalai Yaayiraththul
Ivaiyu Morpaththum
Nerppat Taaravar, Nerppattaar
Nedumaarkadi Maicheyyave. (2) 8.9.11


Nedumaar Kadimai Cheyvenbol
Avanai Karutha Vanychiththu,
Thadumaar Rarra Theekkathigal
Murrum Thavirndha Chathirnninaindhaal,
Kodumaa Vinaiyen Avanadiyaar
Adiye Koodum Ithuvallaal,
Vidumaa Renba Thennandho!
Viyanmoo Vulagu Perinume? (2) 8.10.1

Viyanmoo Vulagu Perinumpoyth
Thaane Thaane Yaanaalum,
Puyalme Kampol Thirumeni
Ammaan Punaipoong Kazaladikkeez,
Chayame Yadimai Thalainninraar
Thiruththaal Vanangi, Immaiye
Payane Yinbam Yaanberra
Thurumo Paavi Yenukke? 8.10.2

Urumo Paavi Yenukkiv
Vulagam Moonrum Utanniraiya,
Chirumaa Meni Nimirththaven
Chendhaa Maraikkan Thirukkuralan
Narumaa Virainnaan Malaradikkeezp
Pukuthal Anri Avanadiyaar,
Chirumaa Manicha Raayennai
Aandaa Ringe Thiriyave. 8.10.3

Inge Thirindher Kizakkurren!
Irumaa Nilamun Nnundumizndha,
Chengo Laththa Pavalavaaych
Chendhaa Maraikka Nennammaan
Pongez Pukazkal Vaayavaayp
Pulangol Vadiven Manaththaay
Angey Malargal Kaiyavaay
Vazipat Tota Arulile? 8.10.4

Vazipat Tota Arulperru
Maayan Kola Malaradikkeez,
Chuzipat Todum Chutarchchothi
Vellath Thinbur Rirundhaalum,
Izipat Todum Utalinir
Pirandhu Thanycheer Yaangarru,
Mozipat Todum Kaviyamutha
Nukarchchi Yurumo Muzuthume? 8.10.5

Nukarchchi Yurumo Moovulagin
Veedu Peru Thangezil,
Pukarchchem Mukaththa Kaliratta
Ponnaa Zikkai Yennammaan,
Nigarchchem Pangi Yerivizigal
Neenda Achura Ruyirellaam,
Thagarththun Tuzalum Putpaagan
Periya Thanimaap Pukaze? 8.10.6

Thanimaap Pukaze Yenynyaanrum
Nirkum Padiyaath Thaandhonri,
Munimaap Pirama Muthalviththaay
Ulagam Moonrum Mulaippiththa,
Thanimaath Theyvath Thaliradikkeezp
Pukuthal Anri Avanadiyaar,
Nanimaak Kalavi Yinbame
Naalum Vaaykka Nangatke. 8.10.7

Naalum Vaaykka Nangatku
Nalirnneerk Kadalaip Padaiththu,Than
Thaalum Tholum Mudigalum
Chamani Laatha Palaparappi,
Neelum Padarpoong Karpagak
Kaavum Niraipan Nnaayirrin,
Kolu Mutaiya Manimalaipol
Kidandhaan Thamargal Koottame. 8.10.8

Thamargal Kootta Valvinaiyai
Naachany Cheyyum Chathirmoorththi,
Amarkol Aazi Changuvaal
Vilthan Taathi Palpadaiyan,
Kumaran Kola Ainganaivel
Thaathai Kothil Adiyaardham.
Thamargal Thamargal Thamargalaam
Chathire Vaaykka Thamiyerke. 8.10.9

Vaaykka Thamiyer Koozitho
Roozi Yoozi Maagaayaam
Pookkol Meni Naanguthol
Ponnaa Zikkai Yennammaan,
Neekka Millaa Adiyaardham
Adiyaar Adiyaar Adiyaareng
Kokkal, Avarkke Kudigalaaych
Chellum Nalla Kotpaate. 8.10.10

Nalla Kotpaat Tulagangal
Moonri Nnullum Thaanniraindha,
Allik Kamalak Kannanai
Andhan Kurukoorch Chadakopan,
Chollap Patta Aayiraththul
Ivaiyum Paththum Vallaargal,
Nalla Pathaththaal Manaivaazvar
Konda Pendir Makkale. (2) 8.10.11


Onbadhaam Paththu

Konda Pendir Makkalurraar Churrath Thavarpirarum,
Kanda Thotu Pattathallaal Kaadhalmarru Yaadhumillai,
Endi Chaiyum Keezummelum Murravu Mundapiraan,
Thonda Romaa Yuyyalallaa Lillaikan Teerthunaiye. (2) 9.1.1

Thunaiyum Chaarvu Maaguvaarpol Churrath Thavarpirarum,
Anaiyavandha Aakkamundel Attaigalpolchuvaippar,
Kanaiyon Raale Yezmaamaramu Meythaeng Kaarmukilai,
Punaiyen Ruyyap Pogilallaa Lillaikan Teerporule. 9.1.2

Porulkai Yundaaych Chellak
Kaanil Porriyen Rerrezuvar,
Irulkol Thunbath Thinmai
Kaanil Enneen Paarumillai,
Marulkol Cheykai Yachurar
Manga Vatamadhu Raippirandhaarku
Arulkol Aalaay Uyyal
Allaal Illaikan Teerarane. 9.1.3

Aranam Aavar Arra
Kaalaik Kenren Ramaikkappattaar,
Iranam Konda Theppar
Aavar Inriyit Taalumaqathe,
Varunith Thenne Vatamadhu
Raippi Randhavan Vanpukaze,
Charanen Ruyyap Pokal
Allaal Illaikan Teerchathire. 9.1.4

Chathuram Enru Thammaith
Thaame Chammathith Thinmoziyaar,
Madhura Poka Madhuvur
Ravare Vaikimar Ronruruvar,
Athirkol Cheykai Yachurar
Manga Vatamadhu Raippirandhaarku ,
Ethirkol Aalaay Uyyal
Allaal Illaikan Teerinbame. 9.1.5

Illai Kandeer Inbam
Andho! Ulladhu Ninaiyaathe,
Thollai Yaarka Leththa Nnaivar
Thonrik Kazindhozindhaar?
Mallai Moothoor Vatama
Thuraippi Randhavan Vanpukaze,
Cholli Yuyyap Pokal
Allaal Marronril Laichurukke. 9.1.6

Marron Rillai Churungach
Chonnom Maannilath Thevvuyirkkum,
Chirra Vendaa Chindhip
Peyamai Yumkan Teergalandho!
Kurraman Rengal Perrath
Thaayan Vatamadhu Raippirandhaan,
Kurra Milcheer Karru
Vaikal Vaazthalkan Teerkuname. 9.1.7

Vaazthal Kandeer Kunami
Thandho! Maayavan Adiparavi,
Pozthu Poka Vulla
Kirkum Punmaiyi Laadhavarkku,
Vaazthu Naiyaa Vatama
Thuraippi Randhavan Vanpukaze,
Veezthu Naiyaayp Pomi
Thanilyaa Thumillai Mikkathe. 9.1.8

Yaadhu Millai Mikka
Thanilen Ranra Thukaruthi,
Kaadhu Cheyvaan Koothai
Cheythu Kataimurai Vaazkaiyumpom,
Maadhu Kilingo Tikkol
Maata Vatamadhu Raippirandha,
Thaadhu Cherthaal Kannan
Allaal Illaikan Teericharane. 9.1.9

Kannan Allaal Illai
Kandeer Charanadhu Nirkavandhu,
Mannin Paaram Neekku
Tharke Vatamadhu Raippirandhaan,
Thinna Maannum Mutaimai
Yundel Avanadi Cherndhuymmino,
Enna Vendaa Numma
Thaadhum Avananri Marrillaiye. 9.1.10

Aadhum Illai Marra
Vanilen Radhuve Thunindhu,
Thaadhu Cherthol Kanna
Nnaikkuru Koorchchatakopanchonna,
Theethi Laadha Vonthamiz
Kalivai Aayiraththu Lippaththum,
Otha Valla Piraakkal
Nammai Yaalutai Yaargalpande. (2) 9.1.11

Pandainnaa Laale Nindhiru Varulum
Pangayath Thaalthiru Varulum
Kondu,Nnin Koyil Cheeyththuppal Padikaal
Kutikuti Vazivandhaat Cheyyum,
Thondarork Karulich Chothivaay Thirandhun
Thaamaraik Kankalaal Nokkaay,
Thendiraip Porunnal Thanpanai Choozndha
Thirupuling Kutikkitann Thaane! (2) 9.2.1

Kutikitann Thaakkany Cheythunnin Theerththa
Adimaikkur Revalcheythu, Unbon
Adikkata Vaathe Vazivaru Kinra
Adiyarork Karuli,Nnee Yorunnaal
Padikkala Vaaga Nimirththannin Paadha
Pangaya Methalaik Kaniyaay,
Kotikkolpon Mathilchooz Kulirvayal Cholaith
Thirupuling Kutikkitann Thaane! 9.2.2

Kitandhannaal Kitandhaay Eththanai Kaalam
Kitaththiyun Thiruvutam Pachaiya,
Thotarndhukur Ravel Cheythuthol Ladimai
Vazivarum Thondarork Karuli,
Thatandholthaa Maraikkan Viziththunnee Yezundhun
Thaamarai Mangaiyum Neeyum,
Itangolmoo Vulagum Thozavirunn Tharulaay
Thirupuling Kutikkitann Thaane! 9.2.3

Pulikutik Kitandhu Varaguna Mangai
Irundhuvai Kundhaththul Ninru,
Thelindhaven Chindhai Akangazi Yaathe
Ennaiyaal Vaayenak Karuli,
Nalindhachee Rulakam Moonrutan Viyappa
Naangalkooth Thaadinnin Raarppa,
Palingunneer Mukilin Pavalam Pol Kanivaay
Chivappannee Kaanavaa Raaye. 9.2.4

Pavalam Pol Kanivaay Chivappannee Kaana
Vandhunnin Pannilaa Muththam,
Thavazkathir Muruval Cheythunnin Thirukkan
Taamarai Thayangunnin Rarulaay,
Pavalannan Patarkkeezch Changurai Porunal
Thandhirup Pulingutik Kitandhaay,
Kavalamaa Kalirri Nnitarketath Thataththuk
Kaaychinap Paravaiyoornn Thaane! 9.2.5

Kaaychinap Paravai Yoorndhupon Malaiyin
Meemichaik Kaarmukil Pola,
Maachina Maali Maalimaan Enrang
Kavarpatak Kananrumun Nninra,
Kaaychina Vendhe! Kathirmuti Yaane!
Kalivayal Thirupuling Kutiyaay,
Kaaychina Aazi Changuvaal Vilthan
Tendhiyem Itarkadi Vaane! 9.2.6

Emmitar Kadindhing Kennaiyaal Vaane!
Imaiyavar Thamakkumaang Kanaiyaay,
Chemmatal Malarum Thaamaraip Pazanath
Thandhirup Pulingutik Kitandhaay,
Nammutai Yadiyar Kavvaikan Tukandhu
Naamkalith Thulannalam Koora,
Immata Vulakar Kaanannee Yorunnaal
Irundhitaay Engalkan Mukappe. 9.2.7

Engalkan Mukappe Ulakargal Ellaam
Inaiyadi Thozuthezunn Thirainchi
Thangalan Paarath Thamadhuchol Valaththaal
Thalaithalaich Chirandhapoo Chippa,
Thingalcher Maatath Thiruppuling Kutiyaay!
Thiruvaikunn Thaththullaay! Thevaa,
Inganmaa Nyaalath Thithanulu Morunnaal
Irundhitaay Veerritang Konde. 9.2.8

Veerritang Kondu Viyangolmaa Nyaalath
Thithanulu Mirundhitaay, Adiyom
Porriyo Vaathe Kanninai Kulirap
Puthumalar Aagaththaip Paruka,
Cherrila Vaalai Chenneloo Tukalum
Chezumpanaith Thiruppuling Kutiyaay,
Koorramaay Achurar Kulamuthal Arindha
Kotuvinaip Pataigalval Laane! 9.2.9

Kotuvinaip Pataigal Vallaiyaay Amarark
Kitarketa, Achurargat Kitarchey,
Katuvinai Nanche! Ennutai Amuthe!
Kalivayal Thiruppuling Kutiyaay,
Vadivinai Yillaa Malarmakal Marrai
Nilamakal Pitikkummel Ladiyai,
Kotuvinai Yenum Pitikkannee Orunnaal
Koovuthal Varuthalchey Yaaye. 9.2.10

`Koovuthal Varuthal Cheythitaay' Enru
Kuraikatal Kataindhavan Dhannai,
Mevinnan Kamarndha Viyanbunal Porunnal
Vazuthinnaa Tanchata Kopan,
Naaviyal Paatal Aayirath Thullum
Ivaiyumor Paththumval Laargal,
Ovutha Linri Yulakammoon Ralandhaan
Adiyinai Yullaththor Vaare. (2) 9.2.11

Oraa Yiramaay Ulakez Alikkum
Peraa Yiramkon Tathorpee Tutaiyan
Kaaraa Yinakaa Lannanme Nniyinan,
Naaraa Yanannang Kalpiraan Avane. (2) 9.3.1

Avane Akalnyaa Lampataith Thitandhaan,
Avane Yaqadhun Tumizndhaan Alandhaan,
Avane Yavanum Avanum Avanum,
Avane Marrellaa Mumarinn Thaname. 9.3.2

Arindhana Vetha Arumporul Noolkal,
Arindhana Kolka Arumporul Aadhal,
Arindhanar Ellaam Ariyai Vanangi,
Arindhanar Noykal Arukkum Marundhe. 9.3.3

Marundhe Nangal Pokama Kizchchikkenru,
Perundhe Varkuzaang Kalpithar Rumpiraan
Karundheva Nemmaan Kannan Vinnulakam
Tharumthe Vanaicho Relkandaay Maname! 9.3.4

Maname! Unnaival Vinaiyen Irandhu,
Kaname Chollinen Ithucho Relkandaay,
Puname Viyapoonn Thanduzaay Alangal,
Iname Thumilaa Nnaiyatai Vadhume. 9.3.5

Ataiva Thumani Yaarmalar Mangaithol,
Mitaiva Thumachu Rarkkuvem Porgale,
Kataiva Thumkata Lulamuthu, Enmanam
Utaiva Thumavar Keyorung Kaagave. 9.3.6

Aagam Chernnara Chingama Thaaki,Or
Aagang Valluki Raalpilann Thaanurai,
Maaga Vaikundham Kaanpadharku, Enmanam
Eka Mennum Iraappaka Linriye. 9.3.7

Inrip Poka Iruvinai Yumketuththu,
Onri Yaakkai Pukaamaiyuy Yakkolvaan,
Ninra Vengatam Neenilath Thulladhu,
Chenru Thevargal Kaithozu Vaargale. 9.3.8

Thozuthu Maamalar Neerchutar Thoopamkondu,
Ezuthu Mennum Ithumikai Yaadhalil,
Pazuthil Tholpukazp Paampanaip Palliyaay,
Thazuvu Maarari Yenuna Thaalkale. 9.3.9

Thaala Thaamarai Yaanuna Thundhiyaan,
Vaalkol Neelmazu Vaaliyun Aagaththaan,
Aala Raayththozu Vaarum Amarargal,
Naalum Enbukaz Kovuna Cheelame? 9.3.10

Cheela Mellaiyi Laanadi Mel,Ani
Kola Neelkuru Koorchchata Kopanchol,
Maalai Yaayirath Thullivai Paththinin
Paalar, Vaikundha Meruthal Paanmaiye. (2) 9.3.11

Maiyaar Karunganni Kamala Malarmel
Cheyyaal, Thirumaar Vinilcher Thirumaale,
Veyyaar Chutaraazi Churichanga Mendhum
Kaiyaa, Unaikkaanak Karuthumen Kanne. 9.4.1

Kanne Yunaikkaanak Karuthi,En Nnencham
Enne Konda Chindhaiyadhaay Ninriyampum,
Vinnor Munivark Kenrumkaan Pariyaayai,
Nannaa Thoziye Nnenrunnaan Azaippane. 9.4.2

Azaikkinra Vadinnaayen Naaykoozai Vaalaal,
Kuzaikkin Radhupol Ennullam Kuzaiyum,
Mazaikkanru Kunrametuththa Thaannirai Kaaththaay,
Pizaikkinra Tharulenru Pethuru Vene. 9.4.3

Uruvathithu Venrunak Kaatpattu, Ninkan
Peruva Thethukolenru Pethaiyen Nencham,
Marukalcheyyum Vaanavar Thaanavark Kenrum,
Ariva Thariya Ariyaaya Ammaane! 9.4.4

Ariyaaya Ammaanai Amarar Piraanai,
Periyaanaip Piramanai Munbataith Thaanai,
Varivaal Aravin Anaippalli Kolkinra,
Kariyaan Kazalkaanak Karuthum Karuththe. 9.4.5

Karuththe Yunaikkaanak Karuthi,En Nnenchath
Thiruththaaga Iruththinen Thevargat Kellaam
Viruththaa, Vilangum Chutarchchothi Yuyarath
Thoruththaa, Unaiyullum Ennullam Ukandhe. 9.4.6

Ukandhe Yunaiyullu Mennullaththu, Akampaal
Akandhaan Amarndhe Yitangonda Amalaa,
Mikundhaana Vanmaar Vakalam Irukooraa
Nakandhaay, Naraching Kamadhaaya Vuruve! 9.4.7

Uruvaa Kiyaaaru Chamayangat Kellaam,
Poruvaaki Ninraan Avanellaap Porutkum,
Aruvaakiya Aathiyaith Thevargat Kellaam,
Karuvaakiya Kannanaik Kandukon Tene. 9.4.8

Kandukon Tenekan Ninaiyaarak Kaliththu,
Pandai Vinaiyaayina Parro Taruththu,
Thondark Kamuthunnach Chonmaalaigal Chonnen,
Andath Thamarar Perumaan! Adiyene. 9.4.9

Adiyaa Nnivanen Renakkaa Rarulcheyyum
Netiyaanai, Niraipukaz Anchiraip Pullin
Kotiyaanai, Kunraamal Ulakam Alandha
Adiyaanai, Ataindhadi Yenuyndha Vaare. 9.4.10

Aara Madhayaanai Atarththavan Dhannai,
Cheraar Vayalthen Kurukoorch Chatakopan,
Noore Chonnavo Raayiraththu Lippaththum,
ERE Tharumvaa Nnavarthamin Nnuyirkke. (2) 9.4.11

Innuyirch Chevalum Neerum
Koovikkonduing Keththanai,
Ennuyir Nova Mazirren
Minkuyil Petaikaal,
Ennuyirk Kanna Piraanai
Neervarak Koovukileer,
Ennuyirk Koovik Kotuppaarkkum
Iththanai Vendumo? (2) 9.5.1

Iththanai Venduva Thanrandho!
Anril Petaikaal,
Eththanai Neerum Nunche
Valumkarainn Thenguthir,
Viththakan Kovindhan Meyya
Nnalla Nnoruvarkkum,
Aththanai Yaamini Yennu
Yiravan Kaiyathe. 9.5.2

Avankaiya Theyena Thaaruyir
Anril Petaikaal,
Evancholli Neerkutainn Thaatu
Thirputai Choozave,
Thavamchey Thillaa Vinaiyaatti
Yenuyi Ringundo,
Evancholli Nirrumnnum Engu
Kookkural Kettume. 9.5.3

Kookkural Kettum Nam Kannan
Maayan Velippataan,
Merkilai Kollenmin Neerum
Chevalum Kozikaal,
Vaakkum Manamum Karuma
Mumnnamak Kaangathe,
Aakkaiyu Maaviyum Andharam
Ninru Zalume. 9.5.4

Andharam Ninruzal Kinra
Yaanutaip Poovaikaal,
Nundhirath Thethu Mitaiyil
Laikuza Renmino,
Indhira Nyaalangal Kaattiyiv
Vezula Kumkonda,
Nandhiru Maarban Nammaavi
Yunnannan Kenninaan. 9.5.5

Nankenni Naanva Larththa
Chirukilip Paithale,
Inkural Neemizir Relen
Nnaaruyirk Kaaguththan,
Nincheyya Vaayokkum Vaayangan
Nangai Kaalinan,
Ninbachuny Chaama Niraththan
Koottundu Neenginaan. 9.5.6

Koottundu Neengi Kolath
Thaamaraik Katchevvaay,
Vaattami Lengaru Maanikkam
Kannan Maayanbol,
Kottiya Villotu Minnum
Mekak Kuzaangalkaal,
Kaatten Minnum Muruen
Nnuyirkkadhu Kaalane. 9.5.7

Uyirkkadhu Kaalanen Rummai
Yaanirann Therku,Nneer
Kuyirpaithal Kaal!Kannan Naama
Mekuza Rikkonreer,
Thayirppa Zanchor Rotupaa
Ladichilum Thandhu,Chol
Payirriya Nalvala Moottineer
Panputai Yeere! 9.5.8

Panputai Vandotu Thumpikaal!
Panmizar Renmin,
Punpurai Velkotu Kuththaalok
Kumnnum Inkural,
Thanperu Neerththatann Thaamarai
Malarndhaa Lokkum
Kanperung Kannan, Nammaavi
Yundeza Nanninaan. 9.5.9

Ezannanni Naamum Namvaana
Naatano Tonrinom,
Pazanannan Nnaaraik Kuzaangal
Kaal!Payin Rennini,
Izainnalla Vaakkai Yumpaiya
Vepuyak Karradhu,
Thazainnalla Inbam Thalaippey
Thengum Thazaikkave. 9.5.10

Inbam Thalaippey Thengum
Thazaiththapal Loozikku,
Thanpuka Zeththath Thanakkarul
Cheytha Maayanai,
Thenguru Koorchchata Kopanchol
Laayirath Thullivai,
Onbatho Tonruk Kummoo
Vulagu Murukume. (2) 9.5.11

Urukumaal Chencham Uyirin Paramanri,
Perukumaal Vetkaiyum Encheyken Thondanen,
Theruvellaam Kaavi Kamazthiruk Kaatkarai,
Maruviya Maayandhan Maayam Ninaithore. (2) 9.6.1

Ninaithorum Chollunn Thorumnneny Chitindhukum
Vinaikolcheer Paadilum Vemena Thaaruyir,
Chunaikolpoony Cholaiththen Kaatkarai Yennappaa,
Ninaikilen Naanunak Kaatcheyyum Neermaiye. 9.6.2

Neermaiyaal Nencham Vanchiththup Pukundhu,Ennai
Eermaichey Thennuyi Raayen Nnuyirundaan,
Cheermalku Cholaiththen Kaatkarai Yennappan,
Kaarmukil Vannandhan Kalvam Arikilen. 9.6.3

Arikilen Thannul Anaiththulakam Nirka,
Nerimaiyaal Thaanum Avarrulnnir Kumpiraan,
Verikamaz Cholaiththen Kaatkarai Ennappan,
Chiriyaven Nnaaruyi Runda Thiruvarule. 9.6.4

Thiruvarul Cheypavan Polaven Nnulpukundhu,
Uruvamum Aaruyirum Utane Yundaan,
Thiruvalar Cholaiththen Kaatkarai Yennappan,
Karuvalar Menien Kannangal Vangale. 9.6.5

Engannan Kalvam Enakkuchchem Maaynnirkum,
Anganna Nnundaven Nnaaruyirk Kothithu,
Punganmai Yeythip Pulampi Yiraappakal,
Enganna Nnenravan Kaatkarai Yeththume. 9.6.6

Kaatkarai Yeththum Adhanulkan Naavennum,
Vetkainnoy Koora Ninaindhu Karaindhukum,
Aatkol Vaanoththen Nnuyirunda Maayanaal,
Kotkurai Pattathen Nnaaruyir Kolunde. 9.6.7

Kolundaan Anrivann Thennuyir Thaanundaan,
Naalunnaal Vandhennai Murravum Thaanundaan,
Kaalanneer Mekaththen Kaatkarai Yennapparku,
Aalanre Pattathen Aaruyir Pattathe. 9.6.8

Aaruyir Patta Thenadhuyir Pattadhu,
Perithaz Thaamaraik Kankani Vaayathor,
Kaarezil Mekaththen Kaatkarai Koyilkol,
Cheerezil Naalthatann Tholtheyva Vaarikke. 9.6.9

`Vaarikkon Tunnai Vizunguvan Kaanil'enru
Aarvurra Ennai Yoziyaven Nnilmunnam
Paariththu, Thaanennai Murrap Parukinaan,
Kaarokkum Kaatkarai Yennappan Kadiyane. 9.6.10

Kadiyanaayk Kanchanaik Konra Piraandhannai,
Kotimathil Thenguru Koorchchata Kopanchol,
Vadivamai Yaayirath Thippaththi Nnaal,Chanmam
Mutiveythi Naachangan Teergaleng Kaanale. (2) 9.6.11

Engaanal Akangazivaay
Iraiththerndhing Kinithamarum,
Chengaala Matannaaraay!
Thirumoozik Kalaththuraiyum,
Kongaarpoonn Thuzaaymutiyeng
Kutakkooththark Kendhoothaay,
Nungaalka Len Dhalaimel
Kezumeero Numarote. (2) 9.7.1

Numarotum Piriyaathe
Neerumnnum Chevalumaay,
Amarkaadhal Kurukinangaal!
Animoozik Kalaththuraiyum,
Emaraalum Pazippunding
Ken?Thammaal Izippundu,
Thamarotang Kuraivaarkkuth
Thakkilame! Keleere. 9.7.2

Thakkilame Keleergal
Thatampunalvaay Iraitherum,
Kokkinangaal! Kurukinangaal!
Kulirmoozik Kalaththuraiyum,
Chekkamalath Thalarpolum
Kankaikaal Chenganivaay,
Akkamalath Thilaipolum
Thirumeni Yadigalukke. 9.7.3

Thirumeni Yadigalukku
Theevinaiyen Vituthoothaay:
Thirumoozik Kalamennum
Chezunnakarvaay Animukilkaal,
Thirumeni Yavatkaruleer
Enrakkaal, Ummaiththan
Thirumeni Yoliyakarrith
Thelivichumpu Kadiyume? 9.7.4

Thelivichumpu Kadithotith
Theevalaiththu Minnilagum,
Olimukilkaal! Thirumoozik
Kalaththuraiyum Onchutarkku,
Thelivichumpu Thirunnaataath
Theevinaiyen Manaththuraiyum,
Thulivaargat Kuzalaarkken
Thoothuraiththal Cheppamine. 9.7.5

Thoothuraiththal Cheppumingal
Thoomoziyaay Vandinangaal,
Pothiraiththu Madhunnukarum
Pozilmoozik Kalaththuraiyum,
Maadharaiththam Maarvakaththe
Vaiththaarkken Vaaymaarram,
Thoothuraiththal Chepputhirel
Chutarvaluyum Kalaiyume. 9.7.6

Chutarvaluyum Kalaiyungondu
Aruvinaiyen Tholthurandha,
Patarpukazaan Thirumoozik
Kalaththuraiyum Pangayakkat,
Chutarpavala Vaayanaikkadu
Orunnaalor Thooymaarram,
Patarpozilvaayk Kurukinangaal!
Enakkonru Paniyeere. 9.7.7

Enakkonru Paniyeergal
Irumpozilvaay Iraitherndhu,
Manakkinbam Patamevum
Vandinangaal! Thumpikaal,
Kanakkolthin Mathilputaichooz
Thirumoozik Kalaththuraiyum,
Punalkolkaa Yaamenip
Poondhuzaay Mutiyaarkke. 9.7.8

Poondhuzaay Mutiyaarkkup
Ponnaazi Kaiyaarkku,
Endhunnee Rilanguruke!
Thirumoozik Kalaththaarkku,
Endhupoon Mulaippayandhen
Inaimalarkkan Neerthadhumpa,
Thaamthammaik Kondakalthal
Thakavanren Ruraiyeere. 9.7.9

Thakavanren Ruraiyeergal
Thatampunalvaay Iraitherndhu,
Mikavinbam Patamevum
Mennataiya Annangaal,
Mikameni Meliveythi
Mekalaiyum Eetazindhu,En
Akameni Yoziyaame
Thirumoozik Kalaththaarkke. 9.7.10

Ozivinrith Thirumoozik
Kalaththuraiyum Onchutarai,
Ozivillaa Animazalaik
Kilimoziyaal Alarriyachol,
Vazuvillaa Vankurukoorch
Chatakopan Vaayndhuraiththa,
Azivillaa Aayiraththip
Paththumnnoy Arukkume. (2) 9.7.11

Arukkum Vinaiyaa Yina Aagaththavanai,
Niruththam Manaththon Riyachinn Thaiyinaarkku,
Veriththan Malarcho Laigalchuz Thirunnaavaay,
Kurukkum Vakaiyundu Kolokoti Yerke? (2) 9.8.1

Kotiye Ritaikko Kanakath Thavalkelvan,
Vadivel Thatangan Matappinnai Manaalan,
Netiyaa Nnuraicho Laigalchooz Thirunnaavaay,
Adiyen Anukap Peru Naal Evaikolo! 9.8.2

`Evaikol Anukap Perunnaal?'En Reppothum,
Kavaiyil Manaminrik Kanneergal Kaluzvan,
Navaiyil Thirunnaaranancher Thirunnaavaay,,
Avaiyul Pukalaava Thornnaal Ariyene. 9.8.3

Naalel Ariyen Enakkul Lana,Nnaanum
Meelaa Adimaip Panicheyyap Pukundhen,
Neelaar Malarcho Laigalchuz Thirunnaavaay,
Vaaley Thatangan Matappinnai Manaalaa! 9.8.4

Manaalan Malarmang Kaikkumman Matandhaikkum,
Kannaalan Ulakath Thuyirthevar Katkellaam,
Vinnaalan Virumpi Yuraiyum Thirunnaavaay,
Kannaarak Kalikkinra Thingenru Kolkande? 9.8.5

Kande Kalikkinra Thingenru Kolkankal,
Thonde Yunakkaa Yozindhaan Thurichinri,
Vandaar Malarcho Laigalchuz Thirunnaavaay,
Konde Yuraikinra Engo Valarkove! 9.8.6

Kovaa Kiyamaa Valiyai Nilangondaay,
Thevaa Churamcher Ravane! Thirumaale,
Naavaa Yuraikinra Ennaa Ranannampee,
`Aavaa Adiyaa Nnivan'en Rarulaaye. 9.8.7

Arulaa Thozivaay Arulcheythu, Adiyenaip
Porulaakki Yunbon Nnadikkeezp Pukavaippaay,
Marule Yinriunnai Ennenchath Thiruththum,
Therule Tharuthen Thirunnaavaay Endheve! 9.8.8

Thevar Munivark Kenrumkaan Tarkariyan,
Moovar Muthalvan Orumoo Vulakaali,
Thevan Virumpi Yuraiyum Thirunnaavaay,
Yaavar Anukap Peruvaar Iniyandho! 9.8.9

Andho! Anukap Perunnaalen Reppothum,
Chindhai Kalangith Thirumaalen Razaippan,
Kondhaar Malarcho Laigalchuz Thirunnaavaay,
Vandhe Yuraikinra Emmaa Manivannaa! 9.8.10

Vannam Manimaata Nannaavaay Ullanai,
Thinnam Mathilthen Kurukoorch Chatakopan,
Pannar Thamizaa Yiraththippath Thumvallaar,
Mannaandu Manamkamaz Varmallikaiye. (2) 9.8.11

Mallikai Kamazthenral Iru Maalo!
Vankuriny Chiyichai Thavazu Maalo,
Chelkathir Maalaiyum Mayakku Maalo!
Chekkarnnan Mekangal Chithaikku Maalo,
Alliyann Thaamaraik Kannan Emmaan
Aayargal Erari Yerem Maayon,
Pulliya Mulaigalum Tholum Kondu
Pukalitam Arikilam Thamiya Maalo! (2) 9.9.1

Pukalitam Arikilam Thamiya Maalo!
Pulampurum Anithenral Aampa Laalo,
Pakalatu Maalaivan Chaandha Maalo!
Panchamam Mullaithan Vaatai Yaalo,
Akalitam Pataiththitann Thundu Mizndhu
Alandhengum Alikkinra Aayan Maayon,
Ikalitath Thachurargal Koorram Vaaraan
Iniyirunn Thennuyir Kaakku Maaren? 9.9.2

Iniyirunn Thennuyir Kaakku Maaren
Inaimulai Namukannun Nitainnu Tanga,
Thuniyirung Kalavichey Thaagam Thoyndhu
Thurandhemmai Yittakal Kannan Kalvan,
Thaniyilany Chingamem Maayan Vaaraan
Thaamaraik Kannumchev Vaayum,Nneelap
Paniyirung Kuzalkalum Naangu Tholum
Paaviyen Manaththennin Reeru Maalo! 9.9.3

Paaviyen Manaththennin Reeru Maalo!
Vaataithan Vaataivev Vaatai Yaalo,
Mevuthan Mathiyamvem Mathiya Maalo!
Menmalarp Pallivem Palli Yaalo,
Thooviyam Pullutaith Theyva Vandu
Thuthaindhaem Penmaiyam Poovi Thaalo,
Aaviyim Paramalla Akaika Laalo!
Yaamutai Nenchamum Thunaiyan Raalo! 9.9.4

Yaamutai Nenchamum Thunaiyan Raalo!
Aapukum Maalaiyum Aakin Raalo,
Yaamudai Aayandhan Manamkal Laalo!
Avanutaith Theenguza Leeru Maalo,
Yaamutai Thunaiyennum Thozi Maarum
Emminmun Nnavanukku Maayva Raalo,
Yaamutai Aaruyir Kaakku Maaren?
Avanutai Yarulpe Rumpothu Arithe. 9.9.5

Avanutai Yarulpe Rumpo Tharithaal
Avvarul Allana Arulum Alla,
Avanarul Perumala Vaavi Nillaadhu
Atupakal Maalaiyum Nenchum Kaanen:
Chivanotu Piramanvan Thiruma Tandhai
Cherthiru Vaagamem Maavi Yeerum,
Evaninip Pukumitam? Evanchey Keno?
Aarukken Cholluken Annai Meergaal! 9.9.6

Aarukken Cholluken Annai Meergaal!
Aaruyir Alavu Anru Ikkoorthan Vaatai,
Kaarokkum Meninnang Kannan Kalvam
Kavarndhavath Thaninnencham Avanga Naqathe,
Cheerurra Akirpukai Yaaznna Rampu
Panchamam Thanpachuny Chaandha Naindhu,
Porurra Vaataithan Malli Kaippoop
Puthumanam Mukandhukon Teriyu Maalo! 9.9.7

Puthumanam Mukandhukon Teriyu Maalo!
Pongila Vaataipun Chekka Raalo,
Adhumanann Thakanrannang Kannan Kalvam
Kanninir Kotithini Adhani Lumpar,
Madhumana Mallikai Mandhak Kovai
Vanpachuny Chaandhinil Pancha Mamvaiththu,
Adhumanann Thinnarul Aaychchi Yarkke
Oothumath Theenguzar Keyuy Yennaan! 9.9.8

Oothumath Theenguzar Keyuy Yennaan!
Adhumozinn Thitaiyitaith Thanchey Kolath,
Thoothuchey Kankalkon Tonru Pechith
Thoomozi Yichaigalkon Tonru Nokki,
Pethurum Mukamcheythu Nondhu Nondhu
Pethainneny Charavarap Paatum Paattai,
Yaadhumon Rarikilam Amma Amma!
Maalaiyum Vandhadhu Maayan Vaaraan. 9.9.9

Maalaiyum Vandhadhu Maayan Vaaraan
Maamani Pulampal Lera Naindha,
Kolannan Nnaagukal Ukalu Maalo!
Kotiyena Kuzalkalum Kuzarumaalo,
Vaaloli Valarmullai Karumu Kaigal
Mallikai Yalampivan Taalu Maalo,
Velaiyum Vichampilvin Talaru Maalo!
Encholli Yuyvaning Kavanai Vitte? 9.9.10

Avanaivit Takanruyir Aarra Killaa
Aniyizai Aaychchiyar Maalaip Poochal,
Avanaivit Takalvadhar Keyi Rangi
Anikuru Koorchchata Kopan Maaran,
Avaniyun Tumizndhavan Melu Raiththa
Aayirath Thullivai Paththum Kondu,
Avaniyul Alarrinnin Ruymmin Thondeer!
Achchonna Maalai Nannith Thozuthe! (2) 9.9.11

Maalainnan Niththozu Thezumino Vinaiketa,
Kaalaimaa Laikama Lamalar Ittunneer,
Velaimo Thummathil Choozthiruk Kannapuraththu,
Aalinme Laalamarnn Thaanadi Yinaigale. (2) 9.10.1

Kallavi Zummalar Ittunnee Rirainchumin,
Nalliche Rumvayal Choozkitang Kinbutai,
Velleeyeynn Thamathil Choozthiruk Kannapuram
Ulli,Nnaa Lumthozu Thezumino Thondare! 9.10.2

Thondar!Nnunn Thandhuyar Pokanneer Ekamaay,
Vinduvaa Taamalar Ittunnee Rirainchumin,
Vandupaa Tumpozil Choozthiruk Kanpurath
Thandavaa Nan,Ama Rarperu Maanaiye. 9.10.3

Maanainnok Kimatap Pinnaithan Kelvanai,
Thenaivaa Taamalar Ittunnee Rirainchumin,
Vaanaiyunn Thummathil Choozthiruk Kannapuram,
Thaan Nayann Thaperu Maan Chara Naagume. 9.10.4

Charanamaa Kumthana Thaalatainn Thaarkkelaam,
Maranamaa Nnaalvaikunn Thamkotuk Kumpiraan,
Aranamainn Thamathil Choozthiruk Kannapuram,
Tharaniyaa Lan,Thana Thanbarkkan Paagume. 9.10.5

Anbanaa Kumthana Thaalatainn Thaarkkelaam,
Chemponaa Kaththavu Nanutal Keendavan,
Nanboneynn Thamathil Choozthiruk Kannapurath
Thanban,Nnaa Lumthan Meyyarkku Meyyane. 9.10.6

Meyyanaa Kumvirum Piththozu Vaarkkelaam,
Poyyanaa Kumpura Methozu Vaarkkelaam,
Cheyyilvaa Laiyuka Lumthiruk Kannapuraththu
Aiyan,Aa Kaththanaip Paargat Kaniyane. 9.10.7

Aniyanaa Kumthana Thaalatainn Thaarkkelaam,
Piniyum Chaaraa Piravi Ketuththaalum,
Maniponeynn Thamathil Choozthiruk Kannapuram
Panimin,Nnaa Lumpara Mettithan Paadhame. 9.10.8

Paadhannaa Lumpani Yaththani Yumpini,
Ethamchaa Raaenak Kelini Yengurai?,
Vetha Varvirum Pumthiruk Kannapuraththu
Aathiyaa Nnai,Atainn Thaarkkallal Illaiye. 9.10.9

Illaiyal Lalenak Kelini Yengurai?,
Allimaa Tharama Rumthiru Maarbinan,
Kallileynn Thamathil Choozthiruk Kannapuram
Cholla,Nnaa Lumthuyar Paatuchaa Raave. 9.10.10

Paatuchaa Raavinai Parrara Venduveer,
Maatannee Tukuru Koorchchata Kopanchol,
Paatalaa Nnadhamiz Aayiraththu Lippaththum
Paadiyaa Tip,Pani Minavan Thaalkale. (2) 9.10.11


Patthaam Patthu

Thaala Thaamaraith Thadamani Vayal Thiru Mogoor
Naalum Mevinan Kamarndhunin Rachuraraith Thakarkkum
Tholum Naangudaich Surikuzal Kamalakkan Kanivaay
Kaala Mekaththai Yan Rimar Ron Rilam Kathiye. (2) 10.1.1

Ilangathi Marron Remmaikkum Eendhan Thuzaayin
Alangalang Kanni Aayiram Perudai Ammaan
Nalangol Naanmarai Vaanargal Vaazthiru Mogoor
Nalanga Zalavan Adinizal Thadamanri Yaame. 10.1.2

Anri Yaamoru Pukalidam Ilam Enren Ralarri
Ninru Naanmukan Aranotu Thevargal Naada
Venrim Moovula Kaliththuzal Vaandhiru Mogoor
Nanru Naamini Nanukuthum Namathidar Ketave. 10.1.3

Idarketa Emmaip Pondhali Yaay Enren Reththi
Chudargol Sothiyaith Thevarum Munivarum Thotara
Padargol Paampanaip Pallikol Vaandhiru Mogoor
Idarke Tavadi Paravuthum Thondeer! Vammine. 10.1.4

Thondeer! Vamminnam Sudaroli Yoruthani Muthalvan
Anda Moovula Kalandhavan Anithiru Mogoor
Endi Saiyumeen Karumpotu Porunchennel Vilaiya
Konda Koyilai Valancheything Kaaduthum Kooththe. 10.1.5

Kooththan Kovalan Kutharruval Lachurargal Koorram
Eththum Nangadakum Amararkkum Munivarkkum Inban
Vaayththa Thanpanai Valavayal Soozthiru Mogoor
Aaththan Thaamarai Yadiyanri Marrilam Arane. 10.1.6

Marri Lamaran Vaanberum Paazthani Muthalaa
Churru Neerpadaith Thathanvazith Thonmuni Muthalaa
Murrum Thevaro Tulakuchey Vaandhiru Mogoor
Churri Naamvalany Seyyanam Thuyarketum Kadithe. 10.1.7

Thuyarke Tumkadi Thadaindhuvan Thadiyavar Thozumin
Uyarkol Solaiyon Thadamani Yolithiru Mogoor
Peyargal Aayira Mudaiyaval Larakkarpuk Kazundha
Thayaradhan Perra Marathaka Maniththadath Thinaiye. 10.1.8

Maniththa Taththadi Malarkkankal Pavalach Sevvaay
Anikakol Naalthadan Tholtheyvam Achurarai Yenrum
Thunikkum Vallarat Tanurai Pozilthiru Mogoor
Naniththu Nammudai Nallaran Naamadain Thaname. 10.1.9

Naama Taindhanal Laranthamak Kenrunal Lamarar
Theemai Seyyumval Lachurarai Yanchichchen Radaindhaal
Kaama Roopamkon Tezundhalip Paandhiru Mogoor
Naama Menavin Rennumin Eththumin Namargaal! 10.1.10.

Eththu Minnamar Kaal Enru Thaanguda Maadu
Kooththanai Kuru Koorchchada Kopangur Reval
Vaayththa Aayirath Thullivai Vanthiru Mogoorkku
Eeththa Paththivai Yeththaval Laarkkidar Ketume. (2) 10.1.11

Ketumida Raayavellaam Kechavaa Venna Nnaalum
Kotuvinai Seyyumkoorrin Thamargalum Kurukakillaar
Vidamudai Yaravilpalli Virumpinaan Surumpalarrum
Thadamudai Vayal Anandhapuranagarp Pukuthuminre. (2) 10.2.1

Inrupoyp Pukuthiraaki Lezumaiyum Ethamchaara
Kunruner Maadamaate Kurundhucher Serundhipunnai
Manralar Pozil Anandhapuranagar Maayannaamam
Onrumo Raayiramaam Ulluvaark Kumparoore. 10.2.2

Oorumput Kodiyum Aqthe Ulakollaamundumizndhaan
Cherumthan Nanandhapuram Sikkenap Pukuthiraakil
Theerumnoyvinaikalellaam Thinnanaam Ariyachchonnom
Perum Oraayiraththul Onruneer Pechumine. 10.2.3

Pechumin Koochaminrip Periyaneer Velaichoozndhu
Vaachame Kamazuncholai Vayal Aniyanandhapuram
Nechamchey Thuraikinraanai Nerimaiyaal Malargalthoovi
Poochanai Seykinraargal Punniyam Seythavaare. 10.2.4

Punniyam Seythunalla Punalotu Malargalthoovi
Ennumi Nnendhainaamam Ippirap Parukkumappaal
Thinnamnaam Ariyachchonnom Seripozil Anandhapuraththu
Annalaar Kamalapaatham Anukuvaar Amararaavaar. 10.2.5

Amararaayth Thirikinraargatku Aathichera Anandhapuraththu
Amararkon Archchikkinrang Kakappani Seyvarvinnor
Namargalo! Sollakkenmin Naamumpoy Nanukavendum
Kumaranaar Thaathaithunbam Thudaiththako Vindhanaare. 10.2.6

Thudaiththako Vindhanaare Yulakuyir Thevummarrum
Padaiththavem Paramamoorththi Paampanaip Pallikondaan
Madaiththalai Vaalaipaayum Vayalaniyanandhapuram
Kadaiththalai Seeykkapperraal Kaduvinai Kalaiyalaame. 10.2.7

Kaduvinai Kalaiyalaakum Kaamanaip Payandhakaalai
Idavakai Kondathenbar Ezilaniyanandhapuram
Padamudai Yaravilpalli Payinravan Paathamkaana
Nadamino Namargalulleer! Naamumak Kariyachchonnom. 10.2.8

Naamumak Kariyachchonna Naalkalum Naniyavaana
Chemam Nangudaiththukkandeer Seripozilanandhapuram
Thoomanal Viraimalargal Thuvalara Aayndhukondu
Vaamanan Adikkenreththa Maayndharum Vinaikalthaame. 10.2.9

Maayndharum Vinaikalthaame Maathavaa Enna Naalum
Eyndhapon Mathilanandhapura Nagarendhaikkenru
Chaandhotu Vilakkamthoopam Thaamarai Malargalnalla
Aayndhukon Teththavallaar Andhamil Pukazinaare. 10.2.10.

Andhamil Pukazanandhapura Nagar Aathithannai
Kondhalar Pozilkurukoor Maaran Chol Laayiraththul
Aindhino Taindhumvallaar Anaivarpoy Amarulakil
Paindhodi Madandhaiyartham Veymaru Tholinaiye. (2) 10.2.11

Veymaru Tholinai Meliyu Maalo!
Melivumen Thanimaiyum Yaathum Nokkaa
Kaamaru Kuyilkalum Koovu Maalo!
Kanamayil Avaikalandhaalu Maalo
Aamaru Vinanirai Meykka Neepokku
Orupaka Laayira Moozi Yaalo
Thaamaraik Kankalkodu Eerdhi Yaalo!
Thakavilai Thakavilaiye Nee Kannaa! (2) 10.3.1

Thakavilai Thakavilai Yenee Kannaa!
Thadamulai Punar Thorum Punarchchik Kaaraa
Chukavellam Visumpirandhu Arivai Moozkkach
Soozndhathu Kanavena Neengi Yaange
Agavuyir Agamathandhorum Ulpukku
Aaviyin Paramalla Vetkai Yandho
Mikamika Iniyunnaip Pirivai Yaamaal
Veeva Nin Pachunirai Meykkap Pokke. 10.3.2

Veevannin Pachunirai Meykkap Pokku
Vevvuyir Kondena Thaavi Vemaal
Yaavarum Thunaiyillai Yaani Rundhun
Anchana Meniyai Yaattam Kaanen
Povathan Rorupakal Neeya Kanraal
Porukayar Kanninai Neerum Nillaa
Chaavathiv Vaaykkulath Kaaychchi Yomaayp
Pirandhavith Thozuththaiyom Thanimai Thaane. 10.3.3

Thozuththaiyom Thanimaiyum Thunaipi Rindhaar
Thuyaramum Ninaikilai Kovin Thaa Nin
Thozuththanil Pachukkalai Yevi Rumpith
Thurandhemmaiyittu Avai Meykkap Pothi
Pazuththanal Lamuthinin Saarru Vellam
Paaviyen Manamakan Thoru Mulpukku
Azuththa Nin Sengani Vaayin Kalvap
Panimozi Ninai Thorum Aavi Vemaal. 10.3.4

Panimozi Ninaithorum Aavi Vemaal
Pakalnirai Meykkiya Poya Kannaa
Piniyaviz Mallikai Vaadai Thoovap
Perumatha Maalaiyum Vandhin Raalo
Manimiku Maarvinil Mullaip Pothen
Vanamulai Kamazviththun Vaayamu Thamdhandhu
Animiku Thaamaraik Kaiyai Yandho!
Adichchi Yomdhalai Michainee Yaniyaay. 10.3.5

Adichchi Yomdhalai Michainee Yaniyaay
Aaziyang Kannaa! Un Kolap Paatham
Pidiththathu Naduvunak Karivaiyarum
Palarathu Nirkavem Penmai Yaarrom
Vadiththadang Kanninai Neerum Nillaa
Manamumnil Laavemak Kathuthan Nnaale
Vedippunin Pasu Nirai Meykkap Pokku
Vem Emadhu Uyir Azal Mezukil Ukke. 10.3.6

Vem Emadhuir Azal Mezukil Ukku
Velvalai Mekalai Kazanru Veeza
Thoomalark Kanninai Muththam Sorath
Thoonaimulai Payandhu Ena Tholkal Vaada
Maamani Vannaa Unsengamala
Vannamen Malaradi Nova Neepoy
Aamakizn Thukandhavai Meykkin Runnodu
Achurargal Thalaippeyyil Evangol Aange? 10.3.7

Asurargal Thalaippeyyil Evango Laangenru
Aazumen Nnaaruyir Aanbin Pokel
Kachikaiyum Vetkaiyum Ulka Landhu
Kalaviyum Naliyumen Kaikazi Yel
Vachicheyun Thaamaraik Kannum Vaayum
Kaikalum Peethaka Vudaiyum Kaatti
Ochicheynun Nidaiyila Aaychchi Yarnee
Ukakkunal Lavarotum Uzitha Raaye. 10.3.8

Ukakkunal Lavarotum Uzithan Thundhan
Thiruvullam Idarketun Thorum Naangal
Viyakka Inburudhum Empenmai Yaarrom
Emperu Maan! Pachu Meykkap Pokel
Mithappala Achurargal Vendum Uruvang
Kondunin Ruzitharuvar Kancha Nneva
Akappadil Avarotum Ninno Taange
Avaththangal Vilaiyumen Sorkol Andho! 10.3.9

Avaththangal Vilaiyumen Sorkol Andho!
Achurargal Vangaiyar Kancha Nnevath
Thavaththavar Maruga Ninruzi Tharuvar
Thanimaiyum Perithunakku Iraamanaiyum
Uvarththalai Udandhiri Kilaiyu Menrenru
Oodura Vennudai Yaavivemaal
Thivaththilum Pachunirai Meyppu Vaththi
Sengani Vaayengal Aayar Theve! 10.3.10.

Chengani Vaayengal Aayar Thevu
Aththiruvadi Thiruvadi Mel Po Runal
Changani Thuraivan Vanthen Kurukoor
Vanchada Kopanchol Laayi Raththul
Mangaiya Raaychchiya Raayndha Maalai
Avanotum Pirivathar Kirangi Thaiyal
Angavan Pachunirai Meyppo Zippaan
Uraiththana Ivaiyumpath Thavarrin Saarve. (2) 10.3.11

Saarvedhava Nerikkuth Thaamodharan Dhaalthal,
Kaarmeka Vannan Kamala Nayanaththan,
Neervaanam Mannerikaa Laayninra Nemiyaan,
Pervaa Nnavargal Pitharrum Perumaiyane. (2) 10.4.1

Perumaiyane Vaanath Thimaiyorkkum Kaandar
Karumaiyane Aakath Thanaiyaathaarkku Enrum
Thirumey Yuraikinra Senganmaal Naalum
Irumai Vinaikadindhingu Ennaiyaal Kinraane. 10.4.2

Aalkinraa Nnaaziyaan Aaraal Kuraivudaiyam?
Meelkinra Thillaip Piravith Thuyarkadindhom,
Vaalkendaiyonkan Madappinnai Than Gelvan,
Thaalkandu Kondu En Thalaimel Punaindhene. 10.4.3

Thalaimel Punaindhen Saranangal Aalin
Ilaimel Thuyinraan Imaiyor Vananga
Malaimelthaan Ninren Manaththu Lirundhaanai
Nilaiperkka Laakaamai Nichchith Thirundhene. 10.4.4

Nichchith Thirundhenen Nencham Kaziyaamai
Kaichchak Karaththannal Kalvam Perithudaiyan
Mechchap Padaanbirarkku Meypolum Poyvallan
Nachchap Padumnamakku Naakath Thanaiyaane. 10.4.5

Naakath Thanaiyaanai Naalthorum Nyaanaththaal
Aakath Thanaippaarkku Arulcheyyum Ammaanai
Maakath Thila Mathiyam Serum Sadaiyaanai
Paakaththu Vaiththaan Than Paadham Panindhene. 10.4.6

Paninenche! Naalum Parama Paramparanai
Piniyonrum Saaraa Piravi Ketuththaalum
Manininra Sothi Mathuchoothan Ennammaan
Anininra Sempon Adalaazi Yaane. 10.4.7

Aaziyaa Nnaazi Yamararkkum Appaalaan
Ooziyaa Nnoozi Padaiththaan Niraimeyththaan
Paaziyan Tholaal Varaiyetuththaan Paathangal
Vaaziyen Nenche! Maravaathu Vaazkandaay. 10.4.8

Kanden Kamala Malarppaatham Kaandalume
Vinde Yozindha Vinaiyaa Yinavellaam
Thondechey Thenrum Thozuthu Vaziyozuka
Pande Paraman Paniththa Panivakaiye. 10.4.9

Vakaiyaal Manamonri Maathavanai Naalum
Pukaiyaal Vilakkaal Puthumalaraal Neeraal
Thikaitho Ramarargal Senriraincha Ninra
Thakaiyaan Saranam Thamargadakor Parre. 10.4.10.

Parrenru Parrip Parama Paramaparanai
Marrindol Maalai Vazuthi Valanaadan
Chorrotaiyan Thaathiyo Raayiraththu Lippaththum
Karraarkkor Parraakum Kannan Kazalinaiye. (2) 10.4.11

Kannan Kazalinai
Nannum Manamudaiyeer
Ennum Thirunaamam
Thinnam Naaraname. (2) 10.5.1

Naaranan Emmaan
Paaranangaalan
Vaaranam Tholaiththa
Kaaranan Thaane. 10.5.2

Thaane Ulagelaam
Thaane Padaiththidandhu
Thaane Undumizndhu
Thaane Aalvaane. 10.5.3

Aalvaan Aazineer
Kolvaaya Aravanaiyaan
Thaalvaay Malarittu
Naalvaay Naadeere. 10.5.4

Naadeer Naalthorum
Vaadaa Malarkondu
Paadeer Avannaamam
Veede Peralaame. 10.5.5

Meyaan Vengadam
Kaayaa Malarvannan
Peyaar Mulaiyunda
Vaayaan Maadhavane. (2) 10.5.6

Maadhavan Enrenru
Odha Valleerel
Theedhonrum Adaiyaa
Edham Saaraave. 10.5.7

Saaraa Edhangal
Neeraar Mugilvannan
Per Aar Othuvaar
Aaraar Amarare. 10.5.8

Amararkku Ariyaanai
Thamargatku Eliyaanai
Amarath Thozuvaargatku
Amaraa Vinaikale. 10.5.9

Vinaival Irulennum
Munaigal Veruvippom
Chunai Nan Malarittu
Ninaimin Nediyaane. 10.5.10.

Nediyaan Arul Soodum
Padiyaan Sadakopan
Nodi Aayiraththippaththu
Adiyaarkku Arul Pere. (2) 10.5.11

Arulperuvaar Adiyaartham Adiyanerku Aaziyaan
Arultharuvaan Amaikinraan Athunamathu Vithivakaiye
Irultharumaa Nyaalaththul Inippiravi Yaanvenden
Marulozinee Madanenche! Vaattaarraan Adivanange. (2) 10.6.1

Vaattaarraa Nnadivanangi Maanyaalap Pirapparuppaan
Kettaaye Madanenche! Kechavanem Perumaanai
Paattaaya Palapaadip Pazavinaikal Parraruththu
Naattaaro Diyalvozindhu Naarananai Nanniname. 10.6.2

Nanninam Naarananai Naamangal Palacholli
Mannulakil Valammikka Vaattaarraan Vandhinru
Vinnulakam Tharuvaanaay Viraikinraan Vithivakaiye
Enninavaa Raakaavik Karumanga Lennenche! 10.6.3

Ennenchath Thullirundhing Kirundhamiznoolivaimozindhu
Vannenchath Thiraniyanai Maarvidandha Vaattaarraan
Mannanchap Paarathaththup Paandavarkkaap Padaithottaan
Nannenche! Namperumaan Namakkarulthaan Seyvaane. 10.6.4

Vaanera Vazithandha Vaattaarraan Panivakaiye
Naanerap Perukinren Narakaththai Nakunenche
Theneru Malarththulavam Thikazpaathan Sezumparavai
Thaanerith Thirivaana Thaalinaiyen Thalaimele. 10.6.5

Thalaimela Thaalinaikal Thaamaraikkan Ennammaan
Nilaiperaan Ennenchath Theppozuthum Emperumaan
Malaimaadath Tharavanaimel Vaattaarraan Mathamikka
Kolaiyaanai Maruppochiththaan Kuraikazalthal Kurukiname. 10.6.6

Kuraikazalkal Kuruginam Nam Kovindhan Kudikondaan
Thiraikuzuvu Kadalpudaichooz Thennaattuth Thilathamanna
Varaikuzuvum Manimaada Vaattaarraan Malaradimel
Viraikuzuvum Narundhulavam Meynninru Kamazume. 10.6.7

Meynninru Kamazthulava Viraiyeru Thirumudiyan
Kainninra Sakkaraththan Karuthumidam Poruthupunal
Mainninra Varaipolum Thiruvuruva Vaattaarraarku
Ennanri Seythenaa Ennenchil Thikazavathuve? 10.6.8

Thikazginra Thirumaarbil Thirumangai Thannotum
Thikazginra Thirumaalaar Servidamthan Vaattaaru
Pukazkinra Pulloorthi Porarakkar Kulamketuththaan
Ikazvinri Ennenchath Theppozuthum Piriyaane. 10.6.9

Piriyaathaat Seyyenru Pirapparuththaal Arakkondaan
Ariyaaki Iraniyanai Aagangeen Taananru
Periyaarkkaat Pattakkaal Peraathapayan Perumaaru
Varivaalvaay Aravanaimel Vaattaarraan Kaattinane. 10.6.10.

Kaattiththan Kanaikazalkal Kadunarakam Pukaloziththa
Vaattaarrem Perumaanai Valangurukoorch Sadakopan
Paattaaya Thamizmaalai Yaayiraththul Ippaththum
Kettu Aaraar Vaanavargal Sevikkiniya Sencholle. (2) 10.6.11

Chengchor Kavikaal! Uyirkaaththaat
Seymin Thirumaa Liruncholai
Vanchak Kalvan Maamaayan
Maayak Kaviyaay Vandhu En
Nenchu Muyiru Mulkalandhu
Ninraar Ariyaa Vannam En
Nenchu Muyirum Avaitundu
Thaane Yaaki Niraindhaane. (2) 10.7.1

Thaane Yaaki Niraindhellaa
Ulakum Uyirum Thaaneyaay
Thaane Yaanen Paanaakith
Thannaith Thaane Thuthiththu Enakkuth
Thene Paale Kannale
Amuthe Thirumaaliruncholai
Kone Yaaki Ninrozindhaan
Ennai Murrum Uyirunde. 10.7.2

Ennai Murrum Uyirunden
Maaya Aakkai Yithanulpukku
Ennai Murrum Thaaneyaay
Ninra Maaya Ammaan Ser
Thennan Thirumaa Liruncholaith
Thichaikai Kooppich Therndhayaan
Innam Pove Nnekolo!
Engol Ammaan Thiruvarule? 10.7.3

Engol Ammaan Thiruvarulkal?
Ulakum Uyirum Thaaneyaay
Nangen Nnudalam Kaividaan
Nyaalath Thoote Nadandhuzakki
Thengol Thichaikkuth Thilathamaay
Ninra Thirumaaliruncholai
Nangal Kunram Kaividaan
Nannaa Achurar Naliyave. 10.7.4

Nannaa Achurar Naliveytha
Nalla Amarar Poliveytha
Ennaa Thanakal Ennumnan
Muniva Rinbam Thalaichirappa
Pannaar Paadal Ingavikal
Yaanaayth Thannaith Thaanbaadi
Thennaa Vennum Ennammaan
Thirumaaliruncolaiyaane. 10.7.5

Thirumaaliruncholaiyaane
Aakich Sezumoo Vulakum Than
Orumaa Vayirri Nnullevaiththu
Oozi Yoozi Thalaiyalikkum
Thirumaalennai Yaalumaal
Sivanum Piramanumkaanaathu
Arumaa Leythi Yadiparava
Arulai Yeendha Ammaane. 10.7.6

Arulai Eeyen Ammaane!
Ennum Mukkan Ammaanum
Therulkol Piraman Ammaanum
Thevar Konum Thevarum
Irulkal Kadiyum Munivarum
Eththum Ammaan Thirumalai
Marulkal Kadiyum Manimalai
Thirumaaliruncholaimalaiye. 10.7.7

Thirumaaliruncholaimalaiye
Thiruppaar Kadale Endhalaiye
Thirumaalvaikunthame Than
Thiruvengadame Enathudale
Arumaa Maayath Thenathuyire
Maname Vaakke Karumame
Orumaa Nodiyum Piriyaan En
Oozi Muthalvan Oruvane. (2) 10.7.8

Oozi Muthalvan Oruvane
Ennum Oruvan Ulakellaam
Oozi Thorum Thannulle
Padaiththuk Kaaththuk Ketuththuzalum
Aazi Vannan Ennammaan
Andhan Thirumaaliruncholai
Vaazi Maname Kaivilel
Udalum Uyirum Mangavotte. 10.7.9

Manga Vottun Maamaayai
Thirumaaliruncholaimeya
Nangal Kone! Yaanenee
Yaaki Yennai Yaliththaane
Pongaim Pulanum Poriyaindhum
Karumenthiriyum Aimpootham
Ingu Ivvuyirey Pirakiruthi
Maanaangaara Manangale. 10.7.10.

Maanaangaara Manamgeta
Aivar Vangai Yarmanga
Thaanaangaara Maayppukkuth
Thaane Thaane Yaanaanai
Thenaang Kaarap Pozilkurukoorch
Sadakopanchollaayiraththul
Maanaangkaaraththivaipaththum
Thirumaalirungcholaimalaikke. (2) 10.7.11

Thirumaaliruncholai Malaimenren Enna
Thirumaalvandhu En Nenchu Niraiyap Pukundhaan
Kurumaa Maniyundhu Punalponnith Thenpaal
Thirumaalchenru Chervidam Then Thiruppere. (2) 10.8.1

Pere Yuraiginra Piraan Inru Vandhu
Perenen Rennenchu Niraiyap Pukundhaan
Kaarez Kadalez Malaiye Zulagundum
Aaraava Yirraanai Yadangap Pidiththene. 10.8.2

Pidiththen Piravi Ketuththen Pinichaaren
Madiththen Manaivaazkkai Yulnirpathor Maayaiyai
Kodikko Puramaadangal Soozthirup Peraan
Adichchervadhenenakkeli Thaayina Vaare. 10.8.3

Elithaa Yinavaaren Rengankal Kalippa
Kalithaa Kiyachin Thaiyanaayk Kalikkinren
Kilithaa Viyachozaikal Soozthirup Peraan
Thelithaa Kiyachen Vichumputharu Vaane. 10.8.4

Vaane Tharuvaa Nnenakkaayen Nnototti
Ooney Kurampai Yithanul Pukundhu Inru
Thaane Thadumaarra Vinaikal Thavirththaan
Thene Pozilthen Thirupper Nakaraane. 10.8.5

Thirupper Nakaraan Thirumaaliruncholaip
Poruppe Yuraikin Rapiraaninruvandhu
Iruppen En Rennenchu Niraiyap Pukundhaan
Viruppe Perramutha Mundu Kaliththene. 10.8.6

Undu Kalithther Kumparen Kurai Melaith
Thondu Kaliththandhi Thozumchollup Perren
Vandu Kalikkum Pozilchooz Thirupperaan
Kandu Kalippak Kannulnin Rakalaane. 10.8.7

Kannulnin Rakalaan Karuththingan Periyan
Ennilnun Porule Zichaiyin Suvaithaane
Vannanan Manimaadangal Soozthirup Peraan
Thinnamen Manaththup Pukundhaan Serindhinre. 10.8.8

Inrennaip Porulaakkith Thannaiyen Nnulvaith Thaan
Anrennaip Purampokap Punarththathen Seyvaan?
Kunrennath Thikazmaadangal Soozthirup Peraan
Onrenak Karulcheyya Vunarththalur Rene. 10.8.9

Urre Nnukandhu Panichey Thunapaatham
Perren Eetheyin Nnamven Tuvathendhaay
Karraar Maraivaanar Kalvaaz Thirupperaarku
Arraar Adiyaar Thamakkallal Nillaave. (2) 10.8.10.

Nillaa Allal Neelvayalchooz Thiruppermel
Nallaar Palarvaaz Kurukoorch Sadakopan
Chollaar Thamizaa Yiraththul Ivaipaththum
Vallaar Thondaraal Vathuchoozpon Vichumpe. (2) 10.8.11

Choozvichum Panimukil Thooriyam Muzakkina
Aazkadal Alaithirai Kaiyetuth Thaadina
Ezpozi Lumvalam Endhiya Ennappan
Vaazpukaz Nnaaranan Thamaraikkakan Tukandhe. (2) 10.9.1

Naaranan Thamaraikkan Tukandhunan Nneermukil
Poorana Porkudam Pooriththa Thuyarvinnil
Neerani Kadalkalnin Raarththana Netuvaraith
Thoranam Niraiththengum Thozuthanar Ulakare. 10.9.2

Thozuthanar Ulakargal Thoopanal Malarmazai
Pozivanar Pooziyan Ralandhavan Thamarmunne
Ezumin En Rimarungichaiththanar Munivargal
Vaziyithu Vaikundhar Kenruvan Thethire. 10.9.3

Ethirethir Imaiyavar Iruppidam Vakuththanar
Kathiravar Avaravar Kainnirai Kaattinar
Athirkural Murachangal Alaikadal Muzakkoththa
Mathuviri Thuzaaymudi Maathavan Thamarkke. 10.9.4

Maathavan Thamarenru Vaachalil Vaanavar
Pothumin Emathidam Pukuthuka Enralum
Keethangal Paadinar Kinnarar Kerudargal
Vethanal Vaayavar Velviyul Maduththe. 10.9.5

Velviyul Maduththalum Viraikamaz Narumpukai
Kaalangal Valampuri Kalandhengum Ichaiththanar
Aalumingal Vaanakam Aaziyaan Thamar Enru
Vaalonkan Madandhaiyar Vaazththinar Makizndhe. 10.9.6

Madandhaiyar Vaazththalum Marutharum Vachukkalum
Thotarndhengum Thoththiram Sollinar Thotukadal
Kidandhaven Kesavan Kilaroli Manimudi
Kudandhaiyen Kovalan Kudiyadi Yaarkke. 10.9.7

Kudiyadi Yaarivar Kovindhan Dhanakkenru
Mudiyudai Vaanavar Muraimurai Ethirkolla
Kodiyani Netumathil Kopuram Kurukinar
Vadivudai Maathavan Vaikundham Pukave. 10.9.8

Naikundham Pukuthalum Vaachalil Vaanavar
Vaikundhan Thamaremar Emathidam Pukukenru
Vaikundhath Thamararum Munivarum Viyandhanar
Vakundham Pukuvathu Mannavar Vithiye. 10.9.9
